mathalu l-janati allati wuʿida l-mutaquna tajri min tahtiha l-anharu ukuluha daimun wazilluha til'ka ʿuq'ba alladhina ittaqaw waʿuq'ba l-kafirina l-naru
wa-alladhina ataynahumu l-kitaba yafrahuna bima unzila ilayka wamina l-ahzabi man yunkiru baʿdahu qul innama umir'tu an aʿbuda l-laha wala ush'rika bihi ilayhi adʿu wa-ilayhi maabi
wakadhalika anzalnahu huk'man ʿarabiyyan wala-ini ittabaʿta ahwaahum baʿdama jaaka mina l-ʿil'mi ma laka mina l-lahi min waliyyin wala waqin
walaqad arsalna rusulan min qablika wajaʿalna lahum azwajan wadhurriyyatan wama kana lirasulin an yatiya biayatin illa bi-idh'ni l-lahi likulli ajalin kitabun
yamhu l-lahu ma yashau wayuth'bitu waʿindahu ummu l-kitabi
wa-in ma nuriyannaka baʿda alladhi naʿiduhum aw natawaffayannaka fa-innama ʿalayka l-balaghu waʿalayna l-hisabu
awalam yaraw anna nati l-arda nanqusuha min atrafiha wal-lahu yahkumu la muʿaqqiba lihuk'mihi wahuwa sariʿu l-hisabi
waqad makara alladhina min qablihim falillahi l-makru jamiʿan yaʿlamu ma taksibu kullu nafsin wasayaʿlamu l-kufaru liman ʿuq'ba l-dari
wayaqulu alladhina kafaru lasta mur'salan qul kafa bil-lahi shahidan bayni wabaynakum waman ʿindahu ʿil'mu l-kitabi
alif-lam-ra kitabun anzalnahu ilayka litukh'rija l-nasa mina l-zulumati ila l-nuri bi-idh'ni rabbihim ila sirati l-ʿazizi l-hamidi
al-lahi alladhi lahu ma fi l-samawati wama fi l-ardi wawaylun lil'kafirina min ʿadhabin shadidin
alladhina yastahibbuna l-hayata l-dun'ya ʿala l-akhirati wayasudduna ʿan sabili l-lahi wayabghunaha ʿiwajan ulaika fi dalalin baʿidin
wama arsalna min rasulin illa bilisani qawmihi liyubayyina lahum fayudillu l-lahu man yashau wayahdi man yashau wahuwa l-ʿazizu l-hakimu
walaqad arsalna musa biayatina an akhrij qawmaka mina l-zulumati ila l-nuri wadhakkir'hum bi-ayyami l-lahi inna fi dhalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakurin
wa-idh qala musa liqawmihi udh'kuru niʿ'mata l-lahi ʿalaykum idh anjakum min ali fir'ʿawna yasumunakum sua l-ʿadhabi wayudhabbihuna abnaakum wayastahyuna nisaakum wafi dhalikum balaon min rabbikum ʿazimun
wa-idh ta-adhana rabbukum la-in shakartum la-azidannakum wala-in kafartum inna ʿadhabi lashadidun
waqala musa in takfuru antum waman fi l-ardi jamiʿan fa-inna l-laha laghaniyyun hamidun
alam yatikum naba-u alladhina min qablikum qawmi nuhin waʿadin wathamuda wa-alladhina min baʿdihim la yaʿlamuhum illa l-lahu jaathum rusuluhum bil-bayinati faraddu aydiyahum fi afwahihim waqalu inna kafarna bima ur'sil'tum bihi wa-inna lafi shakkin mimma tadʿunana ilayhi muribin
qalat rusuluhum afi l-lahi shakkun fatiri l-samawati wal-ardi yadʿukum liyaghfira lakum min dhunubikum wayu-akhirakum ila ajalin musamman qalu in antum illa basharun mith'luna turiduna an tasudduna ʿamma kana yaʿbudu abauna fatuna bisul'tanin mubinin
qalat lahum rusuluhum in nahnu illa basharun mith'lukum walakinna l-laha yamunnu ʿala man yashau min ʿibadihi wama kana lana an natiyakum bisul'tanin illa bi-idh'ni l-lahi waʿala l-lahi falyatawakkali l-mu'minuna
wama lana alla natawakkala ʿala l-lahi waqad hadana subulana walanasbiranna ʿala ma adhaytumuna waʿala l-lahi falyatawakkali l-mutawakiluna
waqala alladhina kafaru lirusulihim lanukh'rijannakum min ardina aw lataʿudunna fi millatina fa-awha ilayhim rabbuhum lanuh'likanna l-zalimina
walanus'kinannakumu l-arda min baʿdihim dhalika liman khafa maqami wakhafa waʿidi
wa-is'taftahu wakhaba kullu jabbarin ʿanidin
min waraihi jahannamu wayus'qa min main sadidin
yatajarraʿuhu wala yakadu yusighuhu wayatihi l-mawtu min kulli makanin wama huwa bimayyitin wamin waraihi ʿadhabun ghalizun
mathalu alladhina kafaru birabbihim aʿmaluhum karamadin ish'taddat bihi l-rihu fi yawmin ʿasifin la yaqdiruna mimma kasabu ʿala shayin dhalika huwa l-dalalu l-baʿidu
alam tara anna l-laha khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda bil-haqi in yasha yudh'hib'kum wayati bikhalqin jadidin
wama dhalika ʿala l-lahi biʿazizin
wabarazu lillahi jamiʿan faqala l-duʿafau lilladhina is'takbaru inna kunna lakum tabaʿan fahal antum mugh'nuna ʿanna min ʿadhabi l-lahi min shayin qalu law hadana l-lahu lahadaynakum sawaon ʿalayna ajaziʿ'na am sabarna ma lana min mahisin
waqala l-shaytanu lamma qudiya l-amru inna l-laha waʿadakum waʿda l-haqi wawaʿadttukum fa-akhlaftukum wama kana liya ʿalaykum min sul'tanin illa an daʿawtukum fa-is'tajabtum li fala talumuni walumu anfusakum ma ana bimus'rikhikum wama antum bimus'rikhiyya inni kafartu bima ashraktumuni min qablu inna l-zalimina lahum ʿadhabun alimun
wa-ud'khila alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati jannatin tajri min tahtiha l-anharu khalidina fiha bi-idh'ni rabbihim tahiyyatuhum fiha salamun
alam tara kayfa daraba l-lahu mathalan kalimatan tayyibatan kashajaratin tayyibatin asluha thabitun wafarʿuha fi l-samai
tu'ti ukulaha kulla hinin bi-idh'ni rabbiha wayadribu l-lahu l-amthala lilnnasi laʿallahum yatadhakkaruna
wamathalu kalimatin khabithatin kashajaratin khabithatin uj'tuthat min fawqi l-ardi ma laha min qararin
yuthabbitu l-lahu alladhina amanu bil-qawli l-thabiti fi l-hayati l-dun'ya wafi l-akhirati wayudillu l-lahu l-zalimina wayafʿalu l-lahu ma yashau
alam tara ila alladhina baddalu niʿ'mata l-lahi kuf'ran wa-ahallu qawmahum dara l-bawari
jahannama yaslawnaha wabi'sa l-qararu
wajaʿalu lillahi andadan liyudillu ʿan sabilihi qul tamattaʿu fa-inna masirakum ila l-nari
qul liʿibadiya alladhina amanu yuqimu l-salata wayunfiqu mimma razaqnahum sirran waʿalaniyatan min qabli an yatiya yawmun la bayʿun fihi wala khilalun
al-lahu alladhi khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda wa-anzala mina l-samai maan fa-akhraja bihi mina l-thamarati riz'qan lakum wasakhara lakumu l-ful'ka litajriya fi l-bahri bi-amrihi wasakhara lakumu l-anhara
wasakhara lakumu l-shamsa wal-qamara daibayni wasakhara lakumu al-layla wal-nahara
waatakum min kulli ma sa-altumuhu wa-in taʿuddu niʿ'mata l-lahi la tuh'suha inna l-insana lazalumun kaffarun
wa-idh qala ib'rahimu rabbi ij'ʿal hadha l-balada aminan wa-uj'nub'ni wabaniyya an naʿbuda l-asnama
rabbi innahunna adlalna kathiran mina l-nasi faman tabiʿani fa-innahu minni waman ʿasani fa-innaka ghafurun rahimun
rabbana inni askantu min dhurriyyati biwadin ghayri dhi zarʿin ʿinda baytika l-muharami rabbana liyuqimu l-salata fa-ij'ʿal afidatan mina l-nasi tahwi ilayhim wa-ur'zuq'hum mina l-thamarati laʿallahum yashkuruna
rabbana innaka taʿlamu ma nukh'fi wama nuʿ'linu wama yakhfa ʿala l-lahi min shayin fi l-ardi wala fi l-samai
al-hamdu lillahi alladhi wahaba li ʿala l-kibari is'maʿila wa-is'haqa inna rabbi lasamiʿu l-duʿai
rabbi ij'ʿalni muqima l-salati wamin dhurriyyati rabbana wataqabbal duʿai
rabbana igh'fir li waliwalidayya walil'mu'minina yawma yaqumu l-hisabu
wala tahsabanna l-laha ghafilan ʿamma yaʿmalu l-zalimuna innama yu-akhiruhum liyawmin tashkhasu fihi l-absaru
muh'tiʿina muq'niʿi ruusihim la yartaddu ilayhim tarfuhum wa-afidatuhum hawaon
wa-andhiri l-nasa yawma yatihimu l-ʿadhabu fayaqulu alladhina zalamu rabbana akhir'na ila ajalin qaribin nujib daʿwataka wanattabiʿi l-rusula awalam takunu aqsamtum min qablu ma lakum min zawalin
wasakantum fi masakini alladhina zalamu anfusahum watabayyana lakum kayfa faʿalna bihim wadarabna lakumu l-amthala
waqad makaru makrahum waʿinda l-lahi makruhum wa-in kana makruhum litazula min'hu l-jibalu
fala tahsabanna l-laha mukh'lifa waʿdihi rusulahu inna l-laha ʿazizun dhu intiqamin
yawma tubaddalu l-ardu ghayra l-ardi wal-samawatu wabarazu lillahi l-wahidi l-qahari
watara l-muj'rimina yawma-idhin muqarranina fi l-asfadi
sarabiluhum min qatiranin wataghsha wujuhahumu l-naru
liyajziya l-lahu kulla nafsin ma kasabat inna l-laha sariʿu l-hisabi
hadha balaghun lilnnasi waliyundharu bihi waliyaʿlamu annama huwa ilahun wahidun waliyadhakkara ulu l-albabi
alif-lam-ra til'ka ayatu l-kitabi waqur'anin mubinin
rubama yawaddu alladhina kafaru law kanu mus'limina
dharhum yakulu wayatamattaʿu wayul'hihimu l-amalu fasawfa yaʿlamuna
wama ahlakna min qaryatin illa walaha kitabun maʿlumun
ma tasbiqu min ummatin ajalaha wama yastakhiruna
waqalu yaayyuha alladhi nuzzila ʿalayhi l-dhik'ru innaka lamajnunun
law ma tatina bil-malaikati in kunta mina l-sadiqina
ma nunazzilu l-malaikata illa bil-haqi wama kanu idhan munzarina
inna nahnu nazzalna l-dhik'ra wa-inna lahu lahafizuna
walaqad arsalna min qablika fi shiyaʿi l-awalina
wama yatihim min rasulin illa kanu bihi yastahziuna
kadhalika naslukuhu fi qulubi l-muj'rimina
la yu'minuna bihi waqad khalat sunnatu l-awalina
walaw fatahna ʿalayhim baban mina l-samai fazallu fihi yaʿrujuna
laqalu innama sukkirat absaruna bal nahnu qawmun mashuruna
walaqad jaʿalna fi l-samai burujan wazayyannaha lilnnazirina
wahafiz'naha min kulli shaytanin rajimin
illa mani is'taraqa l-samʿa fa-atbaʿahu shihabun mubinun
wal-arda madadnaha wa-alqayna fiha rawasiya wa-anbatna fiha min kulli shayin mawzunin
wajaʿalna lakum fiha maʿayisha waman lastum lahu biraziqina
wa-in min shayin illa ʿindana khazainuhu wama nunazziluhu illa biqadarin maʿlumin
wa-arsalna l-riyaha lawaqiha fa-anzalna mina l-samai maan fa-asqaynakumuhu wama antum lahu bikhazinina
wa-inna lanahnu nuh'yi wanumitu wanahnu l-warithuna
walaqad ʿalim'na l-mus'taqdimina minkum walaqad ʿalim'na l-mus'takhirina
wa-inna rabbaka huwa yahshuruhum innahu hakimun ʿalimun
walaqad khalaqna l-insana min salsalin min hama-in masnunin
wal-jana khalaqnahu min qablu min nari l-samumi
wa-idh qala rabbuka lil'malaikati inni khaliqun basharan min salsalin min hama-in masnunin
fa-idha sawwaytuhu wanafakhtu fihi min ruhi faqaʿu lahu sajidina
fasajada l-malaikatu kulluhum ajmaʿuna
illa ib'lisa aba an yakuna maʿa l-sajidina
qala yaib'lisu ma laka alla takuna maʿa l-sajidina
qala lam akun li-asjuda libasharin khalaqtahu min salsalin min hama-in masnunin
qala fa-ukh'ruj min'ha fa-innaka rajimun
wa-inna ʿalayka l-laʿnata ila yawmi l-dini
qala rabbi fa-anzir'ni ila yawmi yub'ʿathuna
qala fa-innaka mina l-munzarina
ila yawmi l-waqti l-maʿlumi
qala rabbi bima aghwaytani la-uzayyinanna lahum fi l-ardi wala-ugh'wiyannahum ajmaʿina
illa ʿibadaka min'humu l-mukh'lasina
qala hadha siratun ʿalayya mus'taqimun
inna ʿibadi laysa laka ʿalayhim sul'tanun illa mani ittabaʿaka mina l-ghawina
wa-inna jahannama lamawʿiduhum ajmaʿina
laha sabʿatu abwabin likulli babin min'hum juz'on maqsumun
inna l-mutaqina fi jannatin waʿuyunin
ud'khuluha bisalamin aminina
wanazaʿna ma fi sudurihim min ghillin ikh'wanan ʿala sururin mutaqabilina
la yamassuhum fiha nasabun wama hum min'ha bimukh'rajina
nabbi ʿibadi anni ana l-ghafuru l-rahimu
wa-anna ʿadhabi huwa l-ʿadhabu l-alimu
wanabbi'hum ʿan dayfi ib'rahima
idh dakhalu ʿalayhi faqalu salaman qala inna minkum wajiluna
qalu la tawjal inna nubashiruka bighulamin ʿalimin
qala abashartumuni ʿala an massaniya l-kibaru fabima tubashiruna
qalu basharnaka bil-haqi fala takun mina l-qanitina
qala waman yaqnatu min rahmati rabbihi illa l-daluna
qala fama khatbukum ayyuha l-mur'saluna
qalu inna ur'sil'na ila qawmin muj'rimina
illa ala lutin inna lamunajjuhum ajmaʿina
illa im'ra-atahu qaddarna innaha lamina l-ghabirina
falamma jaa ala lutin l-mur'saluna
qala innakum qawmun munkaruna
qalu bal ji'naka bima kanu fihi yamtaruna
wa-ataynaka bil-haqi wa-inna lasadiquna
fa-asri bi-ahlika biqit'ʿin mina al-layli wa-ittabiʿ adbarahum wala yaltafit minkum ahadun wa-im'du haythu tu'maruna
waqadayna ilayhi dhalika l-amra anna dabira haulai maqtuʿun mus'bihina
wajaa ahlu l-madinati yastabshiruna
qala inna haulai dayfi fala tafdahuni
wa-ittaqu l-laha wala tukh'zuni
qalu awalam nanhaka ʿani l-ʿalamina
qala haulai banati in kuntum faʿilina
laʿamruka innahum lafi sakratihim yaʿmahuna
fa-akhadhathumu l-sayhatu mush'riqina
fajaʿalna ʿaliyaha safilaha wa-amtarna ʿalayhim hijaratan min sijjilin
inna fi dhalika laayatin lil'mutawassimina
wa-innaha labisabilin muqimin
inna fi dhalika laayatan lil'mu'minina
wa-in kana ashabu l-aykati lazalimina
fa-intaqamna min'hum wa-innahuma labi-imamin mubinin
walaqad kadhaba ashabu l-hij'ri l-mur'salina
waataynahum ayatina fakanu ʿanha muʿ'ridina
wakanu yanhituna mina l-jibali buyutan aminina
fa-akhadhathumu l-sayhatu mus'bihina
fama aghna ʿanhum ma kanu yaksibuna
wama khalaqna l-samawati wal-arda wama baynahuma illa bil-haqi wa-inna l-saʿata laatiyatun fa-is'fahi l-safha l-jamila
inna rabbaka huwa l-khalaqu l-ʿalimu
walaqad ataynaka sabʿan mina l-mathani wal-qur'ana l-ʿazima
la tamuddanna ʿaynayka ila ma mattaʿna bihi azwajan min'hum wala tahzan ʿalayhim wa-ikh'fid janahaka lil'mu'minina
waqul inni ana l-nadhiru l-mubinu
kama anzalna ʿala l-muq'tasimina
alladhina jaʿalu l-qur'ana ʿidina
fawarabbika lanasalannahum ajmaʿina
ʿamma kanu yaʿmaluna
fa-is'daʿ bima tu'maru wa-aʿrid ʿani l-mush'rikina
inna kafaynaka l-mus'tahziina
alladhina yajʿaluna maʿa l-lahi ilahan akhara fasawfa yaʿlamuna
walaqad naʿlamu annaka yadiqu sadruka bima yaquluna
fasabbih bihamdi rabbika wakun mina l-sajidina
wa-uʿ'bud rabbaka hatta yatiyaka l-yaqinu
ata amru l-lahi fala tastaʿjiluhu sub'hanahu wataʿala ʿamma yush'rikuna
yunazzilu l-malaikata bil-ruhi min amrihi ʿala man yashau min ʿibadihi an andhiru annahu la ilaha illa ana fa-ittaquni
khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda bil-haqi taʿala ʿamma yush'rikuna
khalaqa l-insana min nut'fatin fa-idha huwa khasimun mubinun
wal-anʿama khalaqaha lakum fiha dif'on wamanafiʿu wamin'ha takuluna
walakum fiha jamalun hina turihuna wahina tasrahuna
watahmilu athqalakum ila baladin lam takunu balighihi illa bishiqqi l-anfusi inna rabbakum laraufun rahimun
wal-khayla wal-bighala wal-hamira litarkabuha wazinatan wayakhluqu ma la taʿlamuna
waʿala l-lahi qasdu l-sabili wamin'ha jairun walaw shaa lahadakum ajmaʿina
huwa alladhi anzala mina l-samai maan lakum min'hu sharabun wamin'hu shajarun fihi tusimuna
yunbitu lakum bihi l-zarʿa wal-zaytuna wal-nakhila wal-aʿnaba wamin kulli l-thamarati inna fi dhalika laayatan liqawmin yatafakkaruna
wasakhara lakumu al-layla wal-nahara wal-shamsa wal-qamara wal-nujumu musakharatun bi-amrihi inna fi dhalika laayatin liqawmin yaʿqiluna
wama dhara-a lakum fi l-ardi mukh'talifan alwanuhu inna fi dhalika laayatan liqawmin yadhakkaruna
wahuwa alladhi sakhara l-bahra litakulu min'hu lahman tariyyan watastakhriju min'hu hil'yatan talbasunaha watara l-ful'ka mawakhira fihi walitabtaghu min fadlihi walaʿallakum tashkuruna
wa-alqa fi l-ardi rawasiya an tamida bikum wa-anharan wasubulan laʿallakum tahtaduna
waʿalamatin wabil-najmi hum yahtaduna
afaman yakhluqu kaman la yakhluqu afala tadhakkaruna
wa-in taʿuddu niʿ'mata l-lahi la tuh'suha inna l-laha laghafurun rahimun
wal-lahu yaʿlamu ma tusirruna wama tuʿ'linuna
wa-alladhina yadʿuna min duni l-lahi la yakhluquna shayan wahum yukh'laquna
amwatun ghayru ahyain wama yashʿuruna ayyana yub'ʿathuna
ilahukum ilahun wahidun fa-alladhina la yu'minuna bil-akhirati qulubuhum munkiratun wahum mus'takbiruna
la jarama anna l-laha yaʿlamu ma yusirruna wama yuʿ'linuna innahu la yuhibbu l-mus'takbirina
wa-idha qila lahum madha anzala rabbukum qalu asatiru l-awalina
liyahmilu awzarahum kamilatan yawma l-qiyamati wamin awzari alladhina yudillunahum bighayri ʿil'min ala saa ma yaziruna
qad makara alladhina min qablihim fa-ata l-lahu bun'yanahum mina l-qawaʿidi fakharra ʿalayhimu l-saqfu min fawqihim wa-atahumu l-ʿadhabu min haythu la yashʿuruna
thumma yawma l-qiyamati yukh'zihim wayaqulu ayna shurakaiya alladhina kuntum tushaqquna fihim qala alladhina utu l-ʿil'ma inna l-khiz'ya l-yawma wal-sua ʿala l-kafirina
alladhina tatawaffahumu l-malaikatu zalimi anfusihim fa-alqawu l-salama ma kunna naʿmalu min suin bala inna l-laha ʿalimun bima kuntum taʿmaluna
fa-ud'khulu abwaba jahannama khalidina fiha falabi'sa mathwa l-mutakabirina
waqila lilladhina ittaqaw madha anzala rabbukum qalu khayran lilladhina ahsanu fi hadhihi l-dun'ya hasanatun waladaru l-akhirati khayrun walaniʿ'ma daru l-mutaqina
jannatu ʿadnin yadkhulunaha tajri min tahtiha l-anharu lahum fiha ma yashauna kadhalika yajzi l-lahu l-mutaqina
alladhina tatawaffahumu l-malaikatu tayyibina yaquluna salamun ʿalaykumu ud'khulu l-janata bima kuntum taʿmaluna
hal yanzuruna illa an tatiyahumu l-malaikatu aw yatiya amru rabbika kadhalika faʿala alladhina min qablihim wama zalamahumu l-lahu walakin kanu anfusahum yazlimuna
fa-asabahum sayyiatu ma ʿamilu wahaqa bihim ma kanu bihi yastahziuna
waqala alladhina ashraku law shaa l-lahu ma ʿabadna min dunihi min shayin nahnu wala abauna wala harramna min dunihi min shayin kadhalika faʿala alladhina min qablihim fahal ʿala l-rusuli illa l-balaghu l-mubinu
walaqad baʿathna fi kulli ummatin rasulan ani uʿ'budu l-laha wa-ij'tanibu l-taghuta famin'hum man hada l-lahu wamin'hum man haqqat ʿalayhi l-dalalatu fasiru fi l-ardi fa-unzuru kayfa kana ʿaqibatu l-mukadhibina
in tahris ʿala hudahum fa-inna l-laha la yahdi man yudillu wama lahum min nasirina
wa-aqsamu bil-lahi jahda aymanihim la yabʿathu l-lahu man yamutu bala waʿdan ʿalayhi haqqan walakinna akthara l-nasi la yaʿlamuna
liyubayyina lahumu alladhi yakhtalifuna fihi waliyaʿlama alladhina kafaru annahum kanu kadhibina
innama qawluna lishayin idha aradnahu an naqula lahu kun fayakunu
wa-alladhina hajaru fi l-lahi min baʿdi ma zulimu lanubawwi-annahum fi l-dun'ya hasanatan wala-ajru l-akhirati akbaru law kanu yaʿlamuna
alladhina sabaru waʿala rabbihim yatawakkaluna
wama arsalna min qablika illa rijalan nuhi ilayhim fasalu ahla l-dhik'ri in kuntum la taʿlamuna
bil-bayinati wal-zuburi wa-anzalna ilayka l-dhik'ra litubayyina lilnnasi ma nuzzila ilayhim walaʿallahum yatafakkaruna
afa-amina alladhina makaru l-sayiati an yakhsifa l-lahu bihimu l-arda aw yatiyahumu l-ʿadhabu min haythu la yashʿuruna
aw yakhudhahum fi taqallubihim fama hum bimuʿ'jizina
aw yakhudhahum ʿala takhawwufin fa-inna rabbakum laraufun rahimun
awalam yaraw ila ma khalaqa l-lahu min shayin yatafayya-u zilaluhu ʿani l-yamini wal-shamaili sujjadan lillahi wahum dakhiruna
walillahi yasjudu ma fi l-samawati wama fi l-ardi min dabbatin wal-malaikatu wahum la yastakbiruna
yakhafuna rabbahum min fawqihim wayafʿaluna ma yu'maruna
waqala l-lahu la tattakhidhu ilahayni ith'nayni innama huwa ilahun wahidun fa-iyyaya fa-ir'habuni
walahu ma fi l-samawati wal-ardi walahu l-dinu wasiban afaghayra l-lahi tattaquna
wama bikum min niʿ'matin famina l-lahi thumma idha massakumu l-duru fa-ilayhi tajaruna
thumma idha kashafa l-dura ʿankum idha fariqun minkum birabbihim yush'rikuna
liyakfuru bima ataynahum fatamattaʿu fasawfa taʿlamuna
wayajʿaluna lima la yaʿlamuna nasiban mimma razaqnahum tal-lahi latus'alunna ʿamma kuntum taftaruna
wayajʿaluna lillahi l-banati sub'hanahu walahum ma yashtahuna
wa-idha bushira ahaduhum bil-untha zalla wajhuhu mus'waddan wahuwa kazimun
yatawara mina l-qawmi min sui ma bushira bihi ayum'sikuhu ʿala hunin am yadussuhu fi l-turabi ala saa ma yahkumuna
lilladhina la yu'minuna bil-akhirati mathalu l-sawi walillahi l-mathalu l-aʿla wahuwa l-ʿazizu l-hakimu
walaw yuakhidhu l-lahu l-nasa bizul'mihim ma taraka ʿalayha min dabbatin walakin yu-akhiruhum ila ajalin musamman fa-idha jaa ajaluhum la yastakhiruna saʿatan wala yastaqdimuna
wayajʿaluna lillahi ma yakrahuna watasifu alsinatuhumu l-kadhiba anna lahumu l-hus'na la jarama anna lahumu l-nara wa-annahum muf'ratuna
tal-lahi laqad arsalna ila umamin min qablika fazayyana lahumu l-shaytanu aʿmalahum fahuwa waliyyuhumu l-yawma walahum ʿadhabun alimun
wama anzalna ʿalayka l-kitaba illa litubayyina lahumu alladhi ikh'talafu fihi wahudan warahmatan liqawmin yu'minuna
wal-lahu anzala mina l-samai maan fa-ahya bihi l-arda baʿda mawtiha inna fi dhalika laayatan liqawmin yasmaʿuna
wa-inna lakum fi l-anʿami laʿib'ratan nus'qikum mimma fi butunihi min bayni farthin wadamin labanan khalisan saighan lilsharibina
wamin thamarati l-nakhili wal-aʿnabi tattakhidhuna min'hu sakaran wariz'qan hasanan inna fi dhalika laayatan liqawmin yaʿqiluna
wa-awha rabbuka ila l-nahli ani ittakhidhi mina l-jibali buyutan wamina l-shajari wamimma yaʿrishuna
thumma kuli min kulli l-thamarati fa-us'luki subula rabbiki dhululan yakhruju min butuniha sharabun mukh'talifun alwanuhu fihi shifaon lilnnasi inna fi dhalika laayatan liqawmin yatafakkaruna
wal-lahu khalaqakum thumma yatawaffakum waminkum man yuraddu ila ardhali l-ʿumuri likay la yaʿlama baʿda ʿil'min shayan inna l-laha ʿalimun qadirun
wal-lahu faddala baʿdakum ʿala baʿdin fi l-riz'qi fama alladhina fuddilu biraddi riz'qihim ʿala ma malakat aymanuhum fahum fihi sawaon afabiniʿ'mati l-lahi yajhaduna
wal-lahu jaʿala lakum min anfusikum azwajan wajaʿala lakum min azwajikum banina wahafadatan warazaqakum mina l-tayibati afabil-batili yu'minuna wabiniʿ'mati l-lahi hum yakfuruna
wayaʿbuduna min duni l-lahi ma la yamliku lahum riz'qan mina l-samawati wal-ardi shayan wala yastatiʿuna
fala tadribu lillahi l-amthala inna l-laha yaʿlamu wa-antum la taʿlamuna
daraba l-lahu mathalan ʿabdan mamlukan la yaqdiru ʿala shayin waman razaqnahu minna riz'qan hasanan fahuwa yunfiqu min'hu sirran wajahran hal yastawuna l-hamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la yaʿlamuna
wadaraba l-lahu mathalan rajulayni ahaduhuma abkamu la yaqdiru ʿala shayin wahuwa kallun ʿala mawlahu aynama yuwajjihhu la yati bikhayrin hal yastawi huwa waman yamuru bil-ʿadli wahuwa ʿala siratin mus'taqimin
walillahi ghaybu l-samawati wal-ardi wama amru l-saʿati illa kalamhi l-basari aw huwa aqrabu inna l-laha ʿala kulli shayin qadirun
wal-lahu akhrajakum min butuni ummahatikum la taʿlamuna shayan wajaʿala lakumu l-samʿa wal-absara wal-afidata laʿallakum tashkuruna
alam yaraw ila l-tayri musakharatin fi jawwi l-samai ma yum'sikuhunna illa l-lahu inna fi dhalika laayatin liqawmin yu'minuna
wal-lahu jaʿala lakum min buyutikum sakanan wajaʿala lakum min juludi l-anʿami buyutan tastakhiffunaha yawma zaʿnikum wayawma iqamatikum wamin aswafiha wa-awbariha wa-ashʿariha athathan wamataʿan ila hinin
wal-lahu jaʿala lakum mimma khalaqa zilalan wajaʿala lakum mina l-jibali aknanan wajaʿala lakum sarabila taqikumu l-hara wasarabila taqikum basakum kadhalika yutimmu niʿ'matahu ʿalaykum laʿallakum tus'limuna
fa-in tawallaw fa-innama ʿalayka l-balaghu l-mubinu
yaʿrifuna niʿ'mata l-lahi thumma yunkirunaha wa-aktharuhumu l-kafiruna
wayawma nabʿathu min kulli ummatin shahidan thumma la yu'dhanu lilladhina kafaru wala hum yus'taʿtabuna
wa-idha raa alladhina zalamu l-ʿadhaba fala yukhaffafu ʿanhum wala hum yunzaruna
wa-idha raa alladhina ashraku shurakaahum qalu rabbana haulai shurakauna alladhina kunna nadʿu min dunika fa-alqaw ilayhimu l-qawla innakum lakadhibuna
wa-alqaw ila l-lahi yawma-idhin l-salama wadalla ʿanhum ma kanu yaftaruna
alladhina kafaru wasaddu ʿan sabili l-lahi zid'nahum ʿadhaban fawqa l-ʿadhabi bima kanu yuf'siduna
wayawma nabʿathu fi kulli ummatin shahidan ʿalayhim min anfusihim waji'na bika shahidan ʿala haulai wanazzalna ʿalayka l-kitaba tib'yanan likulli shayin wahudan warahmatan wabush'ra lil'mus'limina
inna l-laha yamuru bil-ʿadli wal-ih'sani waitai dhi l-qur'ba wayanha ʿani l-fahshai wal-munkari wal-baghyi yaʿizukum laʿallakum tadhakkaruna
wa-awfu biʿahdi l-lahi idha ʿahadttum wala tanqudu l-aymana baʿda tawkidiha waqad jaʿaltumu l-laha ʿalaykum kafilan inna l-laha yaʿlamu ma tafʿaluna
wala takunu ka-allati naqadat ghazlaha min baʿdi quwwatin ankathan tattakhidhuna aymanakum dakhalan baynakum an takuna ummatun hiya arba min ummatin innama yablukumu l-lahu bihi walayubayyinanna lakum yawma l-qiyamati ma kuntum fihi takhtalifuna
walaw shaa l-lahu lajaʿalakum ummatan wahidatan walakin yudillu man yashau wayahdi man yashau walatus'alunna ʿamma kuntum taʿmaluna
wala tattakhidhu aymanakum dakhalan baynakum fatazilla qadamun baʿda thubutiha watadhuqu l-sua bima sadadttum ʿan sabili l-lahi walakum ʿadhabun ʿazimun
wala tashtaru biʿahdi l-lahi thamanan qalilan innama ʿinda l-lahi huwa khayrun lakum in kuntum taʿlamuna
ma ʿindakum yanfadu wama ʿinda l-lahi baqin walanajziyanna alladhina sabaru ajrahum bi-ahsani ma kanu yaʿmaluna
man ʿamila salihan min dhakarin aw untha wahuwa mu'minun falanuh'yiyannahu hayatan tayyibatan walanajziyannahum ajrahum bi-ahsani ma kanu yaʿmaluna
fa-idha qarata l-qur'ana fa-is'taʿidh bil-lahi mina l-shaytani l-rajimi
innahu laysa lahu sul'tanun ʿala alladhina amanu waʿala rabbihim yatawakkaluna
innama sul'tanuhu ʿala alladhina yatawallawnahu wa-alladhina hum bihi mush'rikuna
wa-idha baddalna ayatan makana ayatin wal-lahu aʿlamu bima yunazzilu qalu innama anta muf'tarin bal aktharuhum la yaʿlamuna
qul nazzalahu ruhu l-qudusi min rabbika bil-haqi liyuthabbita alladhina amanu wahudan wabush'ra lil'mus'limina
walaqad naʿlamu annahum yaquluna innama yuʿallimuhu basharun lisanu alladhi yul'hiduna ilayhi aʿjamiyyun wahadha lisanun ʿarabiyyun mubinun
inna alladhina la yu'minuna biayati l-lahi la yahdihimu l-lahu walahum ʿadhabun alimun
innama yaftari l-kadhiba alladhina la yu'minuna biayati l-lahi wa-ulaika humu l-kadhibuna
man kafara bil-lahi min baʿdi imanihi illa man uk'riha waqalbuhu mut'ma-innun bil-imani walakin man sharaha bil-kuf'ri sadran faʿalayhim ghadabun mina l-lahi walahum ʿadhabun ʿazimun
dhalika bi-annahumu is'tahabbu l-hayata l-dun'ya ʿala l-akhirati wa-anna l-laha la yahdi l-qawma l-kafirina
ulaika alladhina tabaʿa l-lahu ʿala qulubihim wasamʿihim wa-absarihim wa-ulaika humu l-ghafiluna
la jarama annahum fi l-akhirati humu l-khasiruna
thumma inna rabbaka lilladhina hajaru min baʿdi ma futinu thumma jahadu wasabaru inna rabbaka min baʿdiha laghafurun rahimun
yawma tati kullu nafsin tujadilu ʿan nafsiha watuwaffa kullu nafsin ma ʿamilat wahum la yuz'lamuna
wadaraba l-lahu mathalan qaryatan kanat aminatan mut'ma-innatan yatiha riz'quha raghadan min kulli makanin fakafarat bi-anʿumi l-lahi fa-adhaqaha l-lahu libasa l-juʿi wal-khawfi bima kanu yasnaʿuna
walaqad jaahum rasulun min'hum fakadhabuhu fa-akhadhahumu l-ʿadhabu wahum zalimuna
fakulu mimma razaqakumu l-lahu halalan tayyiban wa-ush'kuru niʿ'mata l-lahi in kuntum iyyahu taʿbuduna
innama harrama ʿalaykumu l-maytata wal-dama walahma l-khinziri wama uhilla lighayri l-lahi bihi famani ud'turra ghayra baghin wala ʿadin fa-inna l-laha ghafurun rahimun
wala taqulu lima tasifu alsinatukumu l-kadhiba hadha halalun wahadha haramun litaftaru ʿala l-lahi l-kadhiba inna alladhina yaftaruna ʿala l-lahi l-kadhiba la yuf'lihuna
mataʿun qalilun walahum ʿadhabun alimun
waʿala alladhina hadu harramna ma qasasna ʿalayka min qablu wama zalamnahum walakin kanu anfusahum yazlimuna
thumma inna rabbaka lilladhina ʿamilu l-sua bijahalatin thumma tabu min baʿdi dhalika wa-aslahu inna rabbaka min baʿdiha laghafurun rahimun
inna ib'rahima kana ummatan qanitan lillahi hanifan walam yaku mina l-mush'rikina
shakiran li-anʿumihi ij'tabahu wahadahu ila siratin mus'taqimin
waataynahu fi l-dun'ya hasanatan wa-innahu fi l-akhirati lamina l-salihina
thumma awhayna ilayka ani ittabiʿ millata ib'rahima hanifan wama kana mina l-mush'rikina
innama juʿila l-sabtu ʿala alladhina ikh'talafu fihi wa-inna rabbaka layahkumu baynahum yawma l-qiyamati fima kanu fihi yakhtalifuna
ud'ʿu ila sabili rabbika bil-hik'mati wal-mawʿizati l-hasanati wajadil'hum bi-allati hiya ahsanu inna rabbaka huwa aʿlamu biman dalla ʿan sabilihi wahuwa aʿlamu bil-muh'tadina
wa-in ʿaqabtum faʿaqibu bimith'li ma ʿuqib'tum bihi wala-in sabartum lahuwa khayrun lilssabirina
wa-is'bir wama sabruka illa bil-lahi wala tahzan ʿalayhim wala taku fi dayqin mimma yamkuruna
inna l-laha maʿa alladhina ittaqaw wa-alladhina hum muh'sinuna
sub'hana alladhi asra biʿabdihi laylan mina l-masjidi l-harami ila l-masjidi l-aqsa alladhi barakna hawlahu linuriyahu min ayatina innahu huwa l-samiʿu l-basiru
waatayna musa l-kitaba wajaʿalnahu hudan libani is'raila alla tattakhidhu min duni wakilan
dhurriyyata man hamalna maʿa nuhin innahu kana ʿabdan shakuran
waqadayna ila bani is'raila fi l-kitabi latuf'sidunna fi l-ardi marratayni walataʿlunna ʿuluwwan kabiran
fa-idha jaa waʿdu ulahuma baʿathna ʿalaykum ʿibadan lana uli basin shadidin fajasu khilala l-diyari wakana waʿdan mafʿulan
thumma radadna lakumu l-karata ʿalayhim wa-amdadnakum bi-amwalin wabanina wajaʿalnakum akthara nafiran
in ahsantum ahsantum li-anfusikum wa-in asatum falaha fa-idha jaa waʿdu l-akhirati liyasuu wujuhakum waliyadkhulu l-masjida kama dakhaluhu awwala marratin waliyutabbiru ma ʿalaw tatbiran
ʿasa rabbukum an yarhamakum wa-in ʿudttum ʿud'na wajaʿalna jahannama lil'kafirina hasiran
inna hadha l-qur'ana yahdi lillati hiya aqwamu wayubashiru l-mu'minina alladhina yaʿmaluna l-salihati anna lahum ajran kabiran
wa-anna alladhina la yu'minuna bil-akhirati aʿtadna lahum ʿadhaban aliman
wayadʿu l-insanu bil-shari duʿaahu bil-khayri wakana l-insanu ʿajulan
wajaʿalna al-layla wal-nahara ayatayni famahawna ayata al-layli wajaʿalna ayata l-nahari mub'siratan litabtaghu fadlan min rabbikum walitaʿlamu ʿadada l-sinina wal-hisaba wakulla shayin fassalnahu tafsilan
wakulla insanin alzamnahu tairahu fi ʿunuqihi wanukh'riju lahu yawma l-qiyamati kitaban yalqahu manshuran
iq'ra kitabaka kafa binafsika l-yawma ʿalayka hasiban
mani ih'tada fa-innama yahtadi linafsihi waman dalla fa-innama yadillu ʿalayha wala taziru waziratun wiz'ra ukh'ra wama kunna muʿadhibina hatta nabʿatha rasulan
wa-idha aradna an nuh'lika qaryatan amarna mut'rafiha fafasaqu fiha fahaqqa ʿalayha l-qawlu fadammarnaha tadmiran
wakam ahlakna mina l-quruni min baʿdi nuhin wakafa birabbika bidhunubi ʿibadihi khabiran basiran
man kana yuridu l-ʿajilata ʿajjalna lahu fiha ma nashau liman nuridu thumma jaʿalna lahu jahannama yaslaha madhmuman madhuran
waman arada l-akhirata wasaʿa laha saʿyaha wahuwa mu'minun fa-ulaika kana saʿyuhum mashkuran
kullan numiddu haulai wahaulai min ʿatai rabbika wama kana ʿatau rabbika mahzuran
unzur kayfa faddalna baʿdahum ʿala baʿdin walalakhiratu akbaru darajatin wa-akbaru tafdilan
la tajʿal maʿa l-lahi ilahan akhara fataqʿuda madhmuman makhdhulan
waqada rabbuka alla taʿbudu illa iyyahu wabil-walidayni ih'sanan imma yablughanna ʿindaka l-kibara ahaduhuma aw kilahuma fala taqul lahuma uffin wala tanharhuma waqul lahuma qawlan kariman
wa-ikh'fid lahuma janaha l-dhuli mina l-rahmati waqul rabbi ir'hamhuma kama rabbayani saghiran
rabbukum aʿlamu bima fi nufusikum in takunu salihina fa-innahu kana lil'awwabina ghafuran
waati dha l-qur'ba haqqahu wal-mis'kina wa-ib'na l-sabili wala tubadhir tabdhiran
inna l-mubadhirina kanu ikh'wana l-shayatini wakana l-shaytanu lirabbihi kafuran
wa-imma tuʿ'ridanna ʿanhumu ib'tighaa rahmatin min rabbika tarjuha faqul lahum qawlan maysuran
wala tajʿal yadaka maghlulatan ila ʿunuqika wala tabsut'ha kulla l-basti fataqʿuda maluman mahsuran
inna rabbaka yabsutu l-riz'qa liman yashau wayaqdiru innahu kana biʿibadihi khabiran basiran
wala taqtulu awladakum khashyata im'laqin nahnu narzuquhum wa-iyyakum inna qatlahum kana khit'an kabiran
wala taqrabu l-zina innahu kana fahishatan wasaa sabilan
wala taqtulu l-nafsa allati harrama l-lahu illa bil-haqi waman qutila mazluman faqad jaʿalna liwaliyyihi sul'tanan fala yus'rif fi l-qatli innahu kana mansuran
wala taqrabu mala l-yatimi illa bi-allati hiya ahsanu hatta yablugha ashuddahu wa-awfu bil-ʿahdi inna l-ʿahda kana masulan
wa-awfu l-kayla idha kil'tum wazinu bil-qis'tasi l-mus'taqimi dhalika khayrun wa-ahsanu tawilan
wala taqfu ma laysa laka bihi ʿil'mun inna l-samʿa wal-basara wal-fuada kullu ulaika kana ʿanhu masulan
wala tamshi fi l-ardi marahan innaka lan takhriqa l-arda walan tablugha l-jibala tulan
kullu dhalika kana sayyi-uhu ʿinda rabbika makruhan
dhalika mimma awha ilayka rabbuka mina l-hik'mati wala tajʿal maʿa l-lahi ilahan akhara fatul'qa fi jahannama maluman madhuran
afa-asfakum rabbukum bil-banina wa-ittakhadha mina l-malaikati inathan innakum lataquluna qawlan ʿaziman
walaqad sarrafna fi hadha l-qur'ani liyadhakkaru wama yaziduhum illa nufuran
qul law kana maʿahu alihatun kama yaquluna idhan la-ib'taghaw ila dhi l-ʿarshi sabilan
sub'hanahu wataʿala ʿamma yaquluna ʿuluwwan kabiran
tusabbihu lahu l-samawatu l-sabʿu wal-ardu waman fihinna wa-in min shayin illa yusabbihu bihamdihi walakin la tafqahuna tasbihahum innahu kana haliman ghafuran
wa-idha qarata l-qur'ana jaʿalna baynaka wabayna alladhina la yu'minuna bil-akhirati hijaban masturan
wajaʿalna ʿala qulubihim akinnatan an yafqahuhu wafi adhanihim waqran wa-idha dhakarta rabbaka fi l-qur'ani wahdahu wallaw ʿala adbarihim nufuran
nahnu aʿlamu bima yastamiʿuna bihi idh yastamiʿuna ilayka wa-idh hum najwa idh yaqulu l-zalimuna in tattabiʿuna illa rajulan mashuran
unzur kayfa darabu laka l-amthala fadallu fala yastatiʿuna sabilan
waqalu a-idha kunna ʿizaman warufatan a-inna lamabʿuthuna khalqan jadidan
qul kunu hijaratan aw hadidan
aw khalqan mimma yakburu fi sudurikum fasayaquluna man yuʿiduna quli alladhi fatarakum awwala marratin fasayun'ghiduna ilayka ruusahum wayaquluna mata huwa qul ʿasa an yakuna qariban
yawma yadʿukum fatastajibuna bihamdihi watazunnuna in labith'tum illa qalilan
waqul liʿibadi yaqulu allati hiya ahsanu inna l-shaytana yanzaghu baynahum inna l-shaytana kana lil'insani ʿaduwwan mubinan
rabbukum aʿlamu bikum in yasha yarhamkum aw in yasha yuʿadhib'kum wama arsalnaka ʿalayhim wakilan
warabbuka aʿlamu biman fi l-samawati wal-ardi walaqad faddalna baʿda l-nabiyina ʿala baʿdin waatayna dawuda zaburan
quli id'ʿu alladhina zaʿamtum min dunihi fala yamlikuna kashfa l-duri ʿankum wala tahwilan
ulaika alladhina yadʿuna yabtaghuna ila rabbihimu l-wasilata ayyuhum aqrabu wayarjuna rahmatahu wayakhafuna ʿadhabahu inna ʿadhaba rabbika kana mahdhuran
wa-in min qaryatin illa nahnu muh'likuha qabla yawmi l-qiyamati aw muʿadhibuha ʿadhaban shadidan kana dhalika fi l-kitabi masturan
wama manaʿana an nur'sila bil-ayati illa an kadhaba biha l-awaluna waatayna thamuda l-naqata mub'siratan fazalamu biha wama nur'silu bil-ayati illa takhwifan
wa-idh qul'na laka inna rabbaka ahata bil-nasi wama jaʿalna l-ru'ya allati araynaka illa fit'natan lilnnasi wal-shajarata l-malʿunata fi l-qur'ani wanukhawwifuhum fama yaziduhum illa tugh'yanan kabiran
wa-idh qul'na lil'malaikati us'judu liadama fasajadu illa ib'lisa qala a-asjudu liman khalaqta tinan
qala ara-aytaka hadha alladhi karramta ʿalayya la-in akhartani ila yawmi l-qiyamati la-ahtanikanna dhurriyyatahu illa qalilan
qala idh'hab faman tabiʿaka min'hum fa-inna jahannama jazaukum jazaan mawfuran
wa-is'tafziz mani is'tataʿta min'hum bisawtika wa-ajlib ʿalayhim bikhaylika warajilika washarik'hum fi l-amwali wal-awladi waʿid'hum wama yaʿiduhumu l-shaytanu illa ghururan
inna ʿibadi laysa laka ʿalayhim sul'tanun wakafa birabbika wakilan
rabbukumu alladhi yuz'ji lakumu l-ful'ka fi l-bahri litabtaghu min fadlihi innahu kana bikum rahiman
wa-idha massakumu l-duru fi l-bahri dalla man tadʿuna illa iyyahu falamma najjakum ila l-bari aʿradtum wakana l-insanu kafuran
afa-amintum an yakhsifa bikum janiba l-bari aw yur'sila ʿalaykum hasiban thumma la tajidu lakum wakilan
am amintum an yuʿidakum fihi taratan ukh'ra fayur'sila ʿalaykum qasifan mina l-rihi fayugh'riqakum bima kafartum thumma la tajidu lakum ʿalayna bihi tabiʿan
walaqad karramna bani adama wahamalnahum fi l-bari wal-bahri warazaqnahum mina l-tayibati wafaddalnahum ʿala kathirin mimman khalaqna tafdilan
yawma nadʿu kulla unasin bi-imamihim faman utiya kitabahu biyaminihi fa-ulaika yaqrauna kitabahum wala yuz'lamuna fatilan
waman kana fi hadhihi aʿma fahuwa fi l-akhirati aʿma wa-adallu sabilan
wa-in kadu layaftinunaka ʿani alladhi awhayna ilayka litaftariya ʿalayna ghayrahu wa-idhan la-ittakhadhuka khalilan
walawla an thabbatnaka laqad kidtta tarkanu ilayhim shayan qalilan
idhan la-adhaqnaka diʿ'fa l-hayati wadiʿ'fa l-mamati thumma la tajidu laka ʿalayna nasiran
wa-in kadu layastafizzunaka mina l-ardi liyukh'rijuka min'ha wa-idhan la yalbathuna khilafaka illa qalilan
sunnata man qad arsalna qablaka min rusulina wala tajidu lisunnatina tahwilan
aqimi l-salata liduluki l-shamsi ila ghasaqi al-layli waqur'ana l-fajri inna qur'ana l-fajri kana mashhudan
wamina al-layli fatahajjad bihi nafilatan laka ʿasa an yabʿathaka rabbuka maqaman mahmudan
waqul rabbi adkhil'ni mud'khala sid'qin wa-akhrij'ni mukh'raja sid'qin wa-ij'ʿal li min ladunka sul'tanan nasiran
waqul jaa l-haqu wazahaqa l-batilu inna l-batila kana zahuqan
wanunazzilu mina l-qur'ani ma huwa shifaon warahmatun lil'mu'minina wala yazidu l-zalimina illa khasaran
wa-idha anʿamna ʿala l-insani aʿrada wanaa bijanibihi wa-idha massahu l-sharu kana yausan
qul kullun yaʿmalu ʿala shakilatihi farabbukum aʿlamu biman huwa ahda sabilan
wayasalunaka ʿani l-ruhi quli l-ruhu min amri rabbi wama utitum mina l-ʿil'mi illa qalilan
wala-in shi'na lanadhhabanna bi-alladhi awhayna ilayka thumma la tajidu laka bihi ʿalayna wakilan
illa rahmatan min rabbika inna fadlahu kana ʿalayka kabiran
qul la-ini ij'tamaʿati l-insu wal-jinu ʿala an yatu bimith'li hadha l-qur'ani la yatuna bimith'lihi walaw kana baʿduhum libaʿdin zahiran
walaqad sarrafna lilnnasi fi hadha l-qur'ani min kulli mathalin fa-aba aktharu l-nasi illa kufuran
waqalu lan nu'mina laka hatta tafjura lana mina l-ardi yanbuʿan
aw takuna laka jannatun min nakhilin waʿinabin fatufajjira l-anhara khilalaha tafjiran
aw tus'qita l-samaa kama zaʿamta ʿalayna kisafan aw tatiya bil-lahi wal-malaikati qabilan
aw yakuna laka baytun min zukh'rufin aw tarqa fi l-samai walan nu'mina liruqiyyika hatta tunazzila ʿalayna kitaban naqra-uhu qul sub'hana rabbi hal kuntu illa basharan rasulan
wama manaʿa l-nasa an yu'minu idh jaahumu l-huda illa an qalu abaʿatha l-lahu basharan rasulan
qul law kana fi l-ardi malaikatun yamshuna mut'ma-innina lanazzalna ʿalayhim mina l-samai malakan rasulan
qul kafa bil-lahi shahidan bayni wabaynakum innahu kana biʿibadihi khabiran basiran
waman yahdi l-lahu fahuwa l-muh'tadi waman yud'lil falan tajida lahum awliyaa min dunihi wanahshuruhum yawma l-qiyamati ʿala wujuhihim ʿum'yan wabuk'man wasumman mawahum jahannamu kullama khabat zid'nahum saʿiran
dhalika jazauhum bi-annahum kafaru biayatina waqalu a-idha kunna ʿizaman warufatan a-inna lamabʿuthuna khalqan jadidan
awalam yaraw anna l-laha alladhi khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda qadirun ʿala an yakhluqa mith'lahum wajaʿala lahum ajalan la rayba fihi fa-aba l-zalimuna illa kufuran
qul law antum tamlikuna khazaina rahmati rabbi idhan la-amsaktum khashyata l-infaqi wakana l-insanu qaturan
walaqad atayna musa tis'ʿa ayatin bayyinatin fasal bani is'raila idh jaahum faqala lahu fir'ʿawnu inni la-azunnuka yamusa mashuran
qala laqad ʿalim'ta ma anzala haulai illa rabbu l-samawati wal-ardi basaira wa-inni la-azunnuka yafir'ʿawnu mathburan
fa-arada an yastafizzahum mina l-ardi fa-aghraqnahu waman maʿahu jamiʿan
waqul'na min baʿdihi libani is'raila us'kunu l-arda fa-idha jaa waʿdu l-akhirati ji'na bikum lafifan
wabil-haqi anzalnahu wabil-haqi nazala wama arsalnaka illa mubashiran wanadhiran
waqur'anan faraqnahu litaqra-ahu ʿala l-nasi ʿala muk'thin wanazzalnahu tanzilan
qul aminu bihi aw la tu'minu inna alladhina utu l-ʿil'ma min qablihi idha yut'la ʿalayhim yakhirruna lil'adhqani sujjadan
wayaquluna sub'hana rabbina in kana waʿdu rabbina lamafʿulan
wayakhirruna lil'adhqani yabkuna wayaziduhum khushuʿan
quli id'ʿu l-laha awi id'ʿu l-rahmana ayyan ma tadʿu falahu l-asmau l-hus'na wala tajhar bisalatika wala tukhafit biha wa-ib'taghi bayna dhalika sabilan
waquli l-hamdu lillahi alladhi lam yattakhidh waladan walam yakun lahu sharikun fi l-mul'ki walam yakun lahu waliyyun mina l-dhuli wakabbir'hu takbiran
al-hamdu lillahi alladhi anzala ʿala ʿabdihi l-kitaba walam yajʿal lahu ʿiwaja
qayyiman liyundhira basan shadidan min ladun'hu wayubashira l-mu'minina alladhina yaʿmaluna l-salihati anna lahum ajran hasanan
makithina fihi abadan
wayundhira alladhina qalu ittakhadha l-lahu waladan
ma lahum bihi min ʿil'min wala liabaihim kaburat kalimatan takhruju min afwahihim in yaquluna illa kadhiban
falaʿallaka bakhiʿun nafsaka ʿala atharihim in lam yu'minu bihadha l-hadithi asafan
inna jaʿalna ma ʿala l-ardi zinatan laha linabluwahum ayyuhum ahsanu ʿamalan
wa-inna lajaʿiluna ma ʿalayha saʿidan juruzan
am hasib'ta anna ashaba l-kahfi wal-raqimi kanu min ayatina ʿajaban
idh awa l-fit'yatu ila l-kahfi faqalu rabbana atina min ladunka rahmatan wahayyi lana min amrina rashadan
fadarabna ʿala adhanihim fi l-kahfi sinina ʿadadan
thumma baʿathnahum linaʿlama ayyu l-hiz'bayni ahsa lima labithu amadan
nahnu naqussu ʿalayka naba-ahum bil-haqi innahum fit'yatun amanu birabbihim wazid'nahum hudan
warabatna ʿala qulubihim idh qamu faqalu rabbuna rabbu l-samawati wal-ardi lan nadʿuwa min dunihi ilahan laqad qul'na idhan shatatan
haulai qawmuna ittakhadhu min dunihi alihatan lawla yatuna ʿalayhim bisul'tanin bayyinin faman azlamu mimmani if'tara ʿala l-lahi kadhiban
wa-idhi iʿ'tazaltumuhum wama yaʿbuduna illa l-laha fawu ila l-kahfi yanshur lakum rabbukum min rahmatihi wayuhayyi lakum min amrikum mir'faqan
watara l-shamsa idha talaʿat tazawaru ʿan kahfihim dhata l-yamini wa-idha gharabat taqriduhum dhata l-shimali wahum fi fajwatin min'hu dhalika min ayati l-lahi man yahdi l-lahu fahuwa l-muh'tadi waman yud'lil falan tajida lahu waliyyan mur'shidan
watahsabuhum ayqazan wahum ruqudun wanuqallibuhum dhata l-yamini wadhata l-shimali wakalbuhum basitun dhiraʿayhi bil-wasidi lawi ittalaʿta ʿalayhim lawallayta min'hum firaran walamuli'ta min'hum ruʿ'ban
wakadhalika baʿathnahum liyatasaalu baynahum qala qailun min'hum kam labith'tum qalu labith'na yawman aw baʿda yawmin qalu rabbukum aʿlamu bima labith'tum fa-ib'ʿathu ahadakum biwariqikum hadhihi ila l-madinati falyanzur ayyuha azka taʿaman falyatikum biriz'qin min'hu walyatalattaf wala yush'ʿiranna bikum ahadan
innahum in yazharu ʿalaykum yarjumukum aw yuʿidukum fi millatihim walan tuf'lihu idhan abadan
wakadhalika aʿtharna ʿalayhim liyaʿlamu anna waʿda l-lahi haqqun wa-anna l-saʿata la rayba fiha idh yatanazaʿuna baynahum amrahum faqalu ib'nu ʿalayhim bun'yanan rabbuhum aʿlamu bihim qala alladhina ghalabu ʿala amrihim lanattakhidhanna ʿalayhim masjidan
sayaquluna thalathatun rabiʿuhum kalbuhum wayaquluna khamsatun sadisuhum kalbuhum rajman bil-ghaybi wayaquluna sabʿatun wathaminuhum kalbuhum qul rabbi aʿlamu biʿiddatihim ma yaʿlamuhum illa qalilun fala tumari fihim illa miraan zahiran wala tastafti fihim min'hum ahadan
wala taqulanna lishay'in inni faʿilun dhalika ghadan
illa an yashaa l-lahu wa-udh'kur rabbaka idha nasita waqul ʿasa an yahdiyani rabbi li-aqraba min hadha rashadan
walabithu fi kahfihim thalatha mi-atin sinina wa-iz'dadu tis'ʿan
quli l-lahu aʿlamu bima labithu lahu ghaybu l-samawati wal-ardi absir bihi wa-asmiʿ ma lahum min dunihi min waliyyin wala yush'riku fi huk'mihi ahadan
wa-ut'lu ma uhiya ilayka min kitabi rabbika la mubaddila likalimatihi walan tajida min dunihi mul'tahadan
wa-is'bir nafsaka maʿa alladhina yadʿuna rabbahum bil-ghadati wal-ʿashiyi yuriduna wajhahu wala taʿdu ʿaynaka ʿanhum turidu zinata l-hayati l-dun'ya wala tutiʿ man aghfalna qalbahu ʿan dhik'rina wa-ittabaʿa hawahu wakana amruhu furutan
waquli l-haqu min rabbikum faman shaa falyu'min waman shaa falyakfur inna aʿtadna lilzzalimina naran ahata bihim suradiquha wa-in yastaghithu yughathu bimain kal-muh'li yashwi l-wujuha bi'sa l-sharabu wasaat mur'tafaqan
inna alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati inna la nudiʿu ajra man ahsana ʿamalan
ulaika lahum jannatu ʿadnin tajri min tahtihimu l-anharu yuhallawna fiha min asawira min dhahabin wayalbasuna thiyaban khud'ran min sundusin wa-is'tabraqin muttakiina fiha ʿala l-araiki niʿ'ma l-thawabu wahasunat mur'tafaqan
wa-id'rib lahum mathalan rajulayni jaʿalna li-ahadihima jannatayni min aʿnabin wahafafnahuma binakhlin wajaʿalna baynahuma zarʿan
kil'ta l-janatayni atat ukulaha walam tazlim min'hu shayan wafajjarna khilalahuma naharan
wakana lahu thamarun faqala lisahibihi wahuwa yuhawiruhu ana aktharu minka malan wa-aʿazzu nafaran
wadakhala jannatahu wahuwa zalimun linafsihi qala ma azunnu an tabida hadhihi abadan
wama azunnu l-saʿata qaimatan wala-in rudidttu ila rabbi la-ajidanna khayran min'ha munqalaban
qala lahu sahibuhu wahuwa yuhawiruhu akafarta bi-alladhi khalaqaka min turabin thumma min nut'fatin thumma sawwaka rajulan
lakinna huwa l-lahu rabbi wala ush'riku birabbi ahadan
walawla idh dakhalta jannataka qul'ta ma shaa l-lahu la quwwata illa bil-lahi in tarani ana aqalla minka malan wawaladan
faʿasa rabbi an yu'tiyani khayran min jannatika wayur'sila ʿalayha hus'banan mina l-samai fatus'biha saʿidan zalaqan
aw yus'biha mauha ghawran falan tastatiʿa lahu talaban
wa-uhita bithamarihi fa-asbaha yuqallibu kaffayhi ʿala ma anfaqa fiha wahiya khawiyatun ʿala ʿurushiha wayaqulu yalaytani lam ush'rik birabbi ahadan
walam takun lahu fi-atun yansurunahu min duni l-lahi wama kana muntasiran
hunalika l-walayatu lillahi l-haqi huwa khayrun thawaban wakhayrun ʿuq'ban
wa-id'rib lahum mathala l-hayati l-dun'ya kamain anzalnahu mina l-samai fa-ikh'talata bihi nabatu l-ardi fa-asbaha hashiman tadhruhu l-riyahu wakana l-lahu ʿala kulli shayin muq'tadiran
al-malu wal-banuna zinatu l-hayati l-dun'ya wal-baqiyatu l-salihatu khayrun ʿinda rabbika thawaban wakhayrun amalan
wayawma nusayyiru l-jibala watara l-arda barizatan wahasharnahum falam nughadir min'hum ahadan
waʿuridu ʿala rabbika saffan laqad ji'tumuna kama khalaqnakum awwala marratin bal zaʿamtum allan najʿala lakum mawʿidan
wawudiʿa l-kitabu fatara l-muj'rimina mush'fiqina mimma fihi wayaquluna yawaylatana mali hadha l-kitabi la yughadiru saghiratan wala kabiratan illa ahsaha wawajadu ma ʿamilu hadiran wala yazlimu rabbuka ahadan
wa-idh qul'na lil'malaikati us'judu liadama fasajadu illa ib'lisa kana mina l-jini fafasaqa ʿan amri rabbihi afatattakhidhunahu wadhurriyyatahu awliyaa min duni wahum lakum ʿaduwwun bi'sa lilzzalimina badalan
ma ashhadttuhum khalqa l-samawati wal-ardi wala khalqa anfusihim wama kuntu muttakhidha l-mudilina ʿadudan
wayawma yaqulu nadu shurakaiya alladhina zaʿamtum fadaʿawhum falam yastajibu lahum wajaʿalna baynahum mawbiqan
waraa l-muj'rimuna l-nara fazannu annahum muwaqiʿuha walam yajidu ʿanha masrifan
walaqad sarrafna fi hadha l-qur'ani lilnnasi min kulli mathalin wakana l-insanu akthara shayin jadalan
wama manaʿa l-nasa an yu'minu idh jaahumu l-huda wayastaghfiru rabbahum illa an tatiyahum sunnatu l-awalina aw yatiyahumu l-ʿadhabu qubulan
wama nur'silu l-mur'salina illa mubashirina wamundhirina wayujadilu alladhina kafaru bil-batili liyud'hidu bihi l-haqa wa-ittakhadhu ayati wama undhiru huzuwan
waman azlamu mimman dhukkira biayati rabbihi fa-aʿrada ʿanha wanasiya ma qaddamat yadahu inna jaʿalna ʿala qulubihim akinnatan an yafqahuhu wafi adhanihim waqran wa-in tadʿuhum ila l-huda falan yahtadu idhan abadan
warabbuka l-ghafuru dhu l-rahmati law yuakhidhuhum bima kasabu laʿajjala lahumu l-ʿadhaba bal lahum mawʿidun lan yajidu min dunihi mawilan
watil'ka l-qura ahlaknahum lamma zalamu wajaʿalna limahlikihim mawʿidan
wa-idh qala musa lifatahu la abrahu hatta ablugha majmaʿa l-bahrayni aw amdiya huquban
falamma balagha majmaʿa baynihima nasiya hutahuma fa-ittakhadha sabilahu fi l-bahri saraban
falamma jawaza qala lifatahu atina ghadaana laqad laqina min safarina hadha nasaban
qala ara-ayta idh awayna ila l-sakhrati fa-inni nasitu l-huta wama ansanihu illa l-shaytanu an adhkurahu wa-ittakhadha sabilahu fi l-bahri ʿajaban
qala dhalika ma kunna nabghi fa-ir'tadda ʿala atharihima qasasan
fawajada ʿabdan min ʿibadina ataynahu rahmatan min ʿindina waʿallamnahu min ladunna ʿil'man
qala lahu musa hal attabiʿuka ʿala an tuʿallimani mimma ʿullim'ta rush'dan
qala innaka lan tastatiʿa maʿiya sabran
wakayfa tasbiru ʿala ma lam tuhit bihi khub'ran
qala satajiduni in shaa l-lahu sabiran wala aʿsi laka amran
qala fa-ini ittabaʿtani fala tasalni ʿan shayin hatta uh'ditha laka min'hu dhik'ran
fa-intalaqa hatta idha rakiba fi l-safinati kharaqaha qala akharaqtaha litugh'riqa ahlaha laqad ji'ta shayan im'ran
qala alam aqul innaka lan tastatiʿa maʿiya sabran
qala la tuakhidh'ni bima nasitu wala tur'hiq'ni min amri ʿus'ran
fa-intalaqa hatta idha laqiya ghulaman faqatalahu qala aqatalta nafsan zakiyyatan bighayri nafsin laqad ji'ta shayan nuk'ran
qala alam aqul laka innaka lan tastatiʿa maʿiya sabran
qala in sa-altuka ʿan shayin baʿdaha fala tusahib'ni qad balaghta min ladunni ʿudh'ran
fa-intalaqa hatta idha ataya ahla qaryatin is'tatʿama ahlaha fa-abaw an yudayyifuhuma fawajada fiha jidaran yuridu an yanqadda fa-aqamahu qala law shi'ta lattakhadhta ʿalayhi ajran
qala hadha firaqu bayni wabaynika sa-unabbi-uka bitawili ma lam tastatiʿ ʿalayhi sabran
amma l-safinatu fakanat limasakina yaʿmaluna fi l-bahri fa-aradttu an aʿibaha wakana waraahum malikun yakhudhu kulla safinatin ghasban
wa-amma l-ghulamu fakana abawahu mu'minayni fakhashina an yur'hiqahuma tugh'yanan wakuf'ran
fa-aradna an yub'dilahuma rabbuhuma khayran min'hu zakatan wa-aqraba ruh'man
wa-amma l-jidaru fakana lighulamayni yatimayni fi l-madinati wakana tahtahu kanzun lahuma wakana abuhuma salihan fa-arada rabbuka an yablugha ashuddahuma wayastakhrija kanzahuma rahmatan min rabbika wama faʿaltuhu ʿan amri dhalika tawilu ma lam tastiʿ ʿalayhi sabran
wayasalunaka ʿan dhi l-qarnayni qul sa-atlu ʿalaykum min'hu dhik'ran
inna makkanna lahu fi l-ardi waataynahu min kulli shayin sababan
fa-atbaʿa sababan
hatta idha balagha maghriba l-shamsi wajadaha taghrubu fi ʿaynin hami-atin wawajada ʿindaha qawman qul'na yadha l-qarnayni imma an tuʿadhiba wa-imma an tattakhidha fihim hus'nan
qala amma man zalama fasawfa nuʿadhibuhu thumma yuraddu ila rabbihi fayuʿadhibuhu ʿadhaban nuk'ran
wa-amma man amana waʿamila salihan falahu jazaan l-hus'na wasanaqulu lahu min amrina yus'ran
thumma atbaʿa sababan
hatta idha balagha matliʿa l-shamsi wajadaha tatluʿu ʿala qawmin lam najʿal lahum min duniha sit'ran
kadhalika waqad ahatna bima ladayhi khub'ran
thumma atbaʿa sababan
hatta idha balagha bayna l-sadayni wajada min dunihima qawman la yakaduna yafqahuna qawlan
qalu yadha l-qarnayni inna yajuja wamajuja muf'siduna fi l-ardi fahal najʿalu laka kharjan ʿala an tajʿala baynana wabaynahum saddan
qala ma makkanni fihi rabbi khayrun fa-aʿinuni biquwwatin ajʿal baynakum wabaynahum radman
atuni zubara l-hadidi hatta idha sawa bayna l-sadafayni qala unfukhu hatta idha jaʿalahu naran qala atuni uf'righ ʿalayhi qit'ran
fama is'taʿu an yazharuhu wama is'tataʿu lahu naqban
qala hadha rahmatun min rabbi fa-idha jaa waʿdu rabbi jaʿalahu dakkaa wakana waʿdu rabbi haqqan
watarakna baʿdahum yawma-idhin yamuju fi baʿdin wanufikha fi l-suri fajamaʿnahum jamʿan
waʿaradna jahannama yawma-idhin lil'kafirina ʿardan
alladhina kanat aʿyunuhum fi ghitain ʿan dhik'ri wakanu la yastatiʿuna samʿan
afahasiba alladhina kafaru an yattakhidhu ʿibadi min duni awliyaa inna aʿtadna jahannama lil'kafirina nuzulan
qul hal nunabbi-ukum bil-akhsarina aʿmalan
alladhina dalla saʿyuhum fi l-hayati l-dun'ya wahum yahsabuna annahum yuh'sinuna sun'ʿan
ulaika alladhina kafaru biayati rabbihim waliqaihi fahabitat aʿmaluhum fala nuqimu lahum yawma l-qiyamati waznan
dhalika jazauhum jahannamu bima kafaru wa-ittakhadhu ayati warusuli huzuwan
inna alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati kanat lahum jannatu l-fir'dawsi nuzulan
khalidina fiha la yabghuna ʿanha hiwalan
qul law kana l-bahru midadan likalimati rabbi lanafida l-bahru qabla an tanfada kalimatu rabbi walaw ji'na bimith'lihi madadan
qul innama ana basharun mith'lukum yuha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun faman kana yarju liqaa rabbihi falyaʿmal ʿamalan salihan wala yush'rik biʿibadati rabbihi ahadan
kaf-ha-ya-ain-sad
dhik'ru rahmati rabbika ʿabdahu zakariyya
idh nada rabbahu nidaan khafiyyan
qala rabbi inni wahana l-ʿazmu minni wa-ish'taʿala l-rasu shayban walam akun biduʿaika rabbi shaqiyyan
wa-inni khif'tu l-mawaliya min warai wakanati im'ra-ati ʿaqiran fahab li min ladunka waliyyan
yarithuni wayarithu min ali yaʿquba wa-ij'ʿalhu rabbi radiyyan
yazakariyya inna nubashiruka bighulamin us'muhu yahya lam najʿal lahu min qablu samiyyan
qala rabbi anna yakunu li ghulamun wakanati im'ra-ati ʿaqiran waqad balaghtu mina l-kibari ʿitiyyan
qala kadhalika qala rabbuka huwa ʿalayya hayyinun waqad khalaqtuka min qablu walam taku shayan
qala rabbi ij'ʿal li ayatan qala ayatuka alla tukallima l-nasa thalatha layalin sawiyyan
fakharaja ʿala qawmihi mina l-mih'rabi fa-awha ilayhim an sabbihu buk'ratan waʿashiyyan
yayahya khudhi l-kitaba biquwwatin waataynahu l-huk'ma sabiyyan
wahananan min ladunna wazakatan wakana taqiyyan
wabarran biwalidayhi walam yakun jabbaran ʿasiyyan
wasalamun ʿalayhi yawma wulida wayawma yamutu wayawma yub'ʿathu hayyan
wa-udh'kur fi l-kitabi maryama idhi intabadhat min ahliha makanan sharqiyyan
fa-ittakhadhat min dunihim hijaban fa-arsalna ilayha ruhana fatamathala laha basharan sawiyyan
qalat inni aʿudhu bil-rahmani minka in kunta taqiyyan
qala innama ana rasulu rabbiki li-ahaba laki ghulaman zakiyyan
qalat anna yakunu li ghulamun walam yamsasni basharun walam aku baghiyyan
qala kadhaliki qala rabbuki huwa ʿalayya hayyinun walinajʿalahu ayatan lilnnasi warahmatan minna wakana amran maqdiyyan
fahamalathu fa-intabadhat bihi makanan qasiyyan
fa-ajaaha l-makhadu ila jidh'ʿi l-nakhlati qalat yalaytani mittu qabla hadha wakuntu nasyan mansiyyan
fanadaha min tahtiha alla tahzani qad jaʿala rabbuki tahtaki sariyyan
wahuzzi ilayki bijidh'ʿi l-nakhlati tusaqit ʿalayki rutaban janiyyan
fakuli wa-ish'rabi waqarri ʿaynan fa-imma tarayinna mina l-bashari ahadan faquli inni nadhartu lilrrahmani sawman falan ukallima l-yawma insiyyan
fa-atat bihi qawmaha tahmiluhu qalu yamaryamu laqad ji'ti shayan fariyyan
yaukh'ta haruna ma kana abuki im'ra-a sawin wama kanat ummuki baghiyyan
fa-asharat ilayhi qalu kayfa nukallimu man kana fi l-mahdi sabiyyan
qala inni ʿabdu l-lahi ataniya l-kitaba wajaʿalani nabiyyan
wajaʿalani mubarakan ayna ma kuntu wa-awsani bil-salati wal-zakati ma dum'tu hayyan
wabarran biwalidati walam yajʿalni jabbaran shaqiyyan
wal-salamu ʿalayya yawma wulidttu wayawma amutu wayawma ub'ʿathu hayyan
dhalika ʿisa ub'nu maryama qawla l-haqi alladhi fihi yamtaruna
ma kana lillahi an yattakhidha min waladin sub'hanahu idha qada amran fa-innama yaqulu lahu kun fayakunu
wa-inna l-laha rabbi warabbukum fa-uʿ'buduhu hadha siratun mus'taqimun
fa-ikh'talafa l-ahzabu min baynihim fawaylun lilladhina kafaru min mashhadi yawmin ʿazimin
asmiʿ bihim wa-absir yawma yatunana lakini l-zalimuna l-yawma fi dalalin mubinin
wa-andhir'hum yawma l-hasrati idh qudiya l-amru wahum fi ghaflatin wahum la yu'minuna
inna nahnu narithu l-arda waman ʿalayha wa-ilayna yur'jaʿuna
wa-udh'kur fi l-kitabi ib'rahima innahu kana siddiqan nabiyyan
idh qala li-abihi yaabati lima taʿbudu ma la yasmaʿu wala yub'siru wala yugh'ni ʿanka shayan
yaabati inni qad jaani mina l-ʿil'mi ma lam yatika fa-ittabiʿ'ni ahdika siratan sawiyyan
yaabati la taʿbudi l-shaytana inna l-shaytana kana lilrrahmani ʿasiyyan
yaabati inni akhafu an yamassaka ʿadhabun mina l-rahmani fatakuna lilshaytani waliyyan
qala araghibun anta ʿan alihati yaib'rahimu la-in lam tantahi la-arjumannaka wa-uh'jur'ni maliyyan
qala salamun ʿalayka sa-astaghfiru laka rabbi innahu kana bi hafiyyan
wa-aʿtazilukum wama tadʿuna min duni l-lahi wa-adʿu rabbi ʿasa alla akuna biduʿai rabbi shaqiyyan
falamma iʿ'tazalahum wama yaʿbuduna min duni l-lahi wahabna lahu is'haqa wayaʿquba wakullan jaʿalna nabiyyan
wawahabna lahum min rahmatina wajaʿalna lahum lisana sid'qin ʿaliyyan
wa-udh'kur fi l-kitabi musa innahu kana mukh'lasan wakana rasulan nabiyyan
wanadaynahu min janibi l-turi l-aymani waqarrabnahu najiyyan
wawahabna lahu min rahmatina akhahu haruna nabiyyan
wa-udh'kur fi l-kitabi is'maʿila innahu kana sadiqa l-waʿdi wakana rasulan nabiyyan
wakana yamuru ahlahu bil-salati wal-zakati wakana ʿinda rabbihi mardiyyan
wa-udh'kur fi l-kitabi id'risa innahu kana siddiqan nabiyyan
warafaʿnahu makanan ʿaliyyan
ulaika alladhina anʿama l-lahu ʿalayhim mina l-nabiyina min dhurriyyati adama wamimman hamalna maʿa nuhin wamin dhurriyyati ib'rahima wa-is'raila wamimman hadayna wa-ij'tabayna idha tut'la ʿalayhim ayatu l-rahmani kharru sujjadan wabukiyyan
fakhalafa min baʿdihim khalfun adaʿu l-salata wa-ittabaʿu l-shahawati fasawfa yalqawna ghayyan
illa man taba waamana waʿamila salihan fa-ulaika yadkhuluna l-janata wala yuz'lamuna shayan
jannati ʿadnin allati waʿada l-rahmanu ʿibadahu bil-ghaybi innahu kana waʿduhu matiyyan
la yasmaʿuna fiha laghwan illa salaman walahum riz'quhum fiha buk'ratan waʿashiyyan
til'ka l-janatu allati nurithu min ʿibadina man kana taqiyyan
wama natanazzalu illa bi-amri rabbika lahu ma bayna aydina wama khalfana wama bayna dhalika wama kana rabbuka nasiyyan
rabbu l-samawati wal-ardi wama baynahuma fa-uʿ'bud'hu wa-is'tabir liʿibadatihi hal taʿlamu lahu samiyyan
wayaqulu l-insanu a-idha ma mittu lasawfa ukh'raju hayyan
awala yadhkuru l-insanu anna khalaqnahu min qablu walam yaku shayan
fawarabbika lanahshurannahum wal-shayatina thumma lanuh'dirannahum hawla jahannama jithiyyan
thumma lananziʿanna min kulli shiʿatin ayyuhum ashaddu ʿala l-rahmani ʿitiyyan
thumma lanahnu aʿlamu bi-alladhina hum awla biha siliyyan
wa-in minkum illa wariduha kana ʿala rabbika hatman maqdiyyan
thumma nunajji alladhina ittaqaw wanadharu l-zalimina fiha jithiyyan

wakam ahlakna qablahum min qarnin hum ahsanu athathan wari'yan
qul man kana fi l-dalalati falyamdud lahu l-rahmanu maddan hatta idha ra-aw ma yuʿaduna imma l-ʿadhaba wa-imma l-saʿata fasayaʿlamuna man huwa sharrun makanan wa-adʿafu jundan

wanarithuhu ma yaqulu wayatina fardan

idh awhayna ila ummika ma yuha
ani iq'dhifihi fi l-tabuti fa-iq'dhifihi fi l-yami falyul'qihi l-yamu bil-sahili yakhudh'hu ʿaduwwun li waʿaduwwun lahu wa-alqaytu ʿalayka mahabbatan minni walitus'naʿa ʿala ʿayni
idh tamshi ukh'tuka fataqulu hal adullukum ʿala man yakfuluhu farajaʿnaka ila ummika kay taqarra ʿaynuha wala tahzana waqatalta nafsan fanajjaynaka mina l-ghami wafatannaka futunan falabith'ta sinina fi ahli madyana thumma ji'ta ʿala qadarin yamusa
wa-is'tanaʿtuka linafsi
idh'hab anta wa-akhuka biayati wala taniya fi dhik'ri
idh'haba ila fir'ʿawna innahu tagha
faqula lahu qawlan layyinan laʿallahu yatadhakkaru aw yakhsha
qala rabbana innana nakhafu an yafruta ʿalayna aw an yatgha
qala la takhafa innani maʿakuma asmaʿu wa-ara
fatiyahu faqula inna rasula rabbika fa-arsil maʿana bani is'raila wala tuʿadhib'hum qad ji'naka biayatin min rabbika wal-salamu ʿala mani ittabaʿa l-huda
inna qad uhiya ilayna anna l-ʿadhaba ʿala man kadhaba watawalla
qala faman rabbukuma yamusa

qala fama balu l-quruni l-ula
qala ʿil'muha ʿinda rabbi fi kitabin la yadillu rabbi wala yansa
alladhi jaʿala lakumu l-arda mahdan wasalaka lakum fiha subulan wa-anzala mina l-samai maan fa-akhrajna bihi azwajan min nabatin shatta

min'ha khalaqnakum wafiha nuʿidukum wamin'ha nukh'rijukum taratan ukh'ra
walaqad araynahu ayatina kullaha fakadhaba wa-aba
qala aji'tana litukh'rijana min ardina bisih'rika yamusa

qala mawʿidukum yawmu l-zinati wa-an yuh'shara l-nasu duhan
fatawalla fir'ʿawnu fajamaʿa kaydahu thumma ata
qala lahum musa waylakum la taftaru ʿala l-lahi kadhiban fayus'hitakum biʿadhabin waqad khaba mani if'tara
fatanazaʿu amrahum baynahum wa-asarru l-najwa
qalu in hadhani lasahirani yuridani an yukh'rijakum min ardikum bisih'rihima wayadhhaba bitariqatikumu l-muth'la
fa-ajmiʿu kaydakum thumma i'tu saffan waqad aflaha l-yawma mani is'taʿla
qalu yamusa imma an tul'qiya wa-imma an nakuna awwala man alqa
qala bal alqu fa-idha hibaluhum waʿisiyyuhum yukhayyalu ilayhi min sih'rihim annaha tasʿa
fa-awjasa fi nafsihi khifatan musa
qul'na la takhaf innaka anta l-aʿla
wa-alqi ma fi yaminika talqaf ma sanaʿu innama sanaʿu kaydu sahirin wala yuf'lihu l-sahiru haythu ata
fa-ul'qiya l-saharatu sujjadan qalu amanna birabbi haruna wamusa
qala amantum lahu qabla an adhana lakum innahu lakabirukumu alladhi ʿallamakumu l-sih'ra fala-uqattiʿanna aydiyakum wa-arjulakum min khilafin wala-usallibannakum fi judhuʿi l-nakhli walataʿlamunna ayyuna ashaddu ʿadhaban wa-abqa
qalu lan nu'thiraka ʿala ma jaana mina l-bayinati wa-alladhi fatarana fa-iq'di ma anta qadin innama taqdi hadhihi l-hayata l-dun'ya
inna amanna birabbina liyaghfira lana khatayana wama akrahtana ʿalayhi mina l-sih'ri wal-lahu khayrun wa-abqa
innahu man yati rabbahu muj'riman fa-inna lahu jahannama la yamutu fiha wala yahya

fa-atbaʿahum fir'ʿawnu bijunudihi faghashiyahum mina l-yami ma ghashiyahum
wa-adalla fir'ʿawnu qawmahu wama hada
yabani is'raila qad anjaynakum min ʿaduwwikum wawaʿadnakum janiba l-turi l-aymana wanazzalna ʿalaykumu l-mana wal-salwa
kulu min tayyibati ma razaqnakum wala tatghaw fihi fayahilla ʿalaykum ghadabi waman yahlil ʿalayhi ghadabi faqad hawa
wa-inni laghaffarun liman taba waamana waʿamila salihan thumma ih'tada
wama aʿjalaka ʿan qawmika yamusa
qala hum ulai ʿala athari waʿajil'tu ilayka rabbi litarda
qala fa-inna qad fatanna qawmaka min baʿdika wa-adallahumu l-samiriyu
farajaʿa musa ila qawmihi ghadbana asifan qala yaqawmi alam yaʿid'kum rabbukum waʿdan hasanan afatala ʿalaykumu l-ʿahdu am aradttum an yahilla ʿalaykum ghadabun min rabbikum fa-akhlaftum mawʿidi
qalu ma akhlafna mawʿidaka bimalkina walakinna hummil'na awzaran min zinati l-qawmi faqadhafnaha fakadhalika alqa l-samiriyu
fa-akhraja lahum ʿij'lan jasadan lahu khuwarun faqalu hadha ilahukum wa-ilahu musa fanasiya
afala yarawna alla yarjiʿu ilayhim qawlan wala yamliku lahum darran wala nafʿan
walaqad qala lahum harunu min qablu yaqawmi innama futintum bihi wa-inna rabbakumu l-rahmanu fa-ittabiʿuni wa-atiʿu amri
qalu lan nabraha ʿalayhi ʿakifina hatta yarjiʿa ilayna musa
qala yaharunu ma manaʿaka idh ra-aytahum dallu
alla tattabiʿani afaʿasayta amri

qala fama khatbuka yasamiriyyu
qala basur'tu bima lam yabsuru bihi faqabadtu qabdatan min athari l-rasuli fanabadhtuha wakadhalika sawwalat li nafsi
qala fa-idh'hab fa-inna laka fi l-hayati an taqula la misasa wa-inna laka mawʿidan lan tukh'lafahu wa-unzur ila ilahika alladhi zalta ʿalayhi ʿakifan lanuharriqannahu thumma lanansifannahu fi l-yami nasfan
innama ilahukumu l-lahu alladhi la ilaha illa huwa wasiʿa kulla shayin ʿil'man
kadhalika naqussu ʿalayka min anbai ma qad sabaqa waqad ataynaka min ladunna dhik'ran
man aʿrada ʿanhu fa-innahu yahmilu yawma l-qiyamati wiz'ran
khalidina fihi wasaa lahum yawma l-qiyamati him'lan

yatakhafatuna baynahum in labith'tum illa ʿashran
nahnu aʿlamu bima yaquluna idh yaqulu amthaluhum tariqatan in labith'tum illa yawman

fayadharuha qaʿan safsafan
la tara fiha ʿiwajan wala amtan

yawma-idhin la tanfaʿu l-shafaʿatu illa man adhina lahu l-rahmanu waradiya lahu qawlan
yaʿlamu ma bayna aydihim wama khalfahum wala yuhituna bihi ʿil'man
waʿanati l-wujuhu lil'hayyi l-qayumi waqad khaba man hamala zul'man
waman yaʿmal mina l-salihati wahuwa mu'minun fala yakhafu zul'man wala hadman
wakadhalika anzalnahu qur'anan ʿarabiyyan wasarrafna fihi mina l-waʿidi laʿallahum yattaquna aw yuh'dithu lahum dhik'ran
fataʿala l-lahu l-maliku l-haqu wala taʿjal bil-qur'ani min qabli an yuq'da ilayka wahyuhu waqul rabbi zid'ni ʿil'man
walaqad ʿahid'na ila adama min qablu fanasiya walam najid lahu ʿazman
wa-idh qul'na lil'malaikati us'judu liadama fasajadu illa ib'lisa aba

inna laka alla tajuʿa fiha wala taʿra
wa-annaka la tazma-u fiha wala tadha
fawaswasa ilayhi l-shaytanu qala yaadamu hal adulluka ʿala shajarati l-khul'di wamul'kin la yabla

thumma ij'tabahu rabbuhu fataba ʿalayhi wahada
qala ih'bita min'ha jamiʿan baʿdukum libaʿdin ʿaduwwun fa-imma yatiyannakum minni hudan famani ittabaʿa hudaya fala yadillu wala yashqa
waman aʿrada ʿan dhik'ri fa-inna lahu maʿishatan dankan wanahshuruhu yawma l-qiyamati aʿma
qala rabbi lima hashartani aʿma waqad kuntu basiran
qala kadhalika atatka ayatuna fanasitaha wakadhalika l-yawma tunsa
wakadhalika najzi man asrafa walam yu'min biayati rabbihi walaʿadhabu l-akhirati ashaddu wa-abqa
afalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakna qablahum mina l-quruni yamshuna fi masakinihim inna fi dhalika laayatin li-uli l-nuha
walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika lakana lizaman wa-ajalun musamman
fa-is'bir ʿala ma yaquluna wasabbih bihamdi rabbika qabla tuluʿi l-shamsi waqabla ghurubiha wamin anai al-layli fasabbih wa-atrafa l-nahari laʿallaka tarda
wala tamuddanna ʿaynayka ila ma mattaʿna bihi azwajan min'hum zahrata l-hayati l-dun'ya linaftinahum fihi wariz'qu rabbika khayrun wa-abqa
wamur ahlaka bil-salati wa-is'tabir ʿalayha la nasaluka riz'qan nahnu narzuquka wal-ʿaqibatu lilttaqwa
waqalu lawla yatina biayatin min rabbihi awalam tatihim bayyinatu ma fi l-suhufi l-ula
walaw anna ahlaknahum biʿadhabin min qablihi laqalu rabbana lawla arsalta ilayna rasulan fanattabiʿa ayatika min qabli an nadhilla wanakhza
qul kullun mutarabbisun fatarabbasu fasataʿlamuna man ashabu l-sirati l-sawiyi wamani ih'tada
iq'taraba lilnnasi hisabuhum wahum fi ghaflatin muʿ'riduna
ma yatihim min dhik'rin min rabbihim muh'dathin illa is'tamaʿuhu wahum yalʿabuna

bal qalu adghathu ahlamin bali if'tarahu bal huwa shaʿirun falyatina biayatin kama ur'sila l-awaluna
ma amanat qablahum min qaryatin ahlaknaha afahum yu'minuna

wama jaʿalnahum jasadan la yakuluna l-taʿama wama kanu khalidina
thumma sadaqnahumu l-waʿda fa-anjaynahum waman nashau wa-ahlakna l-mus'rifina

falamma ahassu basana idha hum min'ha yarkuduna

qalu yawaylana inna kunna zalimina
fama zalat til'ka daʿwahum hatta jaʿalnahum hasidan khamidina
wama khalaqna l-samaa wal-arda wama baynahuma laʿibina
law aradna an nattakhidha lahwan la-ittakhadhnahu min ladunna in kunna faʿilina
bal naqdhifu bil-haqi ʿala l-batili fayadmaghuhu fa-idha huwa zahiqun walakumu l-waylu mimma tasifuna
