yusabbihuna al-layla wal-nahara la yafturuna
ami ittakhadhu alihatan mina l-ardi hum yunshiruna
law kana fihima alihatun illa l-lahu lafasadata fasub'hana l-lahi rabbi l-ʿarshi ʿamma yasifuna
la yus'alu ʿamma yafʿalu wahum yus'aluna
ami ittakhadhu min dunihi alihatan qul hatu bur'hanakum hadha dhik'ru man maʿiya wadhik'ru man qabli bal aktharuhum la yaʿlamuna l-haqa fahum muʿ'riduna
wama arsalna min qablika min rasulin illa nuhi ilayhi annahu la ilaha illa ana fa-uʿ'buduni
waqalu ittakhadha l-rahmanu waladan sub'hanahu bal ʿibadun muk'ramuna
la yasbiqunahu bil-qawli wahum bi-amrihi yaʿmaluna
yaʿlamu ma bayna aydihim wama khalfahum wala yashfaʿuna illa limani ir'tada wahum min khashyatihi mush'fiquna
waman yaqul min'hum inni ilahun min dunihi fadhalika najzihi jahannama kadhalika najzi l-zalimina
awalam yara alladhina kafaru anna l-samawati wal-arda kanata ratqan fafataqnahuma wajaʿalna mina l-mai kulla shayin hayyin afala yu'minuna
wajaʿalna fi l-ardi rawasiya an tamida bihim wajaʿalna fiha fijajan subulan laʿallahum yahtaduna
wajaʿalna l-samaa saqfan mahfuzan wahum ʿan ayatiha muʿ'riduna
wahuwa alladhi khalaqa al-layla wal-nahara wal-shamsa wal-qamara kullun fi falakin yasbahuna
wama jaʿalna libasharin min qablika l-khul'da afa-in mitta fahumu l-khaliduna
kullu nafsin dhaiqatu l-mawti wanablukum bil-shari wal-khayri fit'natan wa-ilayna tur'jaʿuna
wa-idha raaka alladhina kafaru in yattakhidhunaka illa huzuwan ahadha alladhi yadhkuru alihatakum wahum bidhik'ri l-rahmani hum kafiruna
khuliqa l-insanu min ʿajalin sa-urikum ayati fala tastaʿjiluni
wayaquluna mata hadha l-waʿdu in kuntum sadiqina
law yaʿlamu alladhina kafaru hina la yakuffuna ʿan wujuhihimu l-nara wala ʿan zuhurihim wala hum yunsaruna
bal tatihim baghtatan fatabhatuhum fala yastatiʿuna raddaha wala hum yunzaruna
walaqadi us'tuh'zi-a birusulin min qablika fahaqa bi-alladhina sakhiru min'hum ma kanu bihi yastahziuna
qul man yakla-ukum bi-al-layli wal-nahari mina l-rahmani bal hum ʿan dhik'ri rabbihim muʿ'riduna
am lahum alihatun tamnaʿuhum min dunina la yastatiʿuna nasra anfusihim wala hum minna yus'habuna
bal mattaʿna haulai waabaahum hatta tala ʿalayhimu l-ʿumuru afala yarawna anna nati l-arda nanqusuha min atrafiha afahumu l-ghalibuna
qul innama undhirukum bil-wahyi wala yasmaʿu l-sumu l-duʿaa idha ma yundharuna
wala-in massathum nafhatun min ʿadhabi rabbika layaqulunna yawaylana inna kunna zalimina
wanadaʿu l-mawazina l-qis'ta liyawmi l-qiyamati fala tuz'lamu nafsun shayan wa-in kana mith'qala habbatin min khardalin atayna biha wakafa bina hasibina
walaqad atayna musa waharuna l-fur'qana wadiyaan wadhik'ran lil'muttaqina
alladhina yakhshawna rabbahum bil-ghaybi wahum mina l-saʿati mush'fiquna
wahadha dhik'run mubarakun anzalnahu afa-antum lahu munkiruna
walaqad atayna ib'rahima rush'dahu min qablu wakunna bihi ʿalimina
idh qala li-abihi waqawmihi ma hadhihi l-tamathilu allati antum laha ʿakifuna
qalu wajadna abaana laha ʿabidina
qala laqad kuntum antum waabaukum fi dalalin mubinin
qalu aji'tana bil-haqi am anta mina l-laʿibina
qala bal rabbukum rabbu l-samawati wal-ardi alladhi fatarahunna wa-ana ʿala dhalikum mina l-shahidina
watal-lahi la-akidanna asnamakum baʿda an tuwallu mud'birina
fajaʿalahum judhadhan illa kabiran lahum laʿallahum ilayhi yarjiʿuna
qalu man faʿala hadha bialihatina innahu lamina l-zalimina
qalu samiʿ'na fatan yadhkuruhum yuqalu lahu ib'rahimu
qalu fatu bihi ʿala aʿyuni l-nasi laʿallahum yashhaduna
qalu a-anta faʿalta hadha bialihatina yaib'rahimu
qala bal faʿalahu kabiruhum hadha fasaluhum in kanu yantiquna
farajaʿu ila anfusihim faqalu innakum antumu l-zalimuna
thumma nukisu ʿala ruusihim laqad ʿalim'ta ma haulai yantiquna
qala afataʿbuduna min duni l-lahi ma la yanfaʿukum shayan wala yadurrukum
uffin lakum walima taʿbuduna min duni l-lahi afala taʿqiluna
qalu harriquhu wa-unsuru alihatakum in kuntum faʿilina
qul'na yanaru kuni bardan wasalaman ʿala ib'rahima
wa-aradu bihi kaydan fajaʿalnahumu l-akhsarina
wanajjaynahu walutan ila l-ardi allati barakna fiha lil'ʿalamina
wawahabna lahu is'haqa wayaʿquba nafilatan wakullan jaʿalna salihina
wajaʿalnahum a-immatan yahduna bi-amrina wa-awhayna ilayhim fiʿ'la l-khayrati wa-iqama l-salati waitaa l-zakati wakanu lana ʿabidina
walutan ataynahu huk'man waʿil'man wanajjaynahu mina l-qaryati allati kanat taʿmalu l-khabaitha innahum kanu qawma sawin fasiqina
wa-adkhalnahu fi rahmatina innahu mina l-salihina
wanuhan idh nada min qablu fa-is'tajabna lahu fanajjaynahu wa-ahlahu mina l-karbi l-ʿazimi
wanasarnahu mina l-qawmi alladhina kadhabu biayatina innahum kanu qawma sawin fa-aghraqnahum ajmaʿina
wadawuda wasulaymana idh yahkumani fi l-harthi idh nafashat fihi ghanamu l-qawmi wakunna lihuk'mihim shahidina
fafahhamnaha sulaymana wakullan atayna huk'man waʿil'man wasakharna maʿa dawuda l-jibala yusabbih'na wal-tayra wakunna faʿilina
waʿallamnahu sanʿata labusin lakum lituh'sinakum min basikum fahal antum shakiruna
walisulaymana l-riha ʿasifatan tajri bi-amrihi ila l-ardi allati barakna fiha wakunna bikulli shayin ʿalimina
wamina l-shayatini man yaghusuna lahu wayaʿmaluna ʿamalan duna dhalika wakunna lahum hafizina
wa-ayyuba idh nada rabbahu anni massaniya l-duru wa-anta arhamu l-rahimina
fa-is'tajabna lahu fakashafna ma bihi min durrin waataynahu ahlahu wamith'lahum maʿahum rahmatan min ʿindina wadhik'ra lil'ʿabidina
wa-is'maʿila wa-id'risa wadha l-kif'li kullun mina l-sabirina
wa-adkhalnahum fi rahmatina innahum mina l-salihina
wadha l-nuni idh dhahaba mughadiban fazanna an lan naqdira ʿalayhi fanada fi l-zulumati an la ilaha illa anta sub'hanaka inni kuntu mina l-zalimina
fa-is'tajabna lahu wanajjaynahu mina l-ghami wakadhalika nunji l-mu'minina
wazakariyya idh nada rabbahu rabbi la tadharni fardan wa-anta khayru l-warithina
fa-is'tajabna lahu wawahabna lahu yahya wa-aslahna lahu zawjahu innahum kanu yusariʿuna fi l-khayrati wayadʿunana raghaban warahaban wakanu lana khashiʿina
wa-allati ahsanat farjaha fanafakhna fiha min ruhina wajaʿalnaha wa-ib'naha ayatan lil'ʿalamina
inna hadhihi ummatukum ummatan wahidatan wa-ana rabbukum fa-uʿ'buduni
wataqattaʿu amrahum baynahum kullun ilayna rajiʿuna
faman yaʿmal mina l-salihati wahuwa mu'minun fala kuf'rana lisaʿyihi wa-inna lahu katibuna
waharamun ʿala qaryatin ahlaknaha annahum la yarjiʿuna
hatta idha futihat yajuju wamajuju wahum min kulli hadabin yansiluna
wa-iq'taraba l-waʿdu l-haqu fa-idha hiya shakhisatun absaru alladhina kafaru yawaylana qad kunna fi ghaflatin min hadha bal kunna zalimina
innakum wama taʿbuduna min duni l-lahi hasabu jahannama antum laha wariduna
law kana haulai alihatan ma waraduha wakullun fiha khaliduna
lahum fiha zafirun wahum fiha la yasmaʿuna
inna alladhina sabaqat lahum minna l-hus'na ulaika ʿanha mub'ʿaduna
la yasmaʿuna hasisaha wahum fi ma ish'tahat anfusuhum khaliduna
la yahzunuhumu l-fazaʿu l-akbaru watatalaqqahumu l-malaikatu hadha yawmukumu alladhi kuntum tuʿaduna
yawma natwi l-samaa katayyi l-sijili lil'kutubi kama badana awwala khalqin nuʿiduhu waʿdan ʿalayna inna kunna faʿilina
walaqad katabna fi l-zaburi min baʿdi l-dhik'ri anna l-arda yarithuha ʿibadiya l-salihuna
inna fi hadha labalaghan liqawmin ʿabidina
wama arsalnaka illa rahmatan lil'ʿalamina
qul innama yuha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun fahal antum mus'limuna
fa-in tawallaw faqul adhantukum ʿala sawain wa-in adri aqaribun am baʿidun ma tuʿaduna
innahu yaʿlamu l-jahra mina l-qawli wayaʿlamu ma taktumuna
wa-in adri laʿallahu fit'natun lakum wamataʿun ila hinin
qala rabbi uh'kum bil-haqi warabbuna l-rahmanu l-mus'taʿanu ʿala ma tasifuna
yaayyuha l-nasu ittaqu rabbakum inna zalzalata l-saʿati shayon ʿazimun
yawma tarawnaha tadhhalu kullu mur'diʿatin ʿamma ardaʿat watadaʿu kullu dhati hamlin hamlaha watara l-nasa sukara wama hum bisukara walakinna ʿadhaba l-lahi shadidun
wamina l-nasi man yujadilu fi l-lahi bighayri ʿil'min wayattabiʿu kulla shaytanin maridin
kutiba ʿalayhi annahu man tawallahu fa-annahu yudilluhu wayahdihi ila ʿadhabi l-saʿiri
yaayyuha l-nasu in kuntum fi raybin mina l-baʿthi fa-inna khalaqnakum min turabin thumma min nut'fatin thumma min ʿalaqatin thumma min mud'ghatin mukhallaqatin waghayri mukhallaqatin linubayyina lakum wanuqirru fi l-arhami ma nashau ila ajalin musamman thumma nukh'rijukum tif'lan thumma litablughu ashuddakum waminkum man yutawaffa waminkum man yuraddu ila ardhali l-ʿumuri likayla yaʿlama min baʿdi ʿil'min shayan watara l-arda hamidatan fa-idha anzalna ʿalayha l-maa ih'tazzat warabat wa-anbatat min kulli zawjin bahijin
dhalika bi-anna l-laha huwa l-haqu wa-annahu yuh'yi l-mawta wa-annahu ʿala kulli shayin qadirun
wa-anna l-saʿata atiyatun la rayba fiha wa-anna l-laha yabʿathu man fi l-quburi
wamina l-nasi man yujadilu fi l-lahi bighayri ʿil'min wala hudan wala kitabin munirin
thaniya ʿit'fihi liyudilla ʿan sabili l-lahi lahu fi l-dun'ya khiz'yun wanudhiquhu yawma l-qiyamati ʿadhaba l-hariqi
dhalika bima qaddamat yadaka wa-anna l-laha laysa bizallamin lil'ʿabidi
wamina l-nasi man yaʿbudu l-laha ʿala harfin fa-in asabahu khayrun it'ma-anna bihi wa-in asabathu fit'natun inqalaba ʿala wajhihi khasira l-dun'ya wal-akhirata dhalika huwa l-khus'ranu l-mubinu
yadʿu min duni l-lahi ma la yadurruhu wama la yanfaʿuhu dhalika huwa l-dalalu l-baʿidu
yadʿu laman darruhu aqrabu min nafʿihi labi'sa l-mawla walabi'sa l-ʿashiru
inna l-laha yud'khilu alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati jannatin tajri min tahtiha l-anharu inna l-laha yafʿalu ma yuridu
man kana yazunnu an lan yansurahu l-lahu fi l-dun'ya wal-akhirati falyamdud bisababin ila l-samai thumma l'yaqtaʿ falyanzur hal yudh'hibanna kayduhu ma yaghizu
wakadhalika anzalnahu ayatin bayyinatin wa-anna l-laha yahdi man yuridu
inna alladhina amanu wa-alladhina hadu wal-sabiina wal-nasara wal-majusa wa-alladhina ashraku inna l-laha yafsilu baynahum yawma l-qiyamati inna l-laha ʿala kulli shayin shahidun
alam tara anna l-laha yasjudu lahu man fi l-samawati waman fi l-ardi wal-shamsu wal-qamaru wal-nujumu wal-jibalu wal-shajaru wal-dawabu wakathirun mina l-nasi wakathirun haqqa ʿalayhi l-ʿadhabu waman yuhini l-lahu fama lahu min muk'rimin inna l-laha yafʿalu ma yashau
hadhani khasmani ikh'tasamu fi rabbihim fa-alladhina kafaru quttiʿat lahum thiyabun min narin yusabbu min fawqi ruusihimu l-hamimu
yus'haru bihi ma fi butunihim wal-juludu
walahum maqamiʿu min hadidin
kullama aradu an yakhruju min'ha min ghammin uʿidu fiha wadhuqu ʿadhaba l-hariqi
inna l-laha yud'khilu alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati jannatin tajri min tahtiha l-anharu yuhallawna fiha min asawira min dhahabin walu'lu-an walibasuhum fiha harirun
wahudu ila l-tayibi mina l-qawli wahudu ila sirati l-hamidi
inna alladhina kafaru wayasudduna ʿan sabili l-lahi wal-masjidi l-harami alladhi jaʿalnahu lilnnasi sawaan l-ʿakifu fihi wal-badi waman yurid fihi bi-il'hadin bizul'min nudhiq'hu min ʿadhabin alimin
wa-idh bawwana li-ib'rahima makana l-bayti an la tush'rik bi shayan watahhir baytiya lilttaifina wal-qaimina wal-rukaʿi l-sujudi
wa-adhin fi l-nasi bil-haji yatuka rijalan waʿala kulli damirin yatina min kulli fajjin ʿamiqin
liyashhadu manafiʿa lahum wayadhkuru is'ma l-lahi fi ayyamin maʿlumatin ʿala ma razaqahum min bahimati l-anʿami fakulu min'ha wa-atʿimu l-baisa l-faqira
thumma l'yaqdu tafathahum walyufu nudhurahum walyattawwafu bil-bayti l-ʿatiqi
dhalika waman yuʿazzim hurumati l-lahi fahuwa khayrun lahu ʿinda rabbihi wa-uhillat lakumu l-anʿamu illa ma yut'la ʿalaykum fa-ij'tanibu l-rij'sa mina l-awthani wa-ij'tanibu qawla l-zuri
hunafaa lillahi ghayra mush'rikina bihi waman yush'rik bil-lahi faka-annama kharra mina l-samai fatakhtafuhu l-tayru aw tahwi bihi l-rihu fi makanin sahiqin
dhalika waman yuʿazzim shaʿaira l-lahi fa-innaha min taqwa l-qulubi
lakum fiha manafiʿu ila ajalin musamman thumma mahilluha ila l-bayti l-ʿatiqi
walikulli ummatin jaʿalna mansakan liyadhkuru is'ma l-lahi ʿala ma razaqahum min bahimati l-anʿami fa-ilahukum ilahun wahidun falahu aslimu wabashiri l-mukh'bitina
alladhina idha dhukira l-lahu wajilat qulubuhum wal-sabirina ʿala ma asabahum wal-muqimi l-salati wamimma razaqnahum yunfiquna
wal-bud'na jaʿalnaha lakum min shaʿairi l-lahi lakum fiha khayrun fa-udh'kuru is'ma l-lahi ʿalayha sawaffa fa-idha wajabat junubuha fakulu min'ha wa-atʿimu l-qaniʿa wal-muʿ'tara kadhalika sakharnaha lakum laʿallakum tashkuruna
lan yanala l-laha luhumuha wala dimauha walakin yanaluhu l-taqwa minkum kadhalika sakharaha lakum litukabbiru l-laha ʿala ma hadakum wabashiri l-muh'sinina
inna l-laha yudafiʿu ʿani alladhina amanu inna l-laha la yuhibbu kulla khawwanin kafurin
udhina lilladhina yuqataluna bi-annahum zulimu wa-inna l-laha ʿala nasrihim laqadirun
alladhina ukh'riju min diyarihim bighayri haqqin illa an yaqulu rabbuna l-lahu walawla dafʿu l-lahi l-nasa baʿdahum bibaʿdin lahuddimat sawamiʿu wabiyaʿun wasalawatun wamasajidu yudh'karu fiha us'mu l-lahi kathiran walayansuranna l-lahu man yansuruhu inna l-laha laqawiyyun ʿazizun
alladhina in makkannahum fi l-ardi aqamu l-salata waatawu l-zakata wa-amaru bil-maʿrufi wanahaw ʿani l-munkari walillahi ʿaqibatu l-umuri
wa-in yukadhibuka faqad kadhabat qablahum qawmu nuhin waʿadun wathamudu
waqawmu ib'rahima waqawmu lutin
wa-ashabu madyana wakudhiba musa fa-amlaytu lil'kafirina thumma akhadhtuhum fakayfa kana nakiri
faka-ayyin min qaryatin ahlaknaha wahiya zalimatun fahiya khawiyatun ʿala ʿurushiha wabi'rin muʿattalatin waqasrin mashidin
afalam yasiru fi l-ardi fatakuna lahum qulubun yaʿqiluna biha aw adhanun yasmaʿuna biha fa-innaha la taʿma l-absaru walakin taʿma l-qulubu allati fi l-suduri
wayastaʿjilunaka bil-ʿadhabi walan yukh'lifa l-lahu waʿdahu wa-inna yawman ʿinda rabbika ka-alfi sanatin mimma taʿudduna
waka-ayyin min qaryatin amlaytu laha wahiya zalimatun thumma akhadhtuha wa-ilayya l-masiru
qul yaayyuha l-nasu innama ana lakum nadhirun mubinun
fa-alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati lahum maghfiratun wariz'qun karimun
wa-alladhina saʿaw fi ayatina muʿajizina ulaika ashabu l-jahimi
wama arsalna min qablika min rasulin wala nabiyyin illa idha tamanna alqa l-shaytanu fi um'niyyatihi fayansakhu l-lahu ma yul'qi l-shaytanu thumma yuh'kimu l-lahu ayatihi wal-lahu ʿalimun hakimun
liyajʿala ma yul'qi l-shaytanu fit'natan lilladhina fi qulubihim maradun wal-qasiyati qulubuhum wa-inna l-zalimina lafi shiqaqin baʿidin
waliyaʿlama alladhina utu l-ʿil'ma annahu l-haqu min rabbika fayu'minu bihi fatukh'bita lahu qulubuhum wa-inna l-laha lahadi alladhina amanu ila siratin mus'taqimin
wala yazalu alladhina kafaru fi mir'yatin min'hu hatta tatiyahumu l-saʿatu baghtatan aw yatiyahum ʿadhabu yawmin ʿaqimin
al-mul'ku yawma-idhin lillahi yahkumu baynahum fa-alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati fi jannati l-naʿimi
wa-alladhina kafaru wakadhabu biayatina fa-ulaika lahum ʿadhabun muhinun
wa-alladhina hajaru fi sabili l-lahi thumma qutilu aw matu layarzuqannahumu l-lahu riz'qan hasanan wa-inna l-laha lahuwa khayru l-raziqina
layud'khilannahum mud'khalan yardawnahu wa-inna l-laha laʿalimun halimun
dhalika waman ʿaqaba bimith'li ma ʿuqiba bihi thumma bughiya ʿalayhi layansurannahu l-lahu inna l-laha laʿafuwwun ghafurun
dhalika bi-anna l-laha yuliju al-layla fi l-nahari wayuliju l-nahara fi al-layli wa-anna l-laha samiʿun basirun
dhalika bi-anna l-laha huwa l-haqu wa-anna ma yadʿuna min dunihi huwa l-batilu wa-anna l-laha huwa l-ʿaliyu l-kabiru
alam tara anna l-laha anzala mina l-samai maan fatus'bihu l-ardu mukh'darratan inna l-laha latifun khabirun
lahu ma fi l-samawati wama fi l-ardi wa-inna l-laha lahuwa l-ghaniyu l-hamidu
alam tara anna l-laha sakhara lakum ma fi l-ardi wal-ful'ka tajri fi l-bahri bi-amrihi wayum'siku l-samaa an taqaʿa ʿala l-ardi illa bi-idh'nihi inna l-laha bil-nasi laraufun rahimun
wahuwa alladhi ahyakum thumma yumitukum thumma yuh'yikum inna l-insana lakafurun
likulli ummatin jaʿalna mansakan hum nasikuhu fala yunaziʿunnaka fi l-amri wa-ud'ʿu ila rabbika innaka laʿala hudan mus'taqimin
wa-in jadaluka faquli l-lahu aʿlamu bima taʿmaluna
al-lahu yahkumu baynakum yawma l-qiyamati fima kuntum fihi takhtalifuna
alam taʿlam anna l-laha yaʿlamu ma fi l-samai wal-ardi inna dhalika fi kitabin inna dhalika ʿala l-lahi yasirun
wayaʿbuduna min duni l-lahi ma lam yunazzil bihi sul'tanan wama laysa lahum bihi ʿil'mun wama lilzzalimina min nasirin
wa-idha tut'la ʿalayhim ayatuna bayyinatin taʿrifu fi wujuhi alladhina kafaru l-munkara yakaduna yastuna bi-alladhina yatluna ʿalayhim ayatina qul afa-unabbi-ukum bisharrin min dhalikumu l-naru waʿadaha l-lahu alladhina kafaru wabi'sa l-masiru
yaayyuha l-nasu duriba mathalun fa-is'tamiʿu lahu inna alladhina tadʿuna min duni l-lahi lan yakhluqu dhubaban walawi ij'tamaʿu lahu wa-in yaslub'humu l-dhubabu shayan la yastanqidhuhu min'hu daʿufa l-talibu wal-matlubu
ma qadaru l-laha haqqa qadrihi inna l-laha laqawiyyun ʿazizun
al-lahu yastafi mina l-malaikati rusulan wamina l-nasi inna l-laha samiʿun basirun
yaʿlamu ma bayna aydihim wama khalfahum wa-ila l-lahi tur'jaʿu l-umuru
yaayyuha alladhina amanu ir'kaʿu wa-us'judu wa-uʿ'budu rabbakum wa-if'ʿalu l-khayra laʿallakum tuf'lihuna
wajahidu fi l-lahi haqqa jihadihi huwa ij'tabakum wama jaʿala ʿalaykum fi l-dini min harajin millata abikum ib'rahima huwa sammakumu l-mus'limina min qablu wafi hadha liyakuna l-rasulu shahidan ʿalaykum watakunu shuhadaa ʿala l-nasi fa-aqimu l-salata waatu l-zakata wa-iʿ'tasimu bil-lahi huwa mawlakum faniʿ'ma l-mawla waniʿ'ma l-nasiru
qad aflaha l-mu'minuna
alladhina hum fi salatihim khashiʿuna
wa-alladhina hum ʿani l-laghwi muʿ'riduna
wa-alladhina hum lilzzakati faʿiluna
wa-alladhina hum lifurujihim hafizuna
illa ʿala azwajihim aw ma malakat aymanuhum fa-innahum ghayru malumina
famani ib'tagha waraa dhalika fa-ulaika humu l-ʿaduna
wa-alladhina hum li-amanatihim waʿahdihim raʿuna
wa-alladhina hum ʿala salawatihim yuhafizuna
ulaika humu l-warithuna
alladhina yarithuna l-fir'dawsa hum fiha khaliduna
walaqad khalaqna l-insana min sulalatin min tinin
thumma jaʿalnahu nut'fatan fi qararin makinin
thumma khalaqna l-nut'fata ʿalaqatan fakhalaqna l-ʿalaqata mud'ghatan fakhalaqna l-mud'ghata ʿizaman fakasawna l-ʿizama lahman thumma anshanahu khalqan akhara fatabaraka l-lahu ahsanu l-khaliqina
thumma innakum baʿda dhalika lamayyituna
thumma innakum yawma l-qiyamati tub'ʿathuna
walaqad khalaqna fawqakum sabʿa taraiqa wama kunna ʿani l-khalqi ghafilina
wa-anzalna mina l-samai maan biqadarin fa-askannahu fi l-ardi wa-inna ʿala dhahabin bihi laqadiruna
fa-anshana lakum bihi jannatin min nakhilin wa-aʿnabin lakum fiha fawakihu kathiratun wamin'ha takuluna
washajaratan takhruju min turi saynaa tanbutu bil-duh'ni wasib'ghin lil'akilina
wa-inna lakum fi l-anʿami laʿib'ratan nus'qikum mimma fi butuniha walakum fiha manafiʿu kathiratun wamin'ha takuluna
waʿalayha waʿala l-ful'ki tuh'maluna
walaqad arsalna nuhan ila qawmihi faqala yaqawmi uʿ'budu l-laha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaquna
faqala l-mala-u alladhina kafaru min qawmihi ma hadha illa basharun mith'lukum yuridu an yatafaddala ʿalaykum walaw shaa l-lahu la-anzala malaikatan ma samiʿ'na bihadha fi abaina l-awalina
in huwa illa rajulun bihi jinnatun fatarabbasu bihi hatta hinin
qala rabbi unsur'ni bima kadhabuni
fa-awhayna ilayhi ani is'naʿi l-ful'ka bi-aʿyunina wawahyina fa-idha jaa amruna wafara l-tanuru fa-us'luk fiha min kullin zawjayni ith'nayni wa-ahlaka illa man sabaqa ʿalayhi l-qawlu min'hum wala tukhatib'ni fi alladhina zalamu innahum mugh'raquna
fa-idha is'tawayta anta waman maʿaka ʿala l-ful'ki faquli l-hamdu lillahi alladhi najjana mina l-qawmi l-zalimina
waqul rabbi anzil'ni munzalan mubarakan wa-anta khayru l-munzilina
inna fi dhalika laayatin wa-in kunna lamub'talina
thumma anshana min baʿdihim qarnan akharina
fa-arsalna fihim rasulan min'hum ani uʿ'budu l-laha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaquna
waqala l-mala-u min qawmihi alladhina kafaru wakadhabu biliqai l-akhirati wa-atrafnahum fi l-hayati l-dun'ya ma hadha illa basharun mith'lukum yakulu mimma takuluna min'hu wayashrabu mimma tashrabuna
wala-in ataʿtum basharan mith'lakum innakum idhan lakhasiruna
ayaʿidukum annakum idha mittum wakuntum turaban waʿizaman annakum mukh'rajuna
hayhata hayhata lima tuʿaduna
in hiya illa hayatuna l-dun'ya namutu wanahya wama nahnu bimabʿuthina
in huwa illa rajulun if'tara ʿala l-lahi kadhiban wama nahnu lahu bimu'minina
qala rabbi unsur'ni bima kadhabuni
qala ʿamma qalilin layus'bihunna nadimina
fa-akhadhathumu l-sayhatu bil-haqi fajaʿalnahum ghuthaan fabuʿ'dan lil'qawmi l-zalimina
thumma anshana min baʿdihim qurunan akharina
ma tasbiqu min ummatin ajalaha wama yastakhiruna
thumma arsalna rusulana tatra kulla ma jaa ummatan rasuluha kadhabuhu fa-atbaʿna baʿdahum baʿdan wajaʿalnahum ahaditha fabuʿ'dan liqawmin la yu'minuna
thumma arsalna musa wa-akhahu haruna biayatina wasul'tanin mubinin
ila fir'ʿawna wamala-ihi fa-is'takbaru wakanu qawman ʿalina
faqalu anu'minu libasharayni mith'lina waqawmuhuma lana ʿabiduna
fakadhabuhuma fakanu mina l-muh'lakina
walaqad atayna musa l-kitaba laʿallahum yahtaduna
wajaʿalna ib'na maryama wa-ummahu ayatan waawaynahuma ila rabwatin dhati qararin wamaʿinin
yaayyuha l-rusulu kulu mina l-tayibati wa-iʿ'malu salihan inni bima taʿmaluna ʿalimun
wa-inna hadhihi ummatukum ummatan wahidatan wa-ana rabbukum fa-ittaquni
fataqattaʿu amrahum baynahum zuburan kullu hiz'bin bima ladayhim farihuna
fadharhum fi ghamratihim hatta hinin
ayahsabuna annama numidduhum bihi min malin wabanina
nusariʿu lahum fi l-khayrati bal la yashʿuruna
inna alladhina hum min khashyati rabbihim mush'fiquna
wa-alladhina hum biayati rabbihim yu'minuna
wa-alladhina hum birabbihim la yush'rikuna
wa-alladhina yu'tuna ma ataw waqulubuhum wajilatun annahum ila rabbihim rajiʿuna
ulaika yusariʿuna fi l-khayrati wahum laha sabiquna
wala nukallifu nafsan illa wus'ʿaha waladayna kitabun yantiqu bil-haqi wahum la yuz'lamuna
bal qulubuhum fi ghamratin min hadha walahum aʿmalun min duni dhalika hum laha ʿamiluna
hatta idha akhadhna mut'rafihim bil-ʿadhabi idha hum yajaruna
la tajaru l-yawma innakum minna la tunsaruna
qad kanat ayati tut'la ʿalaykum fakuntum ʿala aʿqabikum tankisuna
mus'takbirina bihi samiran tahjuruna
afalam yaddabbaru l-qawla am jaahum ma lam yati abaahumu l-awalina
am lam yaʿrifu rasulahum fahum lahu munkiruna
am yaquluna bihi jinnatun bal jaahum bil-haqi wa-aktharuhum lil'haqqi karihuna
walawi ittabaʿa l-haqu ahwaahum lafasadati l-samawatu wal-ardu waman fihinna bal ataynahum bidhik'rihim fahum ʿan dhik'rihim muʿ'riduna
am tasaluhum kharjan fakharaju rabbika khayrun wahuwa khayru l-raziqina
wa-innaka latadʿuhum ila siratin mus'taqimin
wa-inna alladhina la yu'minuna bil-akhirati ʿani l-sirati lanakibuna
walaw rahim'nahum wakashafna ma bihim min durrin lalajju fi tugh'yanihim yaʿmahuna
walaqad akhadhnahum bil-ʿadhabi fama is'takanu lirabbihim wama yatadarraʿuna
hatta idha fatahna ʿalayhim baban dha ʿadhabin shadidin idha hum fihi mub'lisuna
wahuwa alladhi ansha-a lakumu l-samʿa wal-absara wal-afidata qalilan ma tashkuruna
wahuwa alladhi dhara-akum fi l-ardi wa-ilayhi tuh'sharuna
wahuwa alladhi yuh'yi wayumitu walahu ikh'tilafu al-layli wal-nahari afala taʿqiluna
bal qalu mith'la ma qala l-awaluna
qalu a-idha mit'na wakunna turaban waʿizaman a-inna lamabʿuthuna
laqad wuʿid'na nahnu waabauna hadha min qablu in hadha illa asatiru l-awalina
qul limani l-ardu waman fiha in kuntum taʿlamuna
sayaquluna lillahi qul afala tadhakkaruna
qul man rabbu l-samawati l-sabʿi warabbu l-ʿarshi l-ʿazimi
sayaquluna lillahi qul afala tattaquna
qul man biyadihi malakutu kulli shayin wahuwa yujiru wala yujaru ʿalayhi in kuntum taʿlamuna
sayaquluna lillahi qul fa-anna tus'haruna
bal ataynahum bil-haqi wa-innahum lakadhibuna
ma ittakhadha l-lahu min waladin wama kana maʿahu min ilahin idhan ladhahaba kullu ilahin bima khalaqa walaʿala baʿduhum ʿala baʿdin sub'hana l-lahi ʿamma yasifuna
ʿalimi l-ghaybi wal-shahadati fataʿala ʿamma yush'rikuna
qul rabbi imma turiyanni ma yuʿaduna
rabbi fala tajʿalni fi l-qawmi l-zalimina
wa-inna ʿala an nuriyaka ma naʿiduhum laqadiruna
id'faʿ bi-allati hiya ahsanu l-sayi-ata nahnu aʿlamu bima yasifuna
waqul rabbi aʿudhu bika min hamazati l-shayatini
wa-aʿudhu bika rabbi an yahduruni
hatta idha jaa ahadahumu l-mawtu qala rabbi ir'jiʿuni
laʿalli aʿmalu salihan fima taraktu kalla innaha kalimatun huwa qailuha wamin waraihim barzakhun ila yawmi yub'ʿathuna
fa-idha nufikha fi l-suri fala ansaba baynahum yawma-idhin wala yatasaaluna
faman thaqulat mawazinuhu fa-ulaika humu l-muf'lihuna
waman khaffat mawazinuhu fa-ulaika alladhina khasiru anfusahum fi jahannama khaliduna
talfahu wujuhahumu l-naru wahum fiha kalihuna
alam takun ayati tut'la ʿalaykum fakuntum biha tukadhibuna
qalu rabbana ghalabat ʿalayna shiq'watuna wakunna qawman dallina
rabbana akhrij'na min'ha fa-in ʿud'na fa-inna zalimuna
qala ikh'sau fiha wala tukallimuni
innahu kana fariqun min ʿibadi yaquluna rabbana amanna fa-igh'fir lana wa-ir'hamna wa-anta khayru l-rahimina
fa-ittakhadhtumuhum sikh'riyyan hatta ansawkum dhik'ri wakuntum min'hum tadhakuna
inni jazaytuhumu l-yawma bima sabaru annahum humu l-faizuna
qala kam labith'tum fi l-ardi ʿadada sinina
qalu labith'na yawman aw baʿda yawmin fasali l-ʿadina
qala in labith'tum illa qalilan law annakum kuntum taʿlamuna
afahasib'tum annama khalaqnakum ʿabathan wa-annakum ilayna la tur'jaʿuna
fataʿala l-lahu l-maliku l-haqu la ilaha illa huwa rabbu l-ʿarshi l-karimi
waman yadʿu maʿa l-lahi ilahan akhara la bur'hana lahu bihi fa-innama hisabuhu ʿinda rabbihi innahu la yuf'lihu l-kafiruna
waqul rabbi igh'fir wa-ir'ham wa-anta khayru l-rahimina
suratun anzalnaha wafaradnaha wa-anzalna fiha ayatin bayyinatin laʿallakum tadhakkaruna
al-zaniyatu wal-zani fa-ij'lidu kulla wahidin min'huma mi-ata jaldatin wala takhudh'kum bihima rafatun fi dini l-lahi in kuntum tu'minuna bil-lahi wal-yawmi l-akhiri walyashhad ʿadhabahuma taifatun mina l-mu'minina
al-zani la yankihu illa zaniyatan aw mush'rikatan wal-zaniyatu la yankihuha illa zanin aw mush'rikun wahurrima dhalika ʿala l-mu'minina
wa-alladhina yarmuna l-muh'sanati thumma lam yatu bi-arbaʿati shuhadaa fa-ij'liduhum thamanina jaldatan wala taqbalu lahum shahadatan abadan wa-ulaika humu l-fasiquna
illa alladhina tabu min baʿdi dhalika wa-aslahu fa-inna l-laha ghafurun rahimun
wa-alladhina yarmuna azwajahum walam yakun lahum shuhadau illa anfusuhum fashahadatu ahadihim arbaʿu shahadatin bil-lahi innahu lamina l-sadiqina
wal-khamisatu anna laʿnata l-lahi ʿalayhi in kana mina l-kadhibina
wayadra-u ʿanha l-ʿadhaba an tashhada arbaʿa shahadatin bil-lahi innahu lamina l-kadhibina
wal-khamisata anna ghadaba l-lahi ʿalayha in kana mina l-sadiqina
walawla fadlu l-lahi ʿalaykum warahmatuhu wa-anna l-laha tawwabun hakimun
inna alladhina jau bil-if'ki ʿus'batun minkum la tahsabuhu sharran lakum bal huwa khayrun lakum likulli im'ri-in min'hum ma ik'tasaba mina l-ith'mi wa-alladhi tawalla kib'rahu min'hum lahu ʿadhabun ʿazimun
lawla idh samiʿ'tumuhu zanna l-mu'minuna wal-mu'minatu bi-anfusihim khayran waqalu hadha if'kun mubinun
lawla jau ʿalayhi bi-arbaʿati shuhadaa fa-idh lam yatu bil-shuhadai fa-ulaika ʿinda l-lahi humu l-kadhibuna
walawla fadlu l-lahi ʿalaykum warahmatuhu fi l-dun'ya wal-akhirati lamassakum fi ma afadtum fihi ʿadhabun ʿazimun
idh talaqqawnahu bi-alsinatikum wataquluna bi-afwahikum ma laysa lakum bihi ʿil'mun watahsabunahu hayyinan wahuwa ʿinda l-lahi ʿazimun
walawla idh samiʿ'tumuhu qul'tum ma yakunu lana an natakallama bihadha sub'hanaka hadha buh'tanun ʿazimun
yaʿizukumu l-lahu an taʿudu limith'lihi abadan in kuntum mu'minina
wayubayyinu l-lahu lakumu l-ayati wal-lahu ʿalimun hakimun
inna alladhina yuhibbuna an tashiʿa l-fahishatu fi alladhina amanu lahum ʿadhabun alimun fi l-dun'ya wal-akhirati wal-lahu yaʿlamu wa-antum la taʿlamuna
walawla fadlu l-lahi ʿalaykum warahmatuhu wa-anna l-laha raufun rahimun
yaayyuha alladhina amanu la tattabiʿu khutuwati l-shaytani waman yattabiʿ khutuwati l-shaytani fa-innahu yamuru bil-fahshai wal-munkari walawla fadlu l-lahi ʿalaykum warahmatuhu ma zaka minkum min ahadin abadan walakinna l-laha yuzakki man yashau wal-lahu samiʿun ʿalimun
wala yatali ulu l-fadli minkum wal-saʿati an yu'tu uli l-qur'ba wal-masakina wal-muhajirina fi sabili l-lahi walyaʿfu walyasfahu ala tuhibbuna an yaghfira l-lahu lakum wal-lahu ghafurun rahimun
inna alladhina yarmuna l-muh'sanati l-ghafilati l-mu'minati luʿinu fi l-dun'ya wal-akhirati walahum ʿadhabun ʿazimun
yawma tashhadu ʿalayhim alsinatuhum wa-aydihim wa-arjuluhum bima kanu yaʿmaluna
yawma-idhin yuwaffihimu l-lahu dinahumu l-haqa wayaʿlamuna anna l-laha huwa l-haqu l-mubinu
al-khabithatu lil'khabithina wal-khabithuna lil'khabithati wal-tayibatu lilttayyibina wal-tayibuna lilttayyibati ulaika mubarrauna mimma yaquluna lahum maghfiratun wariz'qun karimun
yaayyuha alladhina amanu la tadkhulu buyutan ghayra buyutikum hatta tastanisu watusallimu ʿala ahliha dhalikum khayrun lakum laʿallakum tadhakkaruna
fa-in lam tajidu fiha ahadan fala tadkhuluha hatta yu'dhana lakum wa-in qila lakumu ir'jiʿu fa-ir'jiʿu huwa azka lakum wal-lahu bima taʿmaluna ʿalimun
laysa ʿalaykum junahun an tadkhulu buyutan ghayra maskunatin fiha mataʿun lakum wal-lahu yaʿlamu ma tub'duna wama taktumuna
qul lil'mu'minina yaghuddu min absarihim wayahfazu furujahum dhalika azka lahum inna l-laha khabirun bima yasnaʿuna
waqul lil'mu'minati yaghdud'na min absarihinna wayahfazna furujahunna wala yub'dina zinatahunna illa ma zahara min'ha walyadrib'na bikhumurihinna ʿala juyubihinna wala yub'dina zinatahunna illa libuʿulatihinna aw abaihinna aw abai buʿulatihinna aw abnaihinna aw abnai buʿulatihinna aw ikh'wanihinna aw bani ikh'wanihinna aw bani akhawatihinna aw nisaihinna aw ma malakat aymanuhunna awi l-tabiʿina ghayri uli l-ir'bati mina l-rijali awi l-tif'li alladhina lam yazharu ʿala ʿawrati l-nisai wala yadrib'na bi-arjulihinna liyuʿ'lama ma yukh'fina min zinatihinna watubu ila l-lahi jamiʿan ayyuha l-mu'minuna laʿallakum tuf'lihuna
wa-ankihu l-ayama minkum wal-salihina min ʿibadikum wa-imaikum in yakunu fuqaraa yugh'nihimu l-lahu min fadlihi wal-lahu wasiʿun ʿalimun
walyastaʿfifi alladhina la yajiduna nikahan hatta yugh'niyahumu l-lahu min fadlihi wa-alladhina yabtaghuna l-kitaba mimma malakat aymanukum fakatibuhum in ʿalim'tum fihim khayran waatuhum min mali l-lahi alladhi atakum wala tuk'rihu fatayatikum ʿala l-bighai in aradna tahassunan litabtaghu ʿarada l-hayati l-dun'ya waman yuk'rihhunna fa-inna l-laha min baʿdi ik'rahihinna ghafurun rahimun
walaqad anzalna ilaykum ayatin mubayyinatin wamathalan mina alladhina khalaw min qablikum wamawʿizatan lil'muttaqina
al-lahu nuru l-samawati wal-ardi mathalu nurihi kamish'katin fiha mis'bahun l-mis'bahu fi zujajatin l-zujajatu ka-annaha kawkabun durriyyun yuqadu min shajaratin mubarakatin zaytunatin la sharqiyyatin wala gharbiyyatin yakadu zaytuha yudiu walaw lam tamsashu narun nurun ʿala nurin yahdi l-lahu linurihi man yashau wayadribu l-lahu l-amthala lilnnasi wal-lahu bikulli shayin ʿalimun
fi buyutin adhina l-lahu an tur'faʿa wayudh'kara fiha us'muhu yusabbihu lahu fiha bil-ghuduwi wal-asali
rijalun la tul'hihim tijaratun wala bayʿun ʿan dhik'ri l-lahi wa-iqami l-salati waitai l-zakati yakhafuna yawman tataqallabu fihi l-qulubu wal-absaru
liyajziyahumu l-lahu ahsana ma ʿamilu wayazidahum min fadlihi wal-lahu yarzuqu man yashau bighayri hisabin
wa-alladhina kafaru aʿmaluhum kasarabin biqiʿatin yahsabuhu l-zamanu maan hatta idha jaahu lam yajid'hu shayan wawajada l-laha ʿindahu fawaffahu hisabahu wal-lahu sariʿu l-hisabi
aw kazulumatin fi bahrin lujjiyyin yaghshahu mawjun min fawqihi mawjun min fawqihi sahabun zulumatun baʿduha fawqa baʿdin idha akhraja yadahu lam yakad yaraha waman lam yajʿali l-lahu lahu nuran fama lahu min nurin
alam tara anna l-laha yusabbihu lahu man fi l-samawati wal-ardi wal-tayru saffatin kullun qad ʿalima salatahu watasbihahu wal-lahu ʿalimun bima yafʿaluna
walillahi mul'ku l-samawati wal-ardi wa-ila l-lahi l-masiru
alam tara anna l-laha yuz'ji sahaban thumma yu-allifu baynahu thumma yajʿaluhu rukaman fatara l-wadqa yakhruju min khilalihi wayunazzilu mina l-samai min jibalin fiha min baradin fayusibu bihi man yashau wayasrifuhu ʿan man yashau yakadu sana barqihi yadhhabu bil-absari
yuqallibu l-lahu al-layla wal-nahara inna fi dhalika laʿib'ratan li-uli l-absari
wal-lahu khalaqa kulla dabbatin min main famin'hum man yamshi ʿala batnihi wamin'hum man yamshi ʿala rij'layni wamin'hum man yamshi ʿala arbaʿin yakhluqu l-lahu ma yashau inna l-laha ʿala kulli shayin qadirun
laqad anzalna ayatin mubayyinatin wal-lahu yahdi man yashau ila siratin mus'taqimin
wayaquluna amanna bil-lahi wabil-rasuli wa-ataʿna thumma yatawalla fariqun min'hum min baʿdi dhalika wama ulaika bil-mu'minina
wa-idha duʿu ila l-lahi warasulihi liyahkuma baynahum idha fariqun min'hum muʿ'riduna
wa-in yakun lahumu l-haqu yatu ilayhi mudh'ʿinina
afi qulubihim maradun ami ir'tabu am yakhafuna an yahifa l-lahu ʿalayhim warasuluhu bal ulaika humu l-zalimuna
innama kana qawla l-mu'minina idha duʿu ila l-lahi warasulihi liyahkuma baynahum an yaqulu samiʿ'na wa-ataʿna wa-ulaika humu l-muf'lihuna
waman yutiʿi l-laha warasulahu wayakhsha l-laha wayattaqhi fa-ulaika humu l-faizuna
wa-aqsamu bil-lahi jahda aymanihim la-in amartahum layakhrujunna qul la tuq'simu taʿatun maʿrufatun inna l-laha khabirun bima taʿmaluna
qul atiʿu l-laha wa-atiʿu l-rasula fa-in tawallaw fa-innama ʿalayhi ma hummila waʿalaykum ma hummil'tum wa-in tutiʿuhu tahtadu wama ʿala l-rasuli illa l-balaghu l-mubinu
waʿada l-lahu alladhina amanu minkum waʿamilu l-salihati layastakhlifannahum fi l-ardi kama is'takhlafa alladhina min qablihim walayumakkinanna lahum dinahumu alladhi ir'tada lahum walayubaddilannahum min baʿdi khawfihim amnan yaʿbudunani la yush'rikuna bi shayan waman kafara baʿda dhalika fa-ulaika humu l-fasiquna
wa-aqimu l-salata waatu l-zakata wa-atiʿu l-rasula laʿallakum tur'hamuna
la tahsabanna alladhina kafaru muʿ'jizina fi l-ardi wamawahumu l-naru walabi'sa l-masiru
yaayyuha alladhina amanu liyastadhinkumu alladhina malakat aymanukum wa-alladhina lam yablughu l-huluma minkum thalatha marratin min qabli salati l-fajri wahina tadaʿuna thiyabakum mina l-zahirati wamin baʿdi salati l-ʿishai thalathu ʿawratin lakum laysa ʿalaykum wala ʿalayhim junahun baʿdahunna tawwafuna ʿalaykum baʿdukum ʿala baʿdin kadhalika yubayyinu l-lahu lakumu l-ayati wal-lahu ʿalimun hakimun
wa-idha balagha l-atfalu minkumu l-huluma falyastadhinu kama is'tadhana alladhina min qablihim kadhalika yubayyinu l-lahu lakum ayatihi wal-lahu ʿalimun hakimun
wal-qawaʿidu mina l-nisai allati la yarjuna nikahan falaysa ʿalayhinna junahun an yadaʿna thiyabahunna ghayra mutabarrijatin bizinatin wa-an yastaʿfif'na khayrun lahunna wal-lahu samiʿun ʿalimun
laysa ʿala l-aʿma harajun wala ʿala l-aʿraji harajun wala ʿala l-maridi harajun wala ʿala anfusikum an takulu min buyutikum aw buyuti abaikum aw buyuti ummahatikum aw buyuti ikh'wanikum aw buyuti akhawatikum aw buyuti aʿmamikum aw buyuti ʿammatikum aw buyuti akhwalikum aw buyuti khalatikum aw ma malaktum mafatihahu aw sadiqikum laysa ʿalaykum junahun an takulu jamiʿan aw ashtatan fa-idha dakhaltum buyutan fasallimu ʿala anfusikum tahiyyatan min ʿindi l-lahi mubarakatan tayyibatan kadhalika yubayyinu l-lahu lakumu l-ayati laʿallakum taʿqiluna
innama l-mu'minuna alladhina amanu bil-lahi warasulihi wa-idha kanu maʿahu ʿala amrin jamiʿin lam yadhhabu hatta yastadhinuhu inna alladhina yastadhinunaka ulaika alladhina yu'minuna bil-lahi warasulihi fa-idha is'tadhanuka libaʿdi shanihim fadhan liman shi'ta min'hum wa-is'taghfir lahumu l-laha inna l-laha ghafurun rahimun
la tajʿalu duʿaa l-rasuli baynakum kaduʿai baʿdikum baʿdan qad yaʿlamu l-lahu alladhina yatasallaluna minkum liwadhan falyahdhari alladhina yukhalifuna ʿan amrihi an tusibahum fit'natun aw yusibahum ʿadhabun alimun
ala inna lillahi ma fi l-samawati wal-ardi qad yaʿlamu ma antum ʿalayhi wayawma yur'jaʿuna ilayhi fayunabbi-uhum bima ʿamilu wal-lahu bikulli shayin ʿalimun
tabaraka alladhi nazzala l-fur'qana ʿala ʿabdihi liyakuna lil'ʿalamina nadhiran
alladhi lahu mul'ku l-samawati wal-ardi walam yattakhidh waladan walam yakun lahu sharikun fi l-mul'ki wakhalaqa kulla shayin faqaddarahu taqdiran
wa-ittakhadhu min dunihi alihatan la yakhluquna shayan wahum yukh'laquna wala yamlikuna li-anfusihim darran wala nafʿan wala yamlikuna mawtan wala hayatan wala nushuran
waqala alladhina kafaru in hadha illa if'kun if'tarahu wa-aʿanahu ʿalayhi qawmun akharuna faqad jau zul'man wazuran
waqalu asatiru l-awalina ik'tatabaha fahiya tum'la ʿalayhi buk'ratan wa-asilan
qul anzalahu alladhi yaʿlamu l-sira fi l-samawati wal-ardi innahu kana ghafuran rahiman
waqalu mali hadha l-rasuli yakulu l-taʿama wayamshi fi l-aswaqi lawla unzila ilayhi malakun fayakuna maʿahu nadhiran
aw yul'qa ilayhi kanzun aw takunu lahu jannatun yakulu min'ha waqala l-zalimuna in tattabiʿuna illa rajulan mashuran
unzur kayfa darabu laka l-amthala fadallu fala yastatiʿuna sabilan
tabaraka alladhi in shaa jaʿala laka khayran min dhalika jannatin tajri min tahtiha l-anharu wayajʿal laka qusuran
bal kadhabu bil-saʿati wa-aʿtadna liman kadhaba bil-saʿati saʿiran
idha ra-athum min makanin baʿidin samiʿu laha taghayyuzan wazafiran
wa-idha ul'qu min'ha makanan dayyiqan muqarranina daʿaw hunalika thuburan
la tadʿu l-yawma thuburan wahidan wa-id'ʿu thuburan kathiran
qul adhalika khayrun am jannatu l-khul'di allati wuʿida l-mutaquna kanat lahum jazaan wamasiran
lahum fiha ma yashauna khalidina kana ʿala rabbika waʿdan masulan
wayawma yahshuruhum wama yaʿbuduna min duni l-lahi fayaqulu a-antum adlaltum ʿibadi haulai am hum dallu l-sabila
qalu sub'hanaka ma kana yanbaghi lana an nattakhidha min dunika min awliyaa walakin mattaʿtahum waabaahum hatta nasu l-dhik'ra wakanu qawman buran
faqad kadhabukum bima taquluna fama tastatiʿuna sarfan wala nasran waman yazlim minkum nudhiq'hu ʿadhaban kabiran
wama arsalna qablaka mina l-mur'salina illa innahum layakuluna l-taʿama wayamshuna fi l-aswaqi wajaʿalna baʿdakum libaʿdin fit'natan atasbiruna wakana rabbuka basiran
waqala alladhina la yarjuna liqaana lawla unzila ʿalayna l-malaikatu aw nara rabbana laqadi is'takbaru fi anfusihim waʿataw ʿutuwwan kabiran
yawma yarawna l-malaikata la bush'ra yawma-idhin lil'muj'rimina wayaquluna hij'ran mahjuran
waqadim'na ila ma ʿamilu min ʿamalin fajaʿalnahu habaan manthuran
ashabu l-janati yawma-idhin khayrun mus'taqarran wa-ahsanu maqilan
wayawma tashaqqaqu l-samau bil-ghamami wanuzzila l-malaikatu tanzilan
al-mul'ku yawma-idhin l-haqu lilrrahmani wakana yawman ʿala l-kafirina ʿasiran
wayawma yaʿaddu l-zalimu ʿala yadayhi yaqulu yalaytani ittakhadhtu maʿa l-rasuli sabilan
yawaylata laytani lam attakhidh fulanan khalilan
laqad adallani ʿani l-dhik'ri baʿda idh jaani wakana l-shaytanu lil'insani khadhulan
waqala l-rasulu yarabbi inna qawmi ittakhadhu hadha l-qur'ana mahjuran
wakadhalika jaʿalna likulli nabiyyin ʿaduwwan mina l-muj'rimina wakafa birabbika hadiyan wanasiran
waqala alladhina kafaru lawla nuzzila ʿalayhi l-qur'anu jum'latan wahidatan kadhalika linuthabbita bihi fuadaka warattalnahu tartilan
wala yatunaka bimathalin illa ji'naka bil-haqi wa-ahsana tafsiran
alladhina yuh'sharuna ʿala wujuhihim ila jahannama ulaika sharrun makanan wa-adallu sabilan
walaqad atayna musa l-kitaba wajaʿalna maʿahu akhahu haruna waziran
faqul'na idh'haba ila l-qawmi alladhina kadhabu biayatina fadammarnahum tadmiran
waqawma nuhin lamma kadhabu l-rusula aghraqnahum wajaʿalnahum lilnnasi ayatan wa-aʿtadna lilzzalimina ʿadhaban aliman
waʿadan wathamuda wa-ashaba l-rasi waqurunan bayna dhalika kathiran
wakullan darabna lahu l-amthala wakullan tabbarna tatbiran
walaqad ataw ʿala l-qaryati allati um'tirat matara l-sawi afalam yakunu yarawnaha bal kanu la yarjuna nushuran
wa-idha ra-awka in yattakhidhunaka illa huzuwan ahadha alladhi baʿatha l-lahu rasulan
in kada layudilluna ʿan alihatina lawla an sabarna ʿalayha wasawfa yaʿlamuna hina yarawna l-ʿadhaba man adallu sabilan
ara-ayta mani ittakhadha ilahahu hawahu afa-anta takunu ʿalayhi wakilan
am tahsabu anna aktharahum yasmaʿuna aw yaʿqiluna in hum illa kal-anʿami bal hum adallu sabilan
alam tara ila rabbika kayfa madda l-zila walaw shaa lajaʿalahu sakinan thumma jaʿalna l-shamsa ʿalayhi dalilan
thumma qabadnahu ilayna qabdan yasiran
wahuwa alladhi jaʿala lakumu al-layla libasan wal-nawma subatan wajaʿala l-nahara nushuran
wahuwa alladhi arsala l-riyaha bush'ran bayna yaday rahmatihi wa-anzalna mina l-samai maan tahuran
linuh'yiya bihi baldatan maytan wanus'qiyahu mimma khalaqna anʿaman wa-anasiyya kathiran
walaqad sarrafnahu baynahum liyadhakkaru fa-aba aktharu l-nasi illa kufuran
walaw shi'na labaʿathna fi kulli qaryatin nadhiran
fala tutiʿi l-kafirina wajahid'hum bihi jihadan kabiran
wahuwa alladhi maraja l-bahrayni hadha ʿadhbun furatun wahadha mil'hun ujajun wajaʿala baynahuma barzakhan wahij'ran mahjuran
wahuwa alladhi khalaqa mina l-mai basharan fajaʿalahu nasaban wasih'ran wakana rabbuka qadiran
wayaʿbuduna min duni l-lahi ma la yanfaʿuhum wala yadurruhum wakana l-kafiru ʿala rabbihi zahiran
wama arsalnaka illa mubashiran wanadhiran
qul ma asalukum ʿalayhi min ajrin illa man shaa an yattakhidha ila rabbihi sabilan
watawakkal ʿala l-hayi alladhi la yamutu wasabbih bihamdihi wakafa bihi bidhunubi ʿibadihi khabiran
alladhi khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda wama baynahuma fi sittati ayyamin thumma is'tawa ʿala l-ʿarshi l-rahmanu fasal bihi khabiran
wa-idha qila lahumu us'judu lilrrahmani qalu wama l-rahmanu anasjudu lima tamuruna wazadahum nufuran
tabaraka alladhi jaʿala fi l-samai burujan wajaʿala fiha sirajan waqamaran muniran
wahuwa alladhi jaʿala al-layla wal-nahara khil'fatan liman arada an yadhakkara aw arada shukuran
waʿibadu l-rahmani alladhina yamshuna ʿala l-ardi hawnan wa-idha khatabahumu l-jahiluna qalu salaman
wa-alladhina yabituna lirabbihim sujjadan waqiyaman
wa-alladhina yaquluna rabbana is'rif ʿanna ʿadhaba jahannama inna ʿadhabaha kana gharaman
innaha saat mus'taqarran wamuqaman
wa-alladhina idha anfaqu lam yus'rifu walam yaqturu wakana bayna dhalika qawaman
wa-alladhina la yadʿuna maʿa l-lahi ilahan akhara wala yaqtuluna l-nafsa allati harrama l-lahu illa bil-haqi wala yaznuna waman yafʿal dhalika yalqa athaman
yudaʿaf lahu l-ʿadhabu yawma l-qiyamati wayakhlud fihi muhanan
illa man taba waamana waʿamila ʿamalan salihan fa-ulaika yubaddilu l-lahu sayyiatihim hasanatin wakana l-lahu ghafuran rahiman
waman taba waʿamila salihan fa-innahu yatubu ila l-lahi mataban
wa-alladhina la yashhaduna l-zura wa-idha marru bil-laghwi marru kiraman
wa-alladhina idha dhukkiru biayati rabbihim lam yakhirru ʿalayha summan waʿum'yanan
wa-alladhina yaquluna rabbana hab lana min azwajina wadhurriyyatina qurrata aʿyunin wa-ij'ʿalna lil'muttaqina imaman
ulaika yuj'zawna l-ghur'fata bima sabaru wayulaqqawna fiha tahiyyatan wasalaman
khalidina fiha hasunat mus'taqarran wamuqaman
qul ma yaʿba-u bikum rabbi lawla duʿaukum faqad kadhabtum fasawfa yakunu lizaman
tta-seen-meem
til'ka ayatu l-kitabi l-mubini
laʿallaka bakhiʿun nafsaka alla yakunu mu'minina
in nasha nunazzil ʿalayhim mina l-samai ayatan fazallat aʿnaquhum laha khadiʿina
wama yatihim min dhik'rin mina l-rahmani muh'dathin illa kanu ʿanhu muʿ'ridina
faqad kadhabu fasayatihim anbau ma kanu bihi yastahziuna
awalam yaraw ila l-ardi kam anbatna fiha min kulli zawjin karimin
inna fi dhalika laayatan wama kana aktharuhum mu'minina
wa-inna rabbaka lahuwa l-ʿazizu l-rahimu
wa-idh nada rabbuka musa ani i'ti l-qawma l-zalimina
qawma fir'ʿawna ala yattaquna
qala rabbi inni akhafu an yukadhibuni
wayadiqu sadri wala yantaliqu lisani fa-arsil ila haruna
walahum ʿalayya dhanbun fa-akhafu an yaqtuluni
qala kalla fa-idh'haba biayatina inna maʿakum mus'tamiʿuna
fatiya fir'ʿawna faqula inna rasulu rabbi l-ʿalamina
an arsil maʿana bani is'raila
qala alam nurabbika fina walidan walabith'ta fina min ʿumurika sinina
wafaʿalta faʿlataka allati faʿalta wa-anta mina l-kafirina
qala faʿaltuha idhan wa-ana mina l-dalina
fafarartu minkum lamma khif'tukum fawahaba li rabbi huk'man wajaʿalani mina l-mur'salina
watil'ka niʿ'matun tamunnuha ʿalayya an ʿabbadtta bani is'raila
qala fir'ʿawnu wama rabbu l-ʿalamina
qala rabbu l-samawati wal-ardi wama baynahuma in kuntum muqinina
qala liman hawlahu ala tastamiʿuna
qala rabbukum warabbu abaikumu l-awalina
qala inna rasulakumu alladhi ur'sila ilaykum lamajnunun
qala rabbu l-mashriqi wal-maghribi wama baynahuma in kuntum taʿqiluna
qala la-ini ittakhadhta ilahan ghayri la-ajʿalannaka mina l-masjunina
qala awalaw ji'tuka bishayin mubinin
qala fati bihi in kunta mina l-sadiqina
fa-alqa ʿasahu fa-idha hiya thuʿ'banun mubinun
wanazaʿa yadahu fa-idha hiya baydau lilnnazirina
qala lil'mala-i hawlahu inna hadha lasahirun ʿalimun
yuridu an yukh'rijakum min ardikum bisih'rihi famadha tamuruna
qalu arjih wa-akhahu wa-ib'ʿath fi l-madaini hashirina
yatuka bikulli sahharin ʿalimin
fajumiʿa l-saharatu limiqati yawmin maʿlumin
waqila lilnnasi hal antum muj'tamiʿuna
laʿallana nattabiʿu l-saharata in kanu humu l-ghalibina
falamma jaa l-saharatu qalu lifir'ʿawna a-inna lana la-ajran in kunna nahnu l-ghalibina
qala naʿam wa-innakum idhan lamina l-muqarabina
qala lahum musa alqu ma antum mul'quna
fa-alqaw hibalahum waʿisiyyahum waqalu biʿizzati fir'ʿawna inna lanahnu l-ghalibuna
fa-alqa musa ʿasahu fa-idha hiya talqafu ma yafikuna
fa-ul'qiya l-saharatu sajidina
qalu amanna birabbi l-ʿalamina
rabbi musa waharuna
qala amantum lahu qabla an adhana lakum innahu lakabirukumu alladhi ʿallamakumu l-sih'ra falasawfa taʿlamuna la-uqattiʿanna aydiyakum wa-arjulakum min khilafin wala-usallibannakum ajmaʿina
qalu la dayra inna ila rabbina munqalibuna
inna natmaʿu an yaghfira lana rabbuna khatayana an kunna awwala l-mu'minina
wa-awhayna ila musa an asri biʿibadi innakum muttabaʿuna
fa-arsala fir'ʿawnu fi l-madaini hashirina
inna haulai lashir'dhimatun qaliluna
wa-innahum lana laghaizuna
wa-inna lajamiʿun hadhiruna
fa-akhrajnahum min jannatin waʿuyunin
wakunuzin wamaqamin karimin
kadhalika wa-awrathnaha bani is'raila
fa-atbaʿuhum mush'riqina
falamma taraa l-jamʿani qala ashabu musa inna lamud'rakuna
qala kalla inna maʿiya rabbi sayahdini
fa-awhayna ila musa ani id'rib biʿasaka l-bahra fa-infalaqa fakana kullu fir'qin kal-tawdi l-ʿazimi
wa-azlafna thamma l-akharina
wa-anjayna musa waman maʿahu ajmaʿina
thumma aghraqna l-akharina

wa-ut'lu ʿalayhim naba-a ib'rahima

qalu naʿbudu asnaman fanazallu laha ʿakifina

antum waabaukumu l-aqdamuna

wa-alladhi yumituni thumma yuh'yini
wa-alladhi atmaʿu an yaghfira li khatiati yawma l-dini

wa-igh'fir li-abi innahu kana mina l-dalina

yawma la yanfaʿu malun wala banuna

wa-annahum yaquluna ma la yafʿaluna
illa alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati wadhakaru l-laha kathiran wa-intasaru min baʿdi ma zulimu wasayaʿlamu alladhina zalamu ayya munqalabin yanqalibuna
tta-seen til'ka ayatu l-qur'ani wakitabin mubinin
hudan wabush'ra lil'mu'minina
alladhina yuqimuna l-salata wayu'tuna l-zakata wahum bil-akhirati hum yuqinuna
inna alladhina la yu'minuna bil-akhirati zayyanna lahum aʿmalahum fahum yaʿmahuna
ulaika alladhina lahum suu l-ʿadhabi wahum fi l-akhirati humu l-akhsaruna
wa-innaka latulaqqa l-qur'ana min ladun hakimin ʿalimin
idh qala musa li-ahlihi inni anastu naran saatikum min'ha bikhabarin aw atikum bishihabin qabasin laʿallakum tastaluna
falamma jaaha nudiya an burika man fi l-nari waman hawlaha wasub'hana l-lahi rabbi l-ʿalamina
yamusa innahu ana l-lahu l-ʿazizu l-hakimu
wa-alqi ʿasaka falamma raaha tahtazzu ka-annaha jannun walla mud'biran walam yuʿaqqib yamusa la takhaf inni la yakhafu ladayya l-mur'saluna
illa man zalama thumma baddala hus'nan baʿda suin fa-inni ghafurun rahimun
wa-adkhil yadaka fi jaybika takhruj baydaa min ghayri suin fi tis'ʿi ayatin ila fir'ʿawna waqawmihi innahum kanu qawman fasiqina
falamma jaathum ayatuna mub'siratan qalu hadha sih'run mubinun
wajahadu biha wa-is'tayqanatha anfusuhum zul'man waʿuluwwan fa-unzur kayfa kana ʿaqibatu l-muf'sidina
walaqad atayna dawuda wasulaymana ʿil'man waqala l-hamdu lillahi alladhi faddalana ʿala kathirin min ʿibadihi l-mu'minina
wawaritha sulaymanu dawuda waqala yaayyuha l-nasu ʿullim'na mantiqa l-tayri wautina min kulli shayin inna hadha lahuwa l-fadlu l-mubinu
wahushira lisulaymana junuduhu mina l-jini wal-insi wal-tayri fahum yuzaʿuna
hatta idha ataw ʿala wadi l-namli qalat namlatun yaayyuha l-namlu ud'khulu masakinakum la yahtimannakum sulaymanu wajunuduhu wahum la yashʿuruna
fatabassama dahikan min qawliha waqala rabbi awziʿ'ni an ashkura niʿ'mataka allati anʿamta ʿalayya waʿala walidayya wa-an aʿmala salihan tardahu wa-adkhil'ni birahmatika fi ʿibadika l-salihina
watafaqqada l-tayra faqala ma liya la ara l-hud'huda am kana mina l-ghaibina
la-uʿadhibannahu ʿadhaban shadidan aw laadh'bahannahu aw layatiyanni bisul'tanin mubinin
famakatha ghayra baʿidin faqala ahattu bima lam tuhit bihi waji'tuka min saba-in binaba-in yaqinin
inni wajadttu im'ra-atan tamlikuhum wautiyat min kulli shayin walaha ʿarshun ʿazimun
wajadttuha waqawmaha yasjuduna lilshamsi min duni l-lahi wazayyana lahumu l-shaytanu aʿmalahum fasaddahum ʿani l-sabili fahum la yahtaduna
alla yasjudu lillahi alladhi yukh'riju l-khaba-a fi l-samawati wal-ardi wayaʿlamu ma tukh'funa wama tuʿ'linuna
al-lahu la ilaha illa huwa rabbu l-ʿarshi l-ʿazimi
qala sananzuru asadaqta am kunta mina l-kadhibina
idh'hab bikitabi hadha fa-alqih ilayhim thumma tawalla ʿanhum fa-unzur madha yarjiʿuna
qalat yaayyuha l-mala-u inni ul'qiya ilayya kitabun karimun
innahu min sulaymana wa-innahu bis'mi l-lahi l-rahmani l-rahimi
alla taʿlu ʿalayya watuni mus'limina
qalat yaayyuha l-mala-u aftuni fi amri ma kuntu qatiʿatan amran hatta tashhaduni
qalu nahnu ulu quwwatin wa-ulu basin shadidin wal-amru ilayki fa-unzuri madha tamurina
qalat inna l-muluka idha dakhalu qaryatan afsaduha wajaʿalu aʿizzata ahliha adhillatan wakadhalika yafʿaluna
wa-inni mur'silatun ilayhim bihadiyyatin fanaziratun bima yarjiʿu l-mur'saluna
falamma jaa sulaymana qala atumiddunani bimalin fama ataniya l-lahu khayrun mimma atakum bal antum bihadiyyatikum tafrahuna
ir'jiʿ ilayhim falanatiyannahum bijunudin la qibala lahum biha walanukh'rijannahum min'ha adhillatan wahum saghiruna
qala yaayyuha l-mala-u ayyukum yatini biʿarshiha qabla an yatuni mus'limina
qala ʿif'ritun mina l-jini ana atika bihi qabla an taquma min maqamika wa-inni ʿalayhi laqawiyyun aminun
qala alladhi ʿindahu ʿil'mun mina l-kitabi ana atika bihi qabla an yartadda ilayka tarfuka falamma raahu mus'taqirran ʿindahu qala hadha min fadli rabbi liyabluwani a-ashkuru am akfuru waman shakara fa-innama yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fa-inna rabbi ghaniyyun karimun
qala nakkiru laha ʿarshaha nanzur atahtadi am takunu mina alladhina la yahtaduna
falamma jaat qila ahakadha ʿarshuki qalat ka-annahu huwa wautina l-ʿil'ma min qabliha wakunna mus'limina
wasaddaha ma kanat taʿbudu min duni l-lahi innaha kanat min qawmin kafirina
qila laha ud'khuli l-sarha falamma ra-athu hasibathu lujjatan wakashafat ʿan saqayha qala innahu sarhun mumarradun min qawarira qalat rabbi inni zalamtu nafsi wa-aslamtu maʿa sulaymana lillahi rabbi l-ʿalamina
walaqad arsalna ila thamuda akhahum salihan ani uʿ'budu l-laha fa-idha hum fariqani yakhtasimuna
qala yaqawmi lima tastaʿjiluna bil-sayi-ati qabla l-hasanati lawla tastaghfiruna l-laha laʿallakum tur'hamuna
qalu ittayyarna bika wabiman maʿaka qala tairukum ʿinda l-lahi bal antum qawmun tuf'tanuna
wakana fi l-madinati tis'ʿatu rahtin yuf'siduna fi l-ardi wala yus'lihuna
qalu taqasamu bil-lahi lanubayyitannahu wa-ahlahu thumma lanaqulanna liwaliyyihi ma shahid'na mahlika ahlihi wa-inna lasadiquna
wamakaru makran wamakarna makran wahum la yashʿuruna
fa-unzur kayfa kana ʿaqibatu makrihim anna dammarnahum waqawmahum ajmaʿina
fatil'ka buyutuhum khawiyatan bima zalamu inna fi dhalika laayatan liqawmin yaʿlamuna
wa-anjayna alladhina amanu wakanu yattaquna
walutan idh qala liqawmihi atatuna l-fahishata wa-antum tub'siruna
a-innakum latatuna l-rijala shahwatan min duni l-nisai bal antum qawmun tajhaluna
fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qalu akhriju ala lutin min qaryatikum innahum unasun yatatahharuna
fa-anjaynahu wa-ahlahu illa im'ra-atahu qaddarnaha mina l-ghabirina
wa-amtarna ʿalayhim mataran fasaa mataru l-mundharina
quli l-hamdu lillahi wasalamun ʿala ʿibadihi alladhina is'tafa allahu khayrun amma yush'rikuna
amman khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda wa-anzala lakum mina l-samai maan fa-anbatna bihi hadaiqa dhata bahjatin ma kana lakum an tunbitu shajaraha a-ilahun maʿa l-lahi bal hum qawmun yaʿdiluna
amman jaʿala l-arda qararan wajaʿala khilalaha anharan wajaʿala laha rawasiya wajaʿala bayna l-bahrayni hajizan a-ilahun maʿa l-lahi bal aktharuhum la yaʿlamuna
amman yujibu l-mud'tara idha daʿahu wayakshifu l-sua wayajʿalukum khulafaa l-ardi a-ilahun maʿa l-lahi qalilan ma tadhakkaruna
amman yahdikum fi zulumati l-bari wal-bahri waman yur'silu l-riyaha bush'ran bayna yaday rahmatihi a-ilahun maʿa l-lahi taʿala l-lahu ʿamma yush'rikuna
amman yabda-u l-khalqa thumma yuʿiduhu waman yarzuqukum mina l-samai wal-ardi a-ilahun maʿa l-lahi qul hatu bur'hanakum in kuntum sadiqina
qul la yaʿlamu man fi l-samawati wal-ardi l-ghayba illa l-lahu wama yashʿuruna ayyana yub'ʿathuna
bali iddaraka ʿil'muhum fi l-akhirati bal hum fi shakkin min'ha bal hum min'ha ʿamuna
waqala alladhina kafaru a-idha kunna turaban waabauna a-inna lamukh'rajuna
laqad wuʿid'na hadha nahnu waabauna min qablu in hadha illa asatiru l-awalina
qul siru fi l-ardi fa-unzuru kayfa kana ʿaqibatu l-muj'rimina
wala tahzan ʿalayhim wala takun fi dayqin mimma yamkuruna
wayaquluna mata hadha l-waʿdu in kuntum sadiqina
qul ʿasa an yakuna radifa lakum baʿdu alladhi tastaʿjiluna
wa-inna rabbaka ladhu fadlin ʿala l-nasi walakinna aktharahum la yashkuruna
wa-inna rabbaka layaʿlamu ma tukinnu suduruhum wama yuʿ'linuna
wama min ghaibatin fi l-samai wal-ardi illa fi kitabin mubinin
inna hadha l-qur'ana yaqussu ʿala bani is'raila akthara alladhi hum fihi yakhtalifuna
wa-innahu lahudan warahmatun lil'mu'minina
inna rabbaka yaqdi baynahum bihuk'mihi wahuwa l-ʿazizu l-ʿalimu
fatawakkal ʿala l-lahi innaka ʿala l-haqi l-mubini
innaka la tus'miʿu l-mawta wala tus'miʿu l-suma l-duʿaa idha wallaw mud'birina
wama anta bihadi l-ʿum'yi ʿan dalalatihim in tus'miʿu illa man yu'minu biayatina fahum mus'limuna
wa-idha waqaʿa l-qawlu ʿalayhim akhrajna lahum dabbatan mina l-ardi tukallimuhum anna l-nasa kanu biayatina la yuqinuna
wayawma nahshuru min kulli ummatin fawjan mimman yukadhibu biayatina fahum yuzaʿuna
hatta idha jau qala akadhabtum biayati walam tuhitu biha ʿil'man ammadha kuntum taʿmaluna
wawaqaʿa l-qawlu ʿalayhim bima zalamu fahum la yantiquna
alam yaraw anna jaʿalna al-layla liyaskunu fihi wal-nahara mub'siran inna fi dhalika laayatin liqawmin yu'minuna
wayawma yunfakhu fi l-suri fafaziʿa man fi l-samawati waman fi l-ardi illa man shaa l-lahu wakullun atawhu dakhirina
watara l-jibala tahsabuha jamidatan wahiya tamurru marra l-sahabi sun'ʿa l-lahi alladhi atqana kulla shayin innahu khabirun bima tafʿaluna
man jaa bil-hasanati falahu khayrun min'ha wahum min fazaʿin yawma-idhin aminuna
waman jaa bil-sayi-ati fakubbat wujuhuhum fi l-nari hal tuj'zawna illa ma kuntum taʿmaluna
innama umir'tu an aʿbuda rabba hadhihi l-baldati alladhi harramaha walahu kullu shayin wa-umir'tu an akuna mina l-mus'limina
wa-an atluwa l-qur'ana famani ih'tada fa-innama yahtadi linafsihi waman dalla faqul innama ana mina l-mundhirina
waquli l-hamdu lillahi sayurikum ayatihi fataʿrifunaha wama rabbuka bighafilin ʿamma taʿmaluna
tta-seen-meem
til'ka ayatu l-kitabi l-mubini
natlu ʿalayka min naba-i musa wafir'ʿawna bil-haqi liqawmin yu'minuna
inna fir'ʿawna ʿala fi l-ardi wajaʿala ahlaha shiyaʿan yastadʿifu taifatan min'hum yudhabbihu abnaahum wayastahyi nisaahum innahu kana mina l-muf'sidina
wanuridu an namunna ʿala alladhina us'tud'ʿifu fi l-ardi wanajʿalahum a-immatan wanajʿalahumu l-warithina
wanumakkina lahum fi l-ardi wanuriya fir'ʿawna wahamana wajunudahuma min'hum ma kanu yahdharuna
wa-awhayna ila ummi musa an ardiʿihi fa-idha khif'ti ʿalayhi fa-alqihi fi l-yami wala takhafi wala tahzani inna radduhu ilayki wajaʿiluhu mina l-mur'salina
fal-taqatahu alu fir'ʿawna liyakuna lahum ʿaduwwan wahazanan inna fir'ʿawna wahamana wajunudahuma kanu khatiina
waqalati im'ra-atu fir'ʿawna qurratu ʿaynin li walaka la taqtuluhu ʿasa an yanfaʿana aw nattakhidhahu waladan wahum la yashʿuruna
wa-asbaha fuadu ummi musa farighan in kadat latub'di bihi lawla an rabatna ʿala qalbiha litakuna mina l-mu'minina
waqalat li-ukh'tihi qussihi fabasurat bihi ʿan junubin wahum la yashʿuruna
waharramna ʿalayhi l-maradiʿa min qablu faqalat hal adullukum ʿala ahli baytin yakfulunahu lakum wahum lahu nasihuna
faradadnahu ila ummihi kay taqarra ʿaynuha wala tahzana walitaʿlama anna waʿda l-lahi haqqun walakinna aktharahum la yaʿlamuna
walamma balagha ashuddahu wa-is'tawa ataynahu huk'man waʿil'man wakadhalika najzi l-muh'sinina
wadakhala l-madinata ʿala hini ghaflatin min ahliha fawajada fiha rajulayni yaqtatilani hadha min shiʿatihi wahadha min ʿaduwwihi fa-is'taghathahu alladhi min shiʿatihi ʿala alladhi min ʿaduwwihi fawakazahu musa faqada ʿalayhi qala hadha min ʿamali l-shaytani innahu ʿaduwwun mudillun mubinun
qala rabbi inni zalamtu nafsi fa-igh'fir li faghafara lahu innahu huwa l-ghafuru l-rahimu
qala rabbi bima anʿamta ʿalayya falan akuna zahiran lil'muj'rimina
fa-asbaha fi l-madinati khaifan yataraqqabu fa-idha alladhi is'tansarahu bil-amsi yastasrikhuhu qala lahu musa innaka laghawiyyun mubinun
falamma an arada an yabtisha bi-alladhi huwa ʿaduwwun lahuma qala yamusa aturidu an taqtulani kama qatalta nafsan bil-amsi in turidu illa an takuna jabbaran fi l-ardi wama turidu an takuna mina l-mus'lihina
wajaa rajulun min aqsa l-madinati yasʿa qala yamusa inna l-mala-a yatamiruna bika liyaqtuluka fa-ukh'ruj inni laka mina l-nasihina
fakharaja min'ha khaifan yataraqqabu qala rabbi najjini mina l-qawmi l-zalimina
walamma tawajjaha til'qaa madyana qala ʿasa rabbi an yahdiyani sawaa l-sabili
walamma warada maa madyana wajada ʿalayhi ummatan mina l-nasi yasquna wawajada min dunihimu im'ra-atayni tadhudani qala ma khatbukuma qalata la nasqi hatta yus'dira l-riʿau wa-abuna shaykhun kabirun
fasaqa lahuma thumma tawalla ila l-zili faqala rabbi inni lima anzalta ilayya min khayrin faqirun
fajaathu ih'dahuma tamshi ʿala is'tih'yain qalat inna abi yadʿuka liyajziyaka ajra ma saqayta lana falamma jaahu waqassa ʿalayhi l-qasasa qala la takhaf najawta mina l-qawmi l-zalimina
qalat ih'dahuma yaabati is'tajir'hu inna khayra mani is'tajarta l-qawiyu l-aminu
qala inni uridu an unkihaka ih'da ib'natayya hatayni ʿala an tajurani thamaniya hijajin fa-in atmamta ʿashran famin ʿindika wama uridu an ashuqqa ʿalayka satajiduni in shaa l-lahu mina l-salihina
qala dhalika bayni wabaynaka ayyama l-ajalayni qadaytu fala ʿud'wana ʿalayya wal-lahu ʿala ma naqulu wakilun
falamma qada musa l-ajala wasara bi-ahlihi anasa min janibi l-turi naran qala li-ahlihi um'kuthu inni anastu naran laʿalli atikum min'ha bikhabarin aw jadhwatin mina l-nari laʿallakum tastaluna
falamma ataha nudiya min shati-i l-wadi l-aymani fi l-buq'ʿati l-mubarakati mina l-shajarati an yamusa inni ana l-lahu rabbu l-ʿalamina
wa-an alqi ʿasaka falamma raaha tahtazzu ka-annaha jannun walla mud'biran walam yuʿaqqib yamusa aqbil wala takhaf innaka mina l-aminina
us'luk yadaka fi jaybika takhruj baydaa min ghayri suin wa-ud'mum ilayka janahaka mina l-rahbi fadhanika bur'hanani min rabbika ila fir'ʿawna wamala-ihi innahum kanu qawman fasiqina
qala rabbi inni qataltu min'hum nafsan fa-akhafu an yaqtuluni
wa-akhi harunu huwa afsahu minni lisanan fa-arsil'hu maʿiya rid'an yusaddiquni inni akhafu an yukadhibuni
qala sanashuddu ʿadudaka bi-akhika wanajʿalu lakuma sul'tanan fala yasiluna ilaykuma biayatina antuma wamani ittabaʿakuma l-ghalibuna
falamma jaahum musa biayatina bayyinatin qalu ma hadha illa sih'run muf'taran wama samiʿ'na bihadha fi abaina l-awalina
waqala musa rabbi aʿlamu biman jaa bil-huda min ʿindihi waman takunu lahu ʿaqibatu l-dari innahu la yuf'lihu l-zalimuna
waqala fir'ʿawnu yaayyuha l-mala-u ma ʿalim'tu lakum min ilahin ghayri fa-awqid li yahamanu ʿala l-tini fa-ij'ʿal li sarhan laʿalli attaliʿu ila ilahi musa wa-inni la-azunnuhu mina l-kadhibina
wa-is'takbara huwa wajunuduhu fi l-ardi bighayri l-haqi wazannu annahum ilayna la yur'jaʿuna
fa-akhadhnahu wajunudahu fanabadhnahum fi l-yami fa-unzur kayfa kana ʿaqibatu l-zalimina
wajaʿalnahum a-immatan yadʿuna ila l-nari wayawma l-qiyamati la yunsaruna
wa-atbaʿnahum fi hadhihi l-dun'ya laʿnatan wayawma l-qiyamati hum mina l-maqbuhina
walaqad atayna musa l-kitaba min baʿdi ma ahlakna l-quruna l-ula basaira lilnnasi wahudan warahmatan laʿallahum yatadhakkaruna
wama kunta bijanibi l-gharbiyi idh qadayna ila musa l-amra wama kunta mina l-shahidina
walakinna anshana qurunan fatatawala ʿalayhimu l-ʿumuru wama kunta thawiyan fi ahli madyana tatlu ʿalayhim ayatina walakinna kunna mur'silina
wama kunta bijanibi l-turi idh nadayna walakin rahmatan min rabbika litundhira qawman ma atahum min nadhirin min qablika laʿallahum yatadhakkaruna
walawla an tusibahum musibatun bima qaddamat aydihim fayaqulu rabbana lawla arsalta ilayna rasulan fanattabiʿa ayatika wanakuna mina l-mu'minina
falamma jaahumu l-haqu min ʿindina qalu lawla utiya mith'la ma utiya musa awalam yakfuru bima utiya musa min qablu qalu sih'rani tazahara waqalu inna bikullin kafiruna
qul fatu bikitabin min ʿindi l-lahi huwa ahda min'huma attabiʿ'hu in kuntum sadiqina
fa-in lam yastajibu laka fa-iʿ'lam annama yattabiʿuna ahwaahum waman adallu mimmani ittabaʿa hawahu bighayri hudan mina l-lahi inna l-laha la yahdi l-qawma l-zalimina
walaqad wassalna lahumu l-qawla laʿallahum yatadhakkaruna
alladhina ataynahumu l-kitaba min qablihi hum bihi yu'minuna
wa-idha yut'la ʿalayhim qalu amanna bihi innahu l-haqu min rabbina inna kunna min qablihi mus'limina
ulaika yu'tawna ajrahum marratayni bima sabaru wayadrauna bil-hasanati l-sayi-ata wamimma razaqnahum yunfiquna
wa-idha samiʿu l-laghwa aʿradu ʿanhu waqalu lana aʿmaluna walakum aʿmalukum salamun ʿalaykum la nabtaghi l-jahilina
innaka la tahdi man ahbabta walakinna l-laha yahdi man yashau wahuwa aʿlamu bil-muh'tadina
waqalu in nattabiʿi l-huda maʿaka nutakhattaf min ardina awalam numakkin lahum haraman aminan yuj'ba ilayhi thamaratu kulli shayin riz'qan min ladunna walakinna aktharahum la yaʿlamuna
wakam ahlakna min qaryatin batirat maʿishataha fatil'ka masakinuhum lam tus'kan min baʿdihim illa qalilan wakunna nahnu l-warithina
wama kana rabbuka muh'lika l-qura hatta yabʿatha fi ummiha rasulan yatlu ʿalayhim ayatina wama kunna muh'liki l-qura illa wa-ahluha zalimuna
wama utitum min shayin famataʿu l-hayati l-dun'ya wazinatuha wama ʿinda l-lahi khayrun wa-abqa afala taʿqiluna
afaman waʿadnahu waʿdan hasanan fahuwa laqihi kaman mattaʿnahu mataʿa l-hayati l-dun'ya thumma huwa yawma l-qiyamati mina l-muh'darina
wayawma yunadihim fayaqulu ayna shurakaiya alladhina kuntum tazʿumuna
qala alladhina haqqa ʿalayhimu l-qawlu rabbana haulai alladhina aghwayna aghwaynahum kama ghawayna tabarrana ilayka ma kanu iyyana yaʿbuduna
waqila id'ʿu shurakaakum fadaʿawhum falam yastajibu lahum wara-awu l-ʿadhaba law annahum kanu yahtaduna
wayawma yunadihim fayaqulu madha ajabtumu l-mur'salina
faʿamiyat ʿalayhimu l-anbau yawma-idhin fahum la yatasaaluna
fa-amma man taba waamana waʿamila salihan faʿasa an yakuna mina l-muf'lihina
warabbuka yakhluqu ma yashau wayakhtaru ma kana lahumu l-khiyaratu sub'hana l-lahi wataʿala ʿamma yush'rikuna
warabbuka yaʿlamu ma tukinnu suduruhum wama yuʿ'linuna
wahuwa l-lahu la ilaha illa huwa lahu l-hamdu fi l-ula wal-akhirati walahu l-huk'mu wa-ilayhi tur'jaʿuna
qul ara-aytum in jaʿala l-lahu ʿalaykumu al-layla sarmadan ila yawmi l-qiyamati man ilahun ghayru l-lahi yatikum bidiyain afala tasmaʿuna
qul ara-aytum in jaʿala l-lahu ʿalaykumu l-nahara sarmadan ila yawmi l-qiyamati man ilahun ghayru l-lahi yatikum bilaylin taskununa fihi afala tub'siruna
wamin rahmatihi jaʿala lakumu al-layla wal-nahara litaskunu fihi walitabtaghu min fadlihi walaʿallakum tashkuruna
wayawma yunadihim fayaqulu ayna shurakaiya alladhina kuntum tazʿumuna
wanazaʿna min kulli ummatin shahidan faqul'na hatu bur'hanakum faʿalimu anna l-haqa lillahi wadalla ʿanhum ma kanu yaftaruna
inna qaruna kana min qawmi musa fabagha ʿalayhim waataynahu mina l-kunuzi ma inna mafatihahu latanuu bil-ʿus'bati uli l-quwati idh qala lahu qawmuhu la tafrah inna l-laha la yuhibbu l-farihina
wa-ib'taghi fima ataka l-lahu l-dara l-akhirata wala tansa nasibaka mina l-dun'ya wa-ahsin kama ahsana l-lahu ilayka wala tabghi l-fasada fi l-ardi inna l-laha la yuhibbu l-muf'sidina
qala innama utituhu ʿala ʿil'min ʿindi awalam yaʿlam anna l-laha qad ahlaka min qablihi mina l-quruni man huwa ashaddu min'hu quwwatan wa-aktharu jamʿan wala yus'alu ʿan dhunubihimu l-muj'rimuna
fakharaja ʿala qawmihi fi zinatihi qala alladhina yuriduna l-hayata l-dun'ya yalayta lana mith'la ma utiya qarunu innahu ladhu hazzin ʿazimin
waqala alladhina utu l-ʿil'ma waylakum thawabu l-lahi khayrun liman amana waʿamila salihan wala yulaqqaha illa l-sabiruna
fakhasafna bihi wabidarihi l-arda fama kana lahu min fi-atin yansurunahu min duni l-lahi wama kana mina l-muntasirina
wa-asbaha alladhina tamannaw makanahu bil-amsi yaquluna wayka-anna l-laha yabsutu l-riz'qa liman yashau min ʿibadihi wayaqdiru lawla an manna l-lahu ʿalayna lakhasafa bina wayka-annahu la yuf'lihu l-kafiruna
til'ka l-daru l-akhiratu najʿaluha lilladhina la yuriduna ʿuluwwan fi l-ardi wala fasadan wal-ʿaqibatu lil'muttaqina
man jaa bil-hasanati falahu khayrun min'ha waman jaa bil-sayi-ati fala yuj'za alladhina ʿamilu l-sayiati illa ma kanu yaʿmaluna
inna alladhi farada ʿalayka l-qur'ana laradduka ila maʿadin qul rabbi aʿlamu man jaa bil-huda waman huwa fi dalalin mubinin
wama kunta tarju an yul'qa ilayka l-kitabu illa rahmatan min rabbika fala takunanna zahiran lil'kafirina
wala yasuddunnaka ʿan ayati l-lahi baʿda idh unzilat ilayka wa-ud'ʿu ila rabbika wala takunanna mina l-mush'rikina
wala tadʿu maʿa l-lahi ilahan akhara la ilaha illa huwa kullu shayin halikun illa wajhahu lahu l-huk'mu wa-ilayhi tur'jaʿuna
alif-lam-meem
ahasiba l-nasu an yut'raku an yaqulu amanna wahum la yuf'tanuna
walaqad fatanna alladhina min qablihim falayaʿlamanna l-lahu alladhina sadaqu walayaʿlamanna l-kadhibina
am hasiba alladhina yaʿmaluna l-sayiati an yasbiquna saa ma yahkumuna
man kana yarju liqaa l-lahi fa-inna ajala l-lahi laatin wahuwa l-samiʿu l-ʿalimu
waman jahada fa-innama yujahidu linafsihi inna l-laha laghaniyyun ʿani l-ʿalamina
wa-alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati lanukaffiranna ʿanhum sayyiatihim walanajziyannahum ahsana alladhi kanu yaʿmaluna
wawassayna l-insana biwalidayhi hus'nan wa-in jahadaka litush'rika bi ma laysa laka bihi ʿil'mun fala tutiʿ'huma ilayya marjiʿukum fa-unabbi-ukum bima kuntum taʿmaluna
wa-alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati lanud'khilannahum fi l-salihina
wamina l-nasi man yaqulu amanna bil-lahi fa-idha udhiya fi l-lahi jaʿala fit'nata l-nasi kaʿadhabi l-lahi wala-in jaa nasrun min rabbika layaqulunna inna kunna maʿakum awalaysa l-lahu bi-aʿlama bima fi suduri l-ʿalamina
walayaʿlamanna l-lahu alladhina amanu walayaʿlamanna l-munafiqina
waqala alladhina kafaru lilladhina amanu ittabiʿu sabilana walnahmil khatayakum wama hum bihamilina min khatayahum min shayin innahum lakadhibuna
walayahmilunna athqalahum wa-athqalan maʿa athqalihim walayus'alunna yawma l-qiyamati ʿamma kanu yaftaruna
walaqad arsalna nuhan ila qawmihi falabitha fihim alfa sanatin illa khamsina ʿaman fa-akhadhahumu l-tufanu wahum zalimuna
fa-anjaynahu wa-ashaba l-safinati wajaʿalnaha ayatan lil'ʿalamina
wa-ib'rahima idh qala liqawmihi uʿ'budu l-laha wa-ittaquhu dhalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum taʿlamuna
innama taʿbuduna min duni l-lahi awthanan watakhluquna if'kan inna alladhina taʿbuduna min duni l-lahi la yamlikuna lakum riz'qan fa-ib'taghu ʿinda l-lahi l-riz'qa wa-uʿ'buduhu wa-ush'kuru lahu ilayhi tur'jaʿuna
wa-in tukadhibu faqad kadhaba umamun min qablikum wama ʿala l-rasuli illa l-balaghu l-mubinu
awalam yaraw kayfa yub'di-u l-lahu l-khalqa thumma yuʿiduhu inna dhalika ʿala l-lahi yasirun
qul siru fi l-ardi fa-unzuru kayfa bada-a l-khalqa thumma l-lahu yunshi-u l-nashata l-akhirata inna l-laha ʿala kulli shayin qadirun
yuʿadhibu man yashau wayarhamu man yashau wa-ilayhi tuq'labuna
wama antum bimuʿ'jizina fi l-ardi wala fi l-samai wama lakum min duni l-lahi min waliyyin wala nasirin
wa-alladhina kafaru biayati l-lahi waliqaihi ulaika ya-isu min rahmati wa-ulaika lahum ʿadhabun alimun
fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qalu uq'tuluhu aw harriquhu fa-anjahu l-lahu mina l-nari inna fi dhalika laayatin liqawmin yu'minuna
waqala innama ittakhadhtum min duni l-lahi awthanan mawaddata baynikum fi l-hayati l-dun'ya thumma yawma l-qiyamati yakfuru baʿdukum bibaʿdin wayalʿanu baʿdukum baʿdan wamawakumu l-naru wama lakum min nasirina
faamana lahu lutun waqala inni muhajirun ila rabbi innahu huwa l-ʿazizu l-hakimu
wawahabna lahu is'haqa wayaʿquba wajaʿalna fi dhurriyyatihi l-nubuwata wal-kitaba waataynahu ajrahu fi l-dun'ya wa-innahu fi l-akhirati lamina l-salihina
walutan idh qala liqawmihi innakum latatuna l-fahishata ma sabaqakum biha min ahadin mina l-ʿalamina
a-innakum latatuna l-rijala wataqtaʿuna l-sabila watatuna fi nadikumu l-munkara fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qalu i'tina biʿadhabi l-lahi in kunta mina l-sadiqina
qala rabbi unsur'ni ʿala l-qawmi l-muf'sidina
walamma jaat rusuluna ib'rahima bil-bush'ra qalu inna muh'liku ahli hadhihi l-qaryati inna ahlaha kanu zalimina
qala inna fiha lutan qalu nahnu aʿlamu biman fiha lanunajjiyannahu wa-ahlahu illa im'ra-atahu kanat mina l-ghabirina
walamma an jaat rusuluna lutan sia bihim wadaqa bihim dharʿan waqalu la takhaf wala tahzan inna munajjuka wa-ahlaka illa im'ra-ataka kanat mina l-ghabirina
inna munziluna ʿala ahli hadhihi l-qaryati rij'zan mina l-samai bima kanu yafsuquna
walaqad tarakna min'ha ayatan bayyinatan liqawmin yaʿqiluna
wa-ila madyana akhahum shuʿayban faqala yaqawmi uʿ'budu l-laha wa-ir'ju l-yawma l-akhira wala taʿthaw fi l-ardi muf'sidina
fakadhabuhu fa-akhadhathumu l-rajfatu fa-asbahu fi darihim jathimina
waʿadan wathamuda waqad tabayyana lakum min masakinihim wazayyana lahumu l-shaytanu aʿmalahum fasaddahum ʿani l-sabili wakanu mus'tabsirina
waqaruna wafir'ʿawna wahamana walaqad jaahum musa bil-bayinati fa-is'takbaru fi l-ardi wama kanu sabiqina
fakullan akhadhna bidhanbihi famin'hum man arsalna ʿalayhi hasiban wamin'hum man akhadhathu l-sayhatu wamin'hum man khasafna bihi l-arda wamin'hum man aghraqna wama kana l-lahu liyazlimahum walakin kanu anfusahum yazlimuna
mathalu alladhina ittakhadhu min duni l-lahi awliyaa kamathali l-ʿankabuti ittakhadhat baytan wa-inna awhana l-buyuti labaytu l-ʿankabuti law kanu yaʿlamuna
inna l-laha yaʿlamu ma yadʿuna min dunihi min shayin wahuwa l-ʿazizu l-hakimu
watil'ka l-amthalu nadribuha lilnnasi wama yaʿqiluha illa l-ʿalimuna
khalaqa l-lahu l-samawati wal-arda bil-haqi inna fi dhalika laayatan lil'mu'minina
ut'lu ma uhiya ilayka mina l-kitabi wa-aqimi l-salata inna l-salata tanha ʿani l-fahshai wal-munkari waladhik'ru l-lahi akbaru wal-lahu yaʿlamu ma tasnaʿuna
wala tujadilu ahla l-kitabi illa bi-allati hiya ahsanu illa alladhina zalamu min'hum waqulu amanna bi-alladhi unzila ilayna wa-unzila ilaykum wa-ilahuna wa-ilahukum wahidun wanahnu lahu mus'limuna
wakadhalika anzalna ilayka l-kitaba fa-alladhina ataynahumu l-kitaba yu'minuna bihi wamin haulai man yu'minu bihi wama yajhadu biayatina illa l-kafiruna
wama kunta tatlu min qablihi min kitabin wala takhuttuhu biyaminika idhan la-ir'taba l-mub'tiluna
bal huwa ayatun bayyinatun fi suduri alladhina utu l-ʿil'ma wama yajhadu biayatina illa l-zalimuna
waqalu lawla unzila ʿalayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul innama l-ayatu ʿinda l-lahi wa-innama ana nadhirun mubinun
awalam yakfihim anna anzalna ʿalayka l-kitaba yut'la ʿalayhim inna fi dhalika larahmatan wadhik'ra liqawmin yu'minuna
qul kafa bil-lahi bayni wabaynakum shahidan yaʿlamu ma fi l-samawati wal-ardi wa-alladhina amanu bil-batili wakafaru bil-lahi ulaika humu l-khasiruna
wayastaʿjilunaka bil-ʿadhabi walawla ajalun musamman lajaahumu l-ʿadhabu walayatiyannahum baghtatan wahum la yashʿuruna
yastaʿjilunaka bil-ʿadhabi wa-inna jahannama lamuhitatun bil-kafirina
yawma yaghshahumu l-ʿadhabu min fawqihim wamin tahti arjulihim wayaqulu dhuqu ma kuntum taʿmaluna
yaʿibadiya alladhina amanu inna ardi wasiʿatun fa-iyyaya fa-uʿ'buduni
kullu nafsin dhaiqatu l-mawti thumma ilayna tur'jaʿuna
wa-alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati lanubawwi-annahum mina l-janati ghurafan tajri min tahtiha l-anharu khalidina fiha niʿ'ma ajru l-ʿamilina
alladhina sabaru waʿala rabbihim yatawakkaluna
waka-ayyin min dabbatin la tahmilu riz'qaha l-lahu yarzuquha wa-iyyakum wahuwa l-samiʿu l-ʿalimu
wala-in sa-altahum man khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda wasakhara l-shamsa wal-qamara layaqulunna l-lahu fa-anna yu'fakuna
al-lahu yabsutu l-riz'qa liman yashau min ʿibadihi wayaqdiru lahu inna l-laha bikulli shayin ʿalimun
wala-in sa-altahum man nazzala mina l-samai maan fa-ahya bihi l-arda min baʿdi mawtiha layaqulunna l-lahu quli l-hamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la yaʿqiluna
wama hadhihi l-hayatu l-dun'ya illa lahwun walaʿibun wa-inna l-dara l-akhirata lahiya l-hayawanu law kanu yaʿlamuna
fa-idha rakibu fi l-ful'ki daʿawu l-laha mukh'lisina lahu l-dina falamma najjahum ila l-bari idha hum yush'rikuna

ghulibati l-rumu

awalam yasiru fi l-ardi fayanzuru kayfa kana ʿaqibatu alladhina min qablihim kanu ashadda min'hum quwwatan wa-atharu l-arda waʿamaruha akthara mimma ʿamaruha wajaathum rusuluhum bil-bayinati fama kana l-lahu liyazlimahum walakin kanu anfusahum yazlimuna

wamin ayatihi an khalaqakum min turabin thumma idha antum basharun tantashiruna

wamin ayatihi khalqu l-samawati wal-ardi wa-ikh'tilafu alsinatikum wa-alwanikum inna fi dhalika laayatin lil'ʿalimina

wamin ayatihi an taquma l-samau wal-ardu bi-amrihi thumma idha daʿakum daʿwatan mina l-ardi idha antum takhrujuna
walahu man fi l-samawati wal-ardi kullun lahu qanituna

daraba lakum mathalan min anfusikum hal lakum min ma malakat aymanukum min shurakaa fi ma razaqnakum fa-antum fihi sawaon takhafunahum kakhifatikum anfusakum kadhalika nufassilu l-ayati liqawmin yaʿqiluna

awalam yaraw anna l-laha yabsutu l-riz'qa liman yashau wayaqdiru inna fi dhalika laayatin liqawmin yu'minuna

walaqad arsalna min qablika rusulan ila qawmihim fajauhum bil-bayinati fa-intaqamna mina alladhina ajramu wakana haqqan ʿalayna nasru l-mu'minina

wala-in arsalna rihan fara-awhu mus'farran lazallu min baʿdihi yakfuruna

wa-in jahadaka ʿala an tush'rika bi ma laysa laka bihi ʿil'mun fala tutiʿ'huma wasahib'huma fi l-dun'ya maʿrufan wa-ittabiʿ sabila man anaba ilayya thumma ilayya marjiʿukum fa-unabbi-ukum bima kuntum taʿmaluna

yabunayya aqimi l-salata wamur bil-maʿrufi wa-in'ha ʿani l-munkari wa-is'bir ʿala ma asabaka inna dhalika min ʿazmi l-umuri

alam taraw anna l-laha sakhara lakum ma fi l-samawati wama fi l-ardi wa-asbagha ʿalaykum niʿamahu zahiratan wabatinatan wamina l-nasi man yujadilu fi l-lahi bighayri ʿil'min wala hudan wala kitabin munirin
wa-idha qila lahumu ittabiʿu ma anzala l-lahu qalu bal nattabiʿu ma wajadna ʿalayhi abaana awalaw kana l-shaytanu yadʿuhum ila ʿadhabi l-saʿiri

ma khalqukum wala baʿthukum illa kanafsin wahidatin inna l-laha samiʿun basirun
alam tara anna l-laha yuliju al-layla fi l-nahari wayuliju l-nahara fi al-layli wasakhara l-shamsa wal-qamara kullun yajri ila ajalin musamman wa-anna l-laha bima taʿmaluna khabirun

alam tara anna l-ful'ka tajri fi l-bahri biniʿ'mati l-lahi liyuriyakum min ayatihi inna fi dhalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakurin
