aftara ʿala l-lahi kadhiban am bihi jinnatun bali alladhina la yu'minuna bil-akhirati fi l-ʿadhabi wal-dalali l-baʿidi
afalam yaraw ila ma bayna aydihim wama khalfahum mina l-samai wal-ardi in nasha nakhsif bihimu l-arda aw nus'qit ʿalayhim kisafan mina l-samai inna fi dhalika laayatan likulli ʿabdin munibin
walaqad atayna dawuda minna fadlan yajibalu awwibi maʿahu wal-tayra wa-alanna lahu l-hadida
ani iʿ'mal sabighatin waqaddir fi l-sardi wa-iʿ'malu salihan inni bima taʿmaluna basirun
walisulaymana l-riha ghuduwwuha shahrun warawahuha shahrun wa-asalna lahu ʿayna l-qit'ri wamina l-jini man yaʿmalu bayna yadayhi bi-idh'ni rabbihi waman yazigh min'hum ʿan amrina nudhiq'hu min ʿadhabi l-saʿiri
yaʿmaluna lahu ma yashau min mahariba watamathila wajifanin kal-jawabi waqudurin rasiyatin iʿ'malu ala dawuda shuk'ran waqalilun min ʿibadiya l-shakuru
falamma qadayna ʿalayhi l-mawta ma dallahum ʿala mawtihi illa dabbatu l-ardi takulu minsa-atahu falamma kharra tabayyanati l-jinu an law kanu yaʿlamuna l-ghayba ma labithu fi l-ʿadhabi l-muhini
laqad kana lisaba-in fi maskanihim ayatun jannatani ʿan yaminin washimalin kulu min riz'qi rabbikum wa-ush'kuru lahu baldatun tayyibatun warabbun ghafurun
fa-aʿradu fa-arsalna ʿalayhim sayla l-ʿarimi wabaddalnahum bijannatayhim jannatayni dhawatay ukulin khamtin wa-athlin washayin min sid'rin qalilin
dhalika jazaynahum bima kafaru wahal nujazi illa l-kafura
wajaʿalna baynahum wabayna l-qura allati barakna fiha quran zahiratan waqaddarna fiha l-sayra siru fiha layaliya wa-ayyaman aminina
faqalu rabbana baʿid bayna asfarina wazalamu anfusahum fajaʿalnahum ahaditha wamazzaqnahum kulla mumazzaqin inna fi dhalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakurin
walaqad saddaqa ʿalayhim ib'lisu zannahu fa-ittabaʿuhu illa fariqan mina l-mu'minina
wama kana lahu ʿalayhim min sul'tanin illa linaʿlama man yu'minu bil-akhirati mimman huwa min'ha fi shakkin warabbuka ʿala kulli shayin hafizun
quli id'ʿu alladhina zaʿamtum min duni l-lahi la yamlikuna mith'qala dharratin fi l-samawati wala fi l-ardi wama lahum fihima min shir'kin wama lahu min'hum min zahirin
wala tanfaʿu l-shafaʿatu ʿindahu illa liman adhina lahu hatta idha fuzziʿa ʿan qulubihim qalu madha qala rabbukum qalu l-haqa wahuwa l-ʿaliyu l-kabiru
qul man yarzuqukum mina l-samawati wal-ardi quli l-lahu wa-inna aw iyyakum laʿala hudan aw fi dalalin mubinin
qul la tus'aluna ʿamma ajramna wala nus'alu ʿamma taʿmaluna
qul yajmaʿu baynana rabbuna thumma yaftahu baynana bil-haqi wahuwa l-fatahu l-ʿalimu
qul aruniya alladhina alhaqtum bihi shurakaa kalla bal huwa l-lahu l-ʿazizu l-hakimu
wama arsalnaka illa kaffatan lilnnasi bashiran wanadhiran walakinna akthara l-nasi la yaʿlamuna
wayaquluna mata hadha l-waʿdu in kuntum sadiqina
qul lakum miʿadu yawmin la tastakhiruna ʿanhu saʿatan wala tastaqdimuna
waqala alladhina kafaru lan nu'mina bihadha l-qur'ani wala bi-alladhi bayna yadayhi walaw tara idhi l-zalimuna mawqufuna ʿinda rabbihim yarjiʿu baʿduhum ila baʿdin l-qawla yaqulu alladhina us'tud'ʿifu lilladhina is'takbaru lawla antum lakunna mu'minina
qala alladhina is'takbaru lilladhina us'tud'ʿifu anahnu sadadnakum ʿani l-huda baʿda idh jaakum bal kuntum muj'rimina
waqala alladhina us'tud'ʿifu lilladhina is'takbaru bal makru al-layli wal-nahari idh tamurunana an nakfura bil-lahi wanajʿala lahu andadan wa-asarru l-nadamata lamma ra-awu l-ʿadhaba wajaʿalna l-aghlala fi aʿnaqi alladhina kafaru hal yuj'zawna illa ma kanu yaʿmaluna
wama arsalna fi qaryatin min nadhirin illa qala mut'rafuha inna bima ur'sil'tum bihi kafiruna
waqalu nahnu aktharu amwalan wa-awladan wama nahnu bimuʿadhabina
qul inna rabbi yabsutu l-riz'qa liman yashau wayaqdiru walakinna akthara l-nasi la yaʿlamuna
wama amwalukum wala awladukum bi-allati tuqarribukum ʿindana zul'fa illa man amana waʿamila salihan fa-ulaika lahum jazau l-diʿ'fi bima ʿamilu wahum fi l-ghurufati aminuna
wa-alladhina yasʿawna fi ayatina muʿajizina ulaika fi l-ʿadhabi muh'daruna
qul inna rabbi yabsutu l-riz'qa liman yashau min ʿibadihi wayaqdiru lahu wama anfaqtum min shayin fahuwa yukh'lifuhu wahuwa khayru l-raziqina
wayawma yahshuruhum jamiʿan thumma yaqulu lil'malaikati ahaulai iyyakum kanu yaʿbuduna
qalu sub'hanaka anta waliyyuna min dunihim bal kanu yaʿbuduna l-jina aktharuhum bihim mu'minuna
fal-yawma la yamliku baʿdukum libaʿdin nafʿan wala darran wanaqulu lilladhina zalamu dhuqu ʿadhaba l-nari allati kuntum biha tukadhibuna
wa-idha tut'la ʿalayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qalu ma hadha illa rajulun yuridu an yasuddakum ʿamma kana yaʿbudu abaukum waqalu ma hadha illa if'kun muf'taran waqala alladhina kafaru lil'haqqi lamma jaahum in hadha illa sih'run mubinun
wama ataynahum min kutubin yadrusunaha wama arsalna ilayhim qablaka min nadhirin
wakadhaba alladhina min qablihim wama balaghu miʿ'shara ma ataynahum fakadhabu rusuli fakayfa kana nakiri
qul innama aʿizukum biwahidatin an taqumu lillahi mathna wafurada thumma tatafakkaru ma bisahibikum min jinnatin in huwa illa nadhirun lakum bayna yaday ʿadhabin shadidin
qul ma sa-altukum min ajrin fahuwa lakum in ajriya illa ʿala l-lahi wahuwa ʿala kulli shayin shahidun
qul inna rabbi yaqdhifu bil-haqi ʿallamu l-ghuyubi
qul jaa l-haqu wama yub'di-u l-batilu wama yuʿidu
qul in dalaltu fa-innama adillu ʿala nafsi wa-ini ih'tadaytu fabima yuhi ilayya rabbi innahu samiʿun qaribun
walaw tara idh faziʿu fala fawta wa-ukhidhu min makanin qaribin
waqalu amanna bihi wa-anna lahumu l-tanawushu min makanin baʿidin
waqad kafaru bihi min qablu wayaqdhifuna bil-ghaybi min makanin baʿidin
wahila baynahum wabayna ma yashtahuna kama fuʿila bi-ashyaʿihim min qablu innahum kanu fi shakkin muribin
al-hamdu lillahi fatiri l-samawati wal-ardi jaʿili l-malaikati rusulan uli ajnihatin mathna wathulatha warubaʿa yazidu fi l-khalqi ma yashau inna l-laha ʿala kulli shayin qadirun
ma yaftahi l-lahu lilnnasi min rahmatin fala mum'sika laha wama yum'sik fala mur'sila lahu min baʿdihi wahuwa l-ʿazizu l-hakimu
yaayyuha l-nasu udh'kuru niʿ'mata l-lahi ʿalaykum hal min khaliqin ghayru l-lahi yarzuqukum mina l-samai wal-ardi la ilaha illa huwa fa-anna tu'fakuna
wa-in yukadhibuka faqad kudhibat rusulun min qablika wa-ila l-lahi tur'jaʿu l-umuru
yaayyuha l-nasu inna waʿda l-lahi haqqun fala taghurrannakumu l-hayatu l-dun'ya wala yaghurrannakum bil-lahi l-gharuru
inna l-shaytana lakum ʿaduwwun fa-ittakhidhuhu ʿaduwwan innama yadʿu hiz'bahu liyakunu min ashabi l-saʿiri
alladhina kafaru lahum ʿadhabun shadidun wa-alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati lahum maghfiratun wa-ajrun kabirun
afaman zuyyina lahu suu ʿamalihi faraahu hasanan fa-inna l-laha yudillu man yashau wayahdi man yashau fala tadhhab nafsuka ʿalayhim hasaratin inna l-laha ʿalimun bima yasnaʿuna
wal-lahu alladhi arsala l-riyaha fatuthiru sahaban fasuq'nahu ila baladin mayyitin fa-ahyayna bihi l-arda baʿda mawtiha kadhalika l-nushuru
man kana yuridu l-ʿizata falillahi l-ʿizatu jamiʿan ilayhi yasʿadu l-kalimu l-tayibu wal-ʿamalu l-salihu yarfaʿuhu wa-alladhina yamkuruna l-sayiati lahum ʿadhabun shadidun wamakru ulaika huwa yaburu
wal-lahu khalaqakum min turabin thumma min nut'fatin thumma jaʿalakum azwajan wama tahmilu min untha wala tadaʿu illa biʿil'mihi wama yuʿammaru min muʿammarin wala yunqasu min ʿumurihi illa fi kitabin inna dhalika ʿala l-lahi yasirun
wama yastawi l-bahrani hadha ʿadhbun furatun saighun sharabuhu wahadha mil'hun ujajun wamin kullin takuluna lahman tariyyan watastakhrijuna hil'yatan talbasunaha watara l-ful'ka fihi mawakhira litabtaghu min fadlihi walaʿallakum tashkuruna
yuliju al-layla fi l-nahari wayuliju l-nahara fi al-layli wasakhara l-shamsa wal-qamara kullun yajri li-ajalin musamman dhalikumu l-lahu rabbukum lahu l-mul'ku wa-alladhina tadʿuna min dunihi ma yamlikuna min qit'mirin
in tadʿuhum la yasmaʿu duʿaakum walaw samiʿu ma is'tajabu lakum wayawma l-qiyamati yakfuruna bishir'kikum wala yunabbi-uka mith'lu khabirin
yaayyuha l-nasu antumu l-fuqarau ila l-lahi wal-lahu huwa l-ghaniyu l-hamidu
in yasha yudh'hib'kum wayati bikhalqin jadidin
wama dhalika ʿala l-lahi biʿazizin
wala taziru waziratun wiz'ra ukh'ra wa-in tadʿu muth'qalatun ila him'liha la yuh'mal min'hu shayon walaw kana dha qur'ba innama tundhiru alladhina yakhshawna rabbahum bil-ghaybi wa-aqamu l-salata waman tazakka fa-innama yatazakka linafsihi wa-ila l-lahi l-masiru
wama yastawi l-aʿma wal-basiru
wala l-zulumatu wala l-nuru
wala l-zilu wala l-haruru
wama yastawi l-ahyau wala l-amwatu inna l-laha yus'miʿu man yashau wama anta bimus'miʿin man fi l-quburi
in anta illa nadhirun
inna arsalnaka bil-haqi bashiran wanadhiran wa-in min ummatin illa khala fiha nadhirun
wa-in yukadhibuka faqad kadhaba alladhina min qablihim jaathum rusuluhum bil-bayinati wabil-zuburi wabil-kitabi l-muniri
thumma akhadhtu alladhina kafaru fakayfa kana nakiri
alam tara anna l-laha anzala mina l-samai maan fa-akhrajna bihi thamaratin mukh'talifan alwanuha wamina l-jibali judadun bidun wahum'run mukh'talifun alwanuha wagharabibu sudun
wamina l-nasi wal-dawabi wal-anʿami mukh'talifun alwanuhu kadhalika innama yakhsha l-laha min ʿibadihi l-ʿulamau inna l-laha ʿazizun ghafurun
inna alladhina yatluna kitaba l-lahi wa-aqamu l-salata wa-anfaqu mimma razaqnahum sirran waʿalaniyatan yarjuna tijaratan lan tabura
liyuwaffiyahum ujurahum wayazidahum min fadlihi innahu ghafurun shakurun
wa-alladhi awhayna ilayka mina l-kitabi huwa l-haqu musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi inna l-laha biʿibadihi lakhabirun basirun
thumma awrathna l-kitaba alladhina is'tafayna min ʿibadina famin'hum zalimun linafsihi wamin'hum muq'tasidun wamin'hum sabiqun bil-khayrati bi-idh'ni l-lahi dhalika huwa l-fadlu l-kabiru
jannatu ʿadnin yadkhulunaha yuhallawna fiha min asawira min dhahabin walu'lu-an walibasuhum fiha harirun
waqalu l-hamdu lillahi alladhi adhhaba ʿanna l-hazana inna rabbana laghafurun shakurun
alladhi ahallana dara l-muqamati min fadlihi la yamassuna fiha nasabun wala yamassuna fiha lughubun
wa-alladhina kafaru lahum naru jahannama la yuq'da ʿalayhim fayamutu wala yukhaffafu ʿanhum min ʿadhabiha kadhalika najzi kulla kafurin
wahum yastarikhuna fiha rabbana akhrij'na naʿmal salihan ghayra alladhi kunna naʿmalu awalam nuʿammir'kum ma yatadhakkaru fihi man tadhakkara wajaakumu l-nadhiru fadhuqu fama lilzzalimina min nasirin
inna l-laha ʿalimu ghaybi l-samawati wal-ardi innahu ʿalimun bidhati l-suduri
huwa alladhi jaʿalakum khalaifa fi l-ardi faman kafara faʿalayhi kuf'ruhu wala yazidu l-kafirina kuf'ruhum ʿinda rabbihim illa maqtan wala yazidu l-kafirina kuf'ruhum illa khasaran
qul ara-aytum shurakaakumu alladhina tadʿuna min duni l-lahi aruni madha khalaqu mina l-ardi am lahum shir'kun fi l-samawati am ataynahum kitaban fahum ʿala bayyinatin min'hu bal in yaʿidu l-zalimuna baʿduhum baʿdan illa ghururan
inna l-laha yum'siku l-samawati wal-arda an tazula wala-in zalata in amsakahuma min ahadin min baʿdihi innahu kana haliman ghafuran
wa-aqsamu bil-lahi jahda aymanihim la-in jaahum nadhirun layakununna ahda min ih'da l-umami falamma jaahum nadhirun ma zadahum illa nufuran
is'tik'baran fi l-ardi wamakra l-sayi-i wala yahiqu l-makru l-sayi-u illa bi-ahlihi fahal yanzuruna illa sunnata l-awalina falan tajida lisunnati l-lahi tabdilan walan tajida lisunnati l-lahi tahwilan
awalam yasiru fi l-ardi fayanzuru kayfa kana ʿaqibatu alladhina min qablihim wakanu ashadda min'hum quwwatan wama kana l-lahu liyuʿ'jizahu min shayin fi l-samawati wala fi l-ardi innahu kana ʿaliman qadiran
walaw yuakhidhu l-lahu l-nasa bima kasabu ma taraka ʿala zahriha min dabbatin walakin yu-akhiruhum ila ajalin musamman fa-idha jaa ajaluhum fa-inna l-laha kana biʿibadihi basiran

wajaʿalna min bayni aydihim saddan wamin khalfihim saddan fa-aghshaynahum fahum la yub'siruna
wasawaon ʿalayhim a-andhartahum am lam tundhir'hum la yu'minuna
innama tundhiru mani ittabaʿa l-dhik'ra wakhashiya l-rahmana bil-ghaybi fabashir'hu bimaghfiratin wa-ajrin karimin
inna nahnu nuh'yi l-mawta wanaktubu ma qaddamu waatharahum wakulla shayin ahsaynahu fi imamin mubinin
wa-id'rib lahum mathalan ashaba l-qaryati idh jaaha l-mur'saluna
idh arsalna ilayhimu ith'nayni fakadhabuhuma faʿazzazna bithalithin faqalu inna ilaykum mur'saluna
qalu ma antum illa basharun mith'luna wama anzala l-rahmanu min shayin in antum illa takdhibuna
qalu rabbuna yaʿlamu inna ilaykum lamur'saluna
wama ʿalayna illa l-balaghu l-mubinu
qalu inna tatayyarna bikum la-in lam tantahu lanarjumannakum walayamassannakum minna ʿadhabun alimun
qalu tairukum maʿakum a-in dhukkir'tum bal antum qawmun mus'rifuna
wajaa min aqsa l-madinati rajulun yasʿa qala yaqawmi ittabiʿu l-mur'salina
ittabiʿu man la yasalukum ajran wahum muh'taduna
wama liya la aʿbudu alladhi fatarani wa-ilayhi tur'jaʿuna

inni idhan lafi dalalin mubinin
inni amantu birabbikum fa-is'maʿuni

bima ghafara li rabbi wajaʿalani mina l-muk'ramina

in kanat illa sayhatan wahidatan fa-idha hum khamiduna

wa-in kullun lamma jamiʿun ladayna muh'daruna

wajaʿalna fiha jannatin min nakhilin wa-aʿnabin wafajjarna fiha mina l-ʿuyuni
liyakulu min thamarihi wama ʿamilathu aydihim afala yashkuruna
sub'hana alladhi khalaqa l-azwaja kullaha mimma tunbitu l-ardu wamin anfusihim wamimma la yaʿlamuna
waayatun lahumu al-laylu naslakhu min'hu l-nahara fa-idha hum muz'limuna
wal-shamsu tajri limus'taqarrin laha dhalika taqdiru l-ʿazizi l-ʿalimi
wal-qamara qaddarnahu manazila hatta ʿada kal-ʿur'juni l-qadimi
la l-shamsu yanbaghi laha an tud'rika l-qamara wala al-laylu sabiqu l-nahari wakullun fi falakin yasbahuna

walaw nashau latamasna ʿala aʿyunihim fa-is'tabaqu l-sirata fa-anna yub'siruna

ala lillahi l-dinu l-khalisu wa-alladhina ittakhadhu min dunihi awliyaa ma naʿbuduhum illa liyuqarribuna ila l-lahi zul'fa inna l-laha yahkumu baynahum fi ma hum fihi yakhtalifuna inna l-laha la yahdi man huwa kadhibun kaffarun
law arada l-lahu an yattakhidha waladan la-is'tafa mimma yakhluqu ma yashau sub'hanahu huwa l-lahu l-wahidu l-qaharu
khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda bil-haqi yukawwiru al-layla ʿala l-nahari wayukawwiru l-nahara ʿala al-layli wasakhara l-shamsa wal-qamara kullun yajri li-ajalin musamman ala huwa l-ʿazizu l-ghafaru
khalaqakum min nafsin wahidatin thumma jaʿala min'ha zawjaha wa-anzala lakum mina l-anʿami thamaniyata azwajin yakhluqukum fi butuni ummahatikum khalqan min baʿdi khalqin fi zulumatin thalathin dhalikumu l-lahu rabbukum lahu l-mul'ku la ilaha illa huwa fa-anna tus'rafuna
in takfuru fa-inna l-laha ghaniyyun ʿankum wala yarda liʿibadihi l-kuf'ra wa-in tashkuru yardahu lakum wala taziru waziratun wiz'ra ukh'ra thumma ila rabbikum marjiʿukum fayunabbi-ukum bima kuntum taʿmaluna innahu ʿalimun bidhati l-suduri
wa-idha massa l-insana durrun daʿa rabbahu muniban ilayhi thumma idha khawwalahu niʿ'matan min'hu nasiya ma kana yadʿu ilayhi min qablu wajaʿala lillahi andadan liyudilla ʿan sabilihi qul tamattaʿ bikuf'rika qalilan innaka min ashabi l-nari
amman huwa qanitun anaa al-layli sajidan waqaiman yahdharu l-akhirata wayarju rahmata rabbihi qul hal yastawi alladhina yaʿlamuna wa-alladhina la yaʿlamuna innama yatadhakkaru ulu l-albabi
qul yaʿibadi alladhina amanu ittaqu rabbakum lilladhina ahsanu fi hadhihi l-dun'ya hasanatun wa-ardu l-lahi wasiʿatun innama yuwaffa l-sabiruna ajrahum bighayri hisabin
qul inni umir'tu an aʿbuda l-laha mukh'lisan lahu l-dina
wa-umir'tu li-an akuna awwala l-mus'limina
qul inni akhafu in ʿasaytu rabbi ʿadhaba yawmin ʿazimin
quli l-laha aʿbudu mukh'lisan lahu dini
fa-uʿ'budu ma shi'tum min dunihi qul inna l-khasirina alladhina khasiru anfusahum wa-ahlihim yawma l-qiyamati ala dhalika huwa l-khus'ranu l-mubinu

wa-alladhina ij'tanabu l-taghuta an yaʿbuduha wa-anabu ila l-lahi lahumu l-bush'ra fabashir ʿibadi
alladhina yastamiʿuna l-qawla fayattabiʿuna ahsanahu ulaika alladhina hadahumu l-lahu wa-ulaika hum ulu l-albabi
afaman haqqa ʿalayhi kalimatu l-ʿadhabi afa-anta tunqidhu man fi l-nari
lakini alladhina ittaqaw rabbahum lahum ghurafun min fawqiha ghurafun mabniyyatun tajri min tahtiha l-anharu waʿda l-lahi la yukh'lifu l-lahu l-miʿada
alam tara anna l-laha anzala mina l-samai maan fasalakahu yanabiʿa fi l-ardi thumma yukh'riju bihi zarʿan mukh'talifan alwanuhu thumma yahiju fatarahu mus'farran thumma yajʿaluhu hutaman inna fi dhalika ladhik'ra li-uli l-albabi
afaman sharaha l-lahu sadrahu lil'is'lami fahuwa ʿala nurin min rabbihi fawaylun lil'qasiyati qulubuhum min dhik'ri l-lahi ulaika fi dalalin mubinin
al-lahu nazzala ahsana l-hadithi kitaban mutashabihan mathaniya taqshaʿirru min'hu juludu alladhina yakhshawna rabbahum thumma talinu juluduhum waqulubuhum ila dhik'ri l-lahi dhalika huda l-lahi yahdi bihi man yashau waman yud'lili l-lahu fama lahu min hadin
afaman yattaqi biwajhihi sua l-ʿadhabi yawma l-qiyamati waqila lilzzalimina dhuqu ma kuntum taksibuna
kadhaba alladhina min qablihim fa-atahumu l-ʿadhabu min haythu la yashʿuruna
fa-adhaqahumu l-lahu l-khiz'ya fi l-hayati l-dun'ya walaʿadhabu l-akhirati akbaru law kanu yaʿlamuna
walaqad darabna lilnnasi fi hadha l-qur'ani min kulli mathalin laʿallahum yatadhakkaruna
qur'anan ʿarabiyyan ghayra dhi ʿiwajin laʿallahum yattaquna
daraba l-lahu mathalan rajulan fihi shurakau mutashakisuna warajulan salaman lirajulin hal yastawiyani mathalan l-hamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la yaʿlamuna
innaka mayyitun wa-innahum mayyituna
thumma innakum yawma l-qiyamati ʿinda rabbikum takhtasimuna
faman azlamu mimman kadhaba ʿala l-lahi wakadhaba bil-sid'qi idh jaahu alaysa fi jahannama mathwan lil'kafirina
wa-alladhi jaa bil-sid'qi wasaddaqa bihi ulaika humu l-mutaquna
lahum ma yashauna ʿinda rabbihim dhalika jazau l-muh'sinina
liyukaffira l-lahu ʿanhum aswa-a alladhi ʿamilu wayajziyahum ajrahum bi-ahsani alladhi kanu yaʿmaluna
alaysa l-lahu bikafin ʿabdahu wayukhawwifunaka bi-alladhina min dunihi waman yud'lili l-lahu fama lahu min hadin
waman yahdi l-lahu fama lahu min mudillin alaysa l-lahu biʿazizin dhi intiqamin
wala-in sa-altahum man khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda layaqulunna l-lahu qul afara-aytum ma tadʿuna min duni l-lahi in aradaniya l-lahu bidurrin hal hunna kashifatu durrihi aw aradani birahmatin hal hunna mum'sikatu rahmatihi qul hasbiya l-lahu ʿalayhi yatawakkalu l-mutawakiluna
qul yaqawmi iʿ'malu ʿala makanatikum inni ʿamilun fasawfa taʿlamuna
man yatihi ʿadhabun yukh'zihi wayahillu ʿalayhi ʿadhabun muqimun
inna anzalna ʿalayka l-kitaba lilnnasi bil-haqi famani ih'tada falinafsihi waman dalla fa-innama yadillu ʿalayha wama anta ʿalayhim biwakilin
al-lahu yatawaffa l-anfusa hina mawtiha wa-allati lam tamut fi manamiha fayum'siku allati qada ʿalayha l-mawta wayur'silu l-ukh'ra ila ajalin musamman inna fi dhalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaruna
ami ittakhadhu min duni l-lahi shufaʿaa qul awalaw kanu la yamlikuna shayan wala yaʿqiluna
qul lillahi l-shafaʿatu jamiʿan lahu mul'ku l-samawati wal-ardi thumma ilayhi tur'jaʿuna
wa-idha dhukira l-lahu wahdahu ish'ma-azzat qulubu alladhina la yu'minuna bil-akhirati wa-idha dhukira alladhina min dunihi idha hum yastabshiruna
quli l-lahuma fatira l-samawati wal-ardi ʿalima l-ghaybi wal-shahadati anta tahkumu bayna ʿibadika fi ma kanu fihi yakhtalifuna
walaw anna lilladhina zalamu ma fi l-ardi jamiʿan wamith'lahu maʿahu la-if'tadaw bihi min sui l-ʿadhabi yawma l-qiyamati wabada lahum mina l-lahi ma lam yakunu yahtasibuna
wabada lahum sayyiatu ma kasabu wahaqa bihim ma kanu bihi yastahziuna
fa-idha massa l-insana durrun daʿana thumma idha khawwalnahu niʿ'matan minna qala innama utituhu ʿala ʿil'min bal hiya fit'natun walakinna aktharahum la yaʿlamuna
qad qalaha alladhina min qablihim fama aghna ʿanhum ma kanu yaksibuna
fa-asabahum sayyiatu ma kasabu wa-alladhina zalamu min haulai sayusibuhum sayyiatu ma kasabu wama hum bimuʿ'jizina
awalam yaʿlamu anna l-laha yabsutu l-riz'qa liman yashau wayaqdiru inna fi dhalika laayatin liqawmin yu'minuna
qul yaʿibadiya alladhina asrafu ʿala anfusihim la taqnatu min rahmati l-lahi inna l-laha yaghfiru l-dhunuba jamiʿan innahu huwa l-ghafuru l-rahimu
wa-anibu ila rabbikum wa-aslimu lahu min qabli an yatiyakumu l-ʿadhabu thumma la tunsaruna
wa-ittabiʿu ahsana ma unzila ilaykum min rabbikum min qabli an yatiyakumu l-ʿadhabu baghtatan wa-antum la tashʿuruna
an taqula nafsun yahasrata ʿala ma farrattu fi janbi l-lahi wa-in kuntu lamina l-sakhirina
aw taqula law anna l-laha hadani lakuntu mina l-mutaqina
aw taqula hina tara l-ʿadhaba law anna li karratan fa-akuna mina l-muh'sinina
bala qad jaatka ayati fakadhabta biha wa-is'takbarta wakunta mina l-kafirina
wayawma l-qiyamati tara alladhina kadhabu ʿala l-lahi wujuhuhum mus'waddatun alaysa fi jahannama mathwan lil'mutakabbirina
wayunajji l-lahu alladhina ittaqaw bimafazatihim la yamassuhumu l-suu wala hum yahzanuna
al-lahu khaliqu kulli shayin wahuwa ʿala kulli shayin wakilun
lahu maqalidu l-samawati wal-ardi wa-alladhina kafaru biayati l-lahi ulaika humu l-khasiruna
qul afaghayra l-lahi tamurunni aʿbudu ayyuha l-jahiluna
walaqad uhiya ilayka wa-ila alladhina min qablika la-in ashrakta layahbatanna ʿamaluka walatakunanna mina l-khasirina
bali l-laha fa-uʿ'bud wakun mina l-shakirina
wama qadaru l-laha haqqa qadrihi wal-ardu jamiʿan qabdatuhu yawma l-qiyamati wal-samawatu matwiyyatun biyaminihi sub'hanahu wataʿala ʿamma yush'rikuna
wanufikha fi l-suri fasaʿiqa man fi l-samawati waman fi l-ardi illa man shaa l-lahu thumma nufikha fihi ukh'ra fa-idha hum qiyamun yanzuruna
wa-ashraqati l-ardu binuri rabbiha wawudiʿa l-kitabu wajia bil-nabiyina wal-shuhadai waqudiya baynahum bil-haqi wahum la yuz'lamuna
wawuffiyat kullu nafsin ma ʿamilat wahuwa aʿlamu bima yafʿaluna
wasiqa alladhina kafaru ila jahannama zumaran hatta idha jauha futihat abwabuha waqala lahum khazanatuha alam yatikum rusulun minkum yatluna ʿalaykum ayati rabbikum wayundhirunakum liqaa yawmikum hadha qalu bala walakin haqqat kalimatu l-ʿadhabi ʿala l-kafirina
qila ud'khulu abwaba jahannama khalidina fiha fabi'sa mathwa l-mutakabirina
wasiqa alladhina ittaqaw rabbahum ila l-janati zumaran hatta idha jauha wafutihat abwabuha waqala lahum khazanatuha salamun ʿalaykum tib'tum fa-ud'khuluha khalidina
waqalu l-hamdu lillahi alladhi sadaqana waʿdahu wa-awrathana l-arda natabawwa-u mina l-janati haythu nashau faniʿ'ma ajru l-ʿamilina
watara l-malaikata haffina min hawli l-ʿarshi yusabbihuna bihamdi rabbihim waqudiya baynahum bil-haqi waqila l-hamdu lillahi rabbi l-ʿalamina
hha-meem
tanzilu l-kitabi mina l-lahi l-ʿazizi l-ʿalimi
ghafiri l-dhanbi waqabili l-tawbi shadidi l-ʿiqabi dhi l-tawli la ilaha illa huwa ilayhi l-masiru
ma yujadilu fi ayati l-lahi illa alladhina kafaru fala yaghrur'ka taqallubuhum fi l-biladi
kadhabat qablahum qawmu nuhin wal-ahzabu min baʿdihim wahammat kullu ummatin birasulihim liyakhudhuhu wajadalu bil-batili liyud'hidu bihi l-haqa fa-akhadhtuhum fakayfa kana ʿiqabi
wakadhalika haqqat kalimatu rabbika ʿala alladhina kafaru annahum ashabu l-nari
alladhina yahmiluna l-ʿarsha waman hawlahu yusabbihuna bihamdi rabbihim wayu'minuna bihi wayastaghfiruna lilladhina amanu rabbana wasiʿ'ta kulla shayin rahmatan waʿil'man fa-igh'fir lilladhina tabu wa-ittabaʿu sabilaka waqihim ʿadhaba l-jahimi
rabbana wa-adkhil'hum jannati ʿadnin allati waʿadttahum waman salaha min abaihim wa-azwajihim wadhurriyyatihim innaka anta l-ʿazizu l-hakimu
waqihimu l-sayiati waman taqi l-sayiati yawma-idhin faqad rahim'tahu wadhalika huwa l-fawzu l-ʿazimu
inna alladhina kafaru yunadawna lamaqtu l-lahi akbaru min maqtikum anfusakum idh tud'ʿawna ila l-imani fatakfuruna
qalu rabbana amattana ith'natayni wa-ahyaytana ith'natayni fa-iʿ'tarafna bidhunubina fahal ila khurujin min sabilin
dhalikum bi-annahu idha duʿiya l-lahu wahdahu kafartum wa-in yush'rak bihi tu'minu fal-huk'mu lillahi l-ʿaliyi l-kabiri
huwa alladhi yurikum ayatihi wayunazzilu lakum mina l-samai riz'qan wama yatadhakkaru illa man yunibu
fa-id'ʿu l-laha mukh'lisina lahu l-dina walaw kariha l-kafiruna
rafiʿu l-darajati dhu l-ʿarshi yul'qi l-ruha min amrihi ʿala man yashau min ʿibadihi liyundhira yawma l-talaqi
yawma hum barizuna la yakhfa ʿala l-lahi min'hum shayon limani l-mul'ku l-yawma lillahi l-wahidi l-qahari
al-yawma tuj'za kullu nafsin bima kasabat la zul'ma l-yawma inna l-laha sariʿu l-hisabi
wa-andhir'hum yawma l-azifati idhi l-qulubu lada l-hanajiri kazimina ma lilzzalimina min hamimin wala shafiʿin yutaʿu
yaʿlamu khainata l-aʿyuni wama tukh'fi l-suduru
wal-lahu yaqdi bil-haqi wa-alladhina yadʿuna min dunihi la yaqduna bishayin inna l-laha huwa l-samiʿu l-basiru
awalam yasiru fi l-ardi fayanzuru kayfa kana ʿaqibatu alladhina kanu min qablihim kanu hum ashadda min'hum quwwatan waatharan fi l-ardi fa-akhadhahumu l-lahu bidhunubihim wama kana lahum mina l-lahi min waqin
dhalika bi-annahum kanat tatihim rusuluhum bil-bayinati fakafaru fa-akhadhahumu l-lahu innahu qawiyyun shadidu l-ʿiqabi
walaqad arsalna musa biayatina wasul'tanin mubinin
ila fir'ʿawna wahamana waqaruna faqalu sahirun kadhabun
falamma jaahum bil-haqi min ʿindina qalu uq'tulu abnaa alladhina amanu maʿahu wa-is'tahyu nisaahum wama kaydu l-kafirina illa fi dalalin
waqala fir'ʿawnu dharuni aqtul musa walyadʿu rabbahu inni akhafu an yubaddila dinakum aw an yuz'hira fi l-ardi l-fasada
waqala musa inni ʿudh'tu birabbi warabbikum min kulli mutakabbirin la yu'minu biyawmi l-hisabi
waqala rajulun mu'minun min ali fir'ʿawna yaktumu imanahu ataqtuluna rajulan an yaqula rabbiya l-lahu waqad jaakum bil-bayinati min rabbikum wa-in yaku kadhiban faʿalayhi kadhibuhu wa-in yaku sadiqan yusib'kum baʿdu alladhi yaʿidukum inna l-laha la yahdi man huwa mus'rifun kadhabun
yaqawmi lakumu l-mul'ku l-yawma zahirina fi l-ardi faman yansuruna min basi l-lahi in jaana qala fir'ʿawnu ma urikum illa ma ara wama ahdikum illa sabila l-rashadi
waqala alladhi amana yaqawmi inni akhafu ʿalaykum mith'la yawmi l-ahzabi
mith'la dabi qawmi nuhin waʿadin wathamuda wa-alladhina min baʿdihim wama l-lahu yuridu zul'man lil'ʿibadi
wayaqawmi inni akhafu ʿalaykum yawma l-tanadi
yawma tuwalluna mud'birina ma lakum mina l-lahi min ʿasimin waman yud'lili l-lahu fama lahu min hadin
walaqad jaakum yusufu min qablu bil-bayinati fama zil'tum fi shakkin mimma jaakum bihi hatta idha halaka qul'tum lan yabʿatha l-lahu min baʿdihi rasulan kadhalika yudillu l-lahu man huwa mus'rifun mur'tabun
alladhina yujadiluna fi ayati l-lahi bighayri sul'tanin atahum kabura maqtan ʿinda l-lahi waʿinda alladhina amanu kadhalika yatbaʿu l-lahu ʿala kulli qalbi mutakabbirin jabbarin
waqala fir'ʿawnu yahamanu ib'ni li sarhan laʿalli ablughu l-asbaba
asbaba l-samawati fa-attaliʿa ila ilahi musa wa-inni la-azunnuhu kadhiban wakadhalika zuyyina lifir'ʿawna suu ʿamalihi wasudda ʿani l-sabili wama kaydu fir'ʿawna illa fi tababin
waqala alladhi amana yaqawmi ittabiʿuni ahdikum sabila l-rashadi
yaqawmi innama hadhihi l-hayatu l-dun'ya mataʿun wa-inna l-akhirata hiya daru l-qarari
man ʿamila sayyi-atan fala yuj'za illa mith'laha waman ʿamila salihan min dhakarin aw untha wahuwa mu'minun fa-ulaika yadkhuluna l-janata yur'zaquna fiha bighayri hisabin
wayaqawmi ma li adʿukum ila l-najati watadʿunani ila l-nari
tadʿunani li-akfura bil-lahi wa-ush'rika bihi ma laysa li bihi ʿil'mun wa-ana adʿukum ila l-ʿazizi l-ghafari
la jarama annama tadʿunani ilayhi laysa lahu daʿwatun fi l-dun'ya wala fi l-akhirati wa-anna maraddana ila l-lahi wa-anna l-mus'rifina hum ashabu l-nari
fasatadhkuruna ma aqulu lakum wa-ufawwidu amri ila l-lahi inna l-laha basirun bil-ʿibadi
fawaqahu l-lahu sayyiati ma makaru wahaqa biali fir'ʿawna suu l-ʿadhabi
al-naru yuʿ'raduna ʿalayha ghuduwwan waʿashiyyan wayawma taqumu l-saʿatu adkhilu ala fir'ʿawna ashadda l-ʿadhabi
wa-idh yatahajjuna fi l-nari fayaqulu l-duʿafau lilladhina is'takbaru inna kunna lakum tabaʿan fahal antum mugh'nuna ʿanna nasiban mina l-nari
qala alladhina is'takbaru inna kullun fiha inna l-laha qad hakama bayna l-ʿibadi
waqala alladhina fi l-nari likhazanati jahannama id'ʿu rabbakum yukhaffif ʿanna yawman mina l-ʿadhabi
qalu awalam taku tatikum rusulukum bil-bayinati qalu bala qalu fa-id'ʿu wama duʿau l-kafirina illa fi dalalin
inna lanansuru rusulana wa-alladhina amanu fi l-hayati l-dun'ya wayawma yaqumu l-ashhadu
yawma la yanfaʿu l-zalimina maʿdhiratuhum walahumu l-laʿnatu walahum suu l-dari
walaqad atayna musa l-huda wa-awrathna bani is'raila l-kitaba
hudan wadhik'ra li-uli l-albabi
fa-is'bir inna waʿda l-lahi haqqun wa-is'taghfir lidhanbika wasabbih bihamdi rabbika bil-ʿashiyi wal-ib'kari
inna alladhina yujadiluna fi ayati l-lahi bighayri sul'tanin atahum in fi sudurihim illa kib'run ma hum bibalighihi fa-is'taʿidh bil-lahi innahu huwa l-samiʿu l-basiru
lakhalqu l-samawati wal-ardi akbaru min khalqi l-nasi walakinna akthara l-nasi la yaʿlamuna
wama yastawi l-aʿma wal-basiru wa-alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati wala l-musiu qalilan ma tatadhakkaruna
inna l-saʿata laatiyatun la rayba fiha walakinna akthara l-nasi la yu'minuna
waqala rabbukumu id'ʿuni astajib lakum inna alladhina yastakbiruna ʿan ʿibadati sayadkhuluna jahannama dakhirina
al-lahu alladhi jaʿala lakumu al-layla litaskunu fihi wal-nahara mub'siran inna l-laha ladhu fadlin ʿala l-nasi walakinna akthara l-nasi la yashkuruna
dhalikumu l-lahu rabbukum khaliqu kulli shayin la ilaha illa huwa fa-anna tu'fakuna
kadhalika yu'faku alladhina kanu biayati l-lahi yajhaduna
al-lahu alladhi jaʿala lakumu l-arda qararan wal-samaa binaan wasawwarakum fa-ahsana suwarakum warazaqakum mina l-tayibati dhalikumu l-lahu rabbukum fatabaraka l-lahu rabbu l-ʿalamina
huwa l-hayu la ilaha illa huwa fa-id'ʿuhu mukh'lisina lahu l-dina l-hamdu lillahi rabbi l-ʿalamina
qul inni nuhitu an aʿbuda alladhina tadʿuna min duni l-lahi lamma jaaniya l-bayinatu min rabbi wa-umir'tu an us'lima lirabbi l-ʿalamina
huwa alladhi khalaqakum min turabin thumma min nut'fatin thumma min ʿalaqatin thumma yukh'rijukum tif'lan thumma litablughu ashuddakum thumma litakunu shuyukhan waminkum man yutawaffa min qablu walitablughu ajalan musamman walaʿallakum taʿqiluna
huwa alladhi yuh'yi wayumitu fa-idha qada amran fa-innama yaqulu lahu kun fayakunu
alam tara ila alladhina yujadiluna fi ayati l-lahi anna yus'rafuna
alladhina kadhabu bil-kitabi wabima arsalna bihi rusulana fasawfa yaʿlamuna
idhi l-aghlalu fi aʿnaqihim wal-salasilu yus'habuna
fi l-hamimi thumma fi l-nari yus'jaruna
thumma qila lahum ayna ma kuntum tush'rikuna
min duni l-lahi qalu dallu ʿanna bal lam nakun nadʿu min qablu shayan kadhalika yudillu l-lahu l-kafirina
dhalikum bima kuntum tafrahuna fi l-ardi bighayri l-haqi wabima kuntum tamrahuna
ud'khulu abwaba jahannama khalidina fiha fabi'sa mathwa l-mutakabirina
fa-is'bir inna waʿda l-lahi haqqun fa-imma nuriyannaka baʿda alladhi naʿiduhum aw natawaffayannaka fa-ilayna yur'jaʿuna
walaqad arsalna rusulan min qablika min'hum man qasasna ʿalayka wamin'hum man lam naqsus ʿalayka wama kana lirasulin an yatiya biayatin illa bi-idh'ni l-lahi fa-idha jaa amru l-lahi qudiya bil-haqi wakhasira hunalika l-mub'tiluna
al-lahu alladhi jaʿala lakumu l-anʿama litarkabu min'ha wamin'ha takuluna
walakum fiha manafiʿu walitablughu ʿalayha hajatan fi sudurikum waʿalayha waʿala l-ful'ki tuh'maluna
wayurikum ayatihi fa-ayya ayati l-lahi tunkiruna
afalam yasiru fi l-ardi fayanzuru kayfa kana ʿaqibatu alladhina min qablihim kanu akthara min'hum wa-ashadda quwwatan waatharan fi l-ardi fama aghna ʿanhum ma kanu yaksibuna
falamma jaathum rusuluhum bil-bayinati farihu bima ʿindahum mina l-ʿil'mi wahaqa bihim ma kanu bihi yastahziuna
falamma ra-aw basana qalu amanna bil-lahi wahdahu wakafarna bima kunna bihi mush'rikina
falam yaku yanfaʿuhum imanuhum lamma ra-aw basana sunnata l-lahi allati qad khalat fi ʿibadihi wakhasira hunalika l-kafiruna
hha-meem
tanzilun mina l-rahmani l-rahimi
kitabun fussilat ayatuhu qur'anan ʿarabiyyan liqawmin yaʿlamuna
bashiran wanadhiran fa-aʿrada aktharuhum fahum la yasmaʿuna
waqalu qulubuna fi akinnatin mimma tadʿuna ilayhi wafi adhanina waqrun wamin baynina wabaynika hijabun fa-iʿ'mal innana ʿamiluna
qul innama ana basharun mith'lukum yuha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun fa-is'taqimu ilayhi wa-is'taghfiruhu wawaylun lil'mush'rikina
alladhina la yu'tuna l-zakata wahum bil-akhirati hum kafiruna
inna alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati lahum ajrun ghayru mamnunin
qul a-innakum latakfuruna bi-alladhi khalaqa l-arda fi yawmayni watajʿaluna lahu andadan dhalika rabbu l-ʿalamina
wajaʿala fiha rawasiya min fawqiha wabaraka fiha waqaddara fiha aqwataha fi arbaʿati ayyamin sawaan lilssailina
thumma is'tawa ila l-samai wahiya dukhanun faqala laha walil'ardi i'tiya tawʿan aw karhan qalata atayna taiʿina
faqadahunna sabʿa samawatin fi yawmayni wa-awha fi kulli samain amraha wazayyanna l-samaa l-dun'ya bimasabiha wahif'zan dhalika taqdiru l-ʿazizi l-ʿalimi
fa-in aʿradu faqul andhartukum saʿiqatan mith'la saʿiqati ʿadin wathamuda
idh jaathumu l-rusulu min bayni aydihim wamin khalfihim alla taʿbudu illa l-laha qalu law shaa rabbuna la-anzala malaikatan fa-inna bima ur'sil'tum bihi kafiruna
fa-amma ʿadun fa-is'takbaru fi l-ardi bighayri l-haqi waqalu man ashaddu minna quwwatan awalam yaraw anna l-laha alladhi khalaqahum huwa ashaddu min'hum quwwatan wakanu biayatina yajhaduna
fa-arsalna ʿalayhim rihan sarsaran fi ayyamin nahisatin linudhiqahum ʿadhaba l-khiz'yi fi l-hayati l-dun'ya walaʿadhabu l-akhirati akhza wahum la yunsaruna
wa-amma thamudu fahadaynahum fa-is'tahabbu l-ʿama ʿala l-huda fa-akhadhathum saʿiqatu l-ʿadhabi l-huni bima kanu yaksibuna
wanajjayna alladhina amanu wakanu yattaquna
wayawma yuh'sharu aʿdau l-lahi ila l-nari fahum yuzaʿuna
hatta idha ma jauha shahida ʿalayhim samʿuhum wa-absaruhum wajuluduhum bima kanu yaʿmaluna
waqalu lijuludihim lima shahidttum ʿalayna qalu antaqana l-lahu alladhi antaqa kulla shayin wahuwa khalaqakum awwala marratin wa-ilayhi tur'jaʿuna
wama kuntum tastatiruna an yashhada ʿalaykum samʿukum wala absarukum wala juludukum walakin zanantum anna l-laha la yaʿlamu kathiran mimma taʿmaluna
wadhalikum zannukumu alladhi zanantum birabbikum ardakum fa-asbahtum mina l-khasirina
fa-in yasbiru fal-naru mathwan lahum wa-in yastaʿtibu fama hum mina l-muʿ'tabina
waqayyadna lahum quranaa fazayyanu lahum ma bayna aydihim wama khalfahum wahaqqa ʿalayhimu l-qawlu fi umamin qad khalat min qablihim mina l-jini wal-insi innahum kanu khasirina
waqala alladhina kafaru la tasmaʿu lihadha l-qur'ani wal-ghaw fihi laʿallakum taghlibuna
falanudhiqanna alladhina kafaru ʿadhaban shadidan walanajziyannahum aswa-a alladhi kanu yaʿmaluna
dhalika jazau aʿdai l-lahi l-naru lahum fiha daru l-khul'di jazaan bima kanu biayatina yajhaduna
waqala alladhina kafaru rabbana arina alladhayni adallana mina l-jini wal-insi najʿalhuma tahta aqdamina liyakuna mina l-asfalina
inna alladhina qalu rabbuna l-lahu thumma is'taqamu tatanazzalu ʿalayhimu l-malaikatu alla takhafu wala tahzanu wa-abshiru bil-janati allati kuntum tuʿaduna
nahnu awliyaukum fi l-hayati l-dun'ya wafi l-akhirati walakum fiha ma tashtahi anfusukum walakum fiha ma taddaʿuna
nuzulan min ghafurin rahimin
waman ahsanu qawlan mimman daʿa ila l-lahi waʿamila salihan waqala innani mina l-mus'limina
wala tastawi l-hasanatu wala l-sayi-atu id'faʿ bi-allati hiya ahsanu fa-idha alladhi baynaka wabaynahu ʿadawatun ka-annahu waliyyun hamimun
wama yulaqqaha illa alladhina sabaru wama yulaqqaha illa dhu hazzin ʿazimin
wa-imma yanzaghannaka mina l-shaytani nazghun fa-is'taʿidh bil-lahi innahu huwa l-samiʿu l-ʿalimu
wamin ayatihi al-laylu wal-naharu wal-shamsu wal-qamaru la tasjudu lilshamsi wala lil'qamari wa-us'judu lillahi alladhi khalaqahunna in kuntum iyyahu taʿbuduna
fa-ini is'takbaru fa-alladhina ʿinda rabbika yusabbihuna lahu bi-al-layli wal-nahari wahum la yasamuna
wamin ayatihi annaka tara l-arda khashiʿatan fa-idha anzalna ʿalayha l-maa ih'tazzat warabat inna alladhi ahyaha lamuh'yi l-mawta innahu ʿala kulli shayin qadirun
inna alladhina yul'hiduna fi ayatina la yakhfawna ʿalayna afaman yul'qa fi l-nari khayrun am man yati aminan yawma l-qiyamati iʿ'malu ma shi'tum innahu bima taʿmaluna basirun
inna alladhina kafaru bil-dhik'ri lamma jaahum wa-innahu lakitabun ʿazizun
la yatihi l-batilu min bayni yadayhi wala min khalfihi tanzilun min hakimin hamidin
ma yuqalu laka illa ma qad qila lilrrusuli min qablika inna rabbaka ladhu maghfiratin wadhu ʿiqabin alimin
walaw jaʿalnahu qur'anan aʿjamiyyan laqalu lawla fussilat ayatuhu aʿ'jamiyyun waʿarabiyyun qul huwa lilladhina amanu hudan washifaon wa-alladhina la yu'minuna fi adhanihim waqrun wahuwa ʿalayhim ʿaman ulaika yunadawna min makanin baʿidin
walaqad atayna musa l-kitaba fa-ukh'tulifa fihi walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum wa-innahum lafi shakkin min'hu muribin
man ʿamila salihan falinafsihi waman asaa faʿalayha wama rabbuka bizallamin lil'ʿabidi
ilayhi yuraddu ʿil'mu l-saʿati wama takhruju min thamaratin min akmamiha wama tahmilu min untha wala tadaʿu illa biʿil'mihi wayawma yunadihim ayna shurakai qalu adhannaka ma minna min shahidin
wadalla ʿanhum ma kanu yadʿuna min qablu wazannu ma lahum min mahisin
la yasamu l-insanu min duʿai l-khayri wa-in massahu l-sharu fayausun qanutun
wala-in adhaqnahu rahmatan minna min baʿdi darraa massathu layaqulanna hadha li wama azunnu l-saʿata qaimatan wala-in rujiʿ'tu ila rabbi inna li ʿindahu lalhus'na falanunabbi-anna alladhina kafaru bima ʿamilu walanudhiqannahum min ʿadhabin ghalizin
wa-idha anʿamna ʿala l-insani aʿrada wanaa bijanibihi wa-idha massahu l-sharu fadhu duʿain ʿaridin
qul ara-aytum in kana min ʿindi l-lahi thumma kafartum bihi man adallu mimman huwa fi shiqaqin baʿidin
sanurihim ayatina fi l-afaqi wafi anfusihim hatta yatabayyana lahum annahu l-haqu awalam yakfi birabbika annahu ʿala kulli shayin shahidun
ala innahum fi mir'yatin min liqai rabbihim ala innahu bikulli shayin muhitun
hha-meem
ain-seen-qaf
kadhalika yuhi ilayka wa-ila alladhina min qablika l-lahu l-ʿazizu l-hakimu
lahu ma fi l-samawati wama fi l-ardi wahuwa l-ʿaliyu l-ʿazimu
takadu l-samawatu yatafattarna min fawqihinna wal-malaikatu yusabbihuna bihamdi rabbihim wayastaghfiruna liman fi l-ardi ala inna l-laha huwa l-ghafuru l-rahimu
wa-alladhina ittakhadhu min dunihi awliyaa l-lahu hafizun ʿalayhim wama anta ʿalayhim biwakilin
wakadhalika awhayna ilayka qur'anan ʿarabiyyan litundhira umma l-qura waman hawlaha watundhira yawma l-jamʿi la rayba fihi fariqun fi l-janati wafariqun fi l-saʿiri
walaw shaa l-lahu lajaʿalahum ummatan wahidatan walakin yud'khilu man yashau fi rahmatihi wal-zalimuna ma lahum min waliyyin wala nasirin
ami ittakhadhu min dunihi awliyaa fal-lahu huwa l-waliyu wahuwa yuh'yi l-mawta wahuwa ʿala kulli shayin qadirun
wama ikh'talaftum fihi min shayin fahuk'muhu ila l-lahi dhalikumu l-lahu rabbi ʿalayhi tawakkaltu wa-ilayhi unibu
fatiru l-samawati wal-ardi jaʿala lakum min anfusikum azwajan wamina l-anʿami azwajan yadhra-ukum fihi laysa kamith'lihi shayon wahuwa l-samiʿu l-basiru
lahu maqalidu l-samawati wal-ardi yabsutu l-riz'qa liman yashau wayaqdiru innahu bikulli shayin ʿalimun
sharaʿa lakum mina l-dini ma wassa bihi nuhan wa-alladhi awhayna ilayka wama wassayna bihi ib'rahima wamusa waʿisa an aqimu l-dina wala tatafarraqu fihi kabura ʿala l-mush'rikina ma tadʿuhum ilayhi l-lahu yajtabi ilayhi man yashau wayahdi ilayhi man yunibu
wama tafarraqu illa min baʿdi ma jaahumu l-ʿil'mu baghyan baynahum walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika ila ajalin musamman laqudiya baynahum wa-inna alladhina urithu l-kitaba min baʿdihim lafi shakkin min'hu muribin
falidhalika fa-ud'ʿu wa-is'taqim kama umir'ta wala tattabiʿ ahwaahum waqul amantu bima anzala l-lahu min kitabin wa-umir'tu li-aʿdila baynakumu l-lahu rabbuna warabbukum lana aʿmaluna walakum aʿmalukum la hujjata baynana wabaynakumu l-lahu yajmaʿu baynana wa-ilayhi l-masiru
wa-alladhina yuhajjuna fi l-lahi min baʿdi ma us'tujiba lahu hujjatuhum dahidatun ʿinda rabbihim waʿalayhim ghadabun walahum ʿadhabun shadidun
al-lahu alladhi anzala l-kitaba bil-haqi wal-mizana wama yud'rika laʿalla l-saʿata qaribun
yastaʿjilu biha alladhina la yu'minuna biha wa-alladhina amanu mush'fiquna min'ha wayaʿlamuna annaha l-haqu ala inna alladhina yumaruna fi l-saʿati lafi dalalin baʿidin
al-lahu latifun biʿibadihi yarzuqu man yashau wahuwa l-qawiyu l-ʿazizu
man kana yuridu hartha l-akhirati nazid lahu fi harthihi waman kana yuridu hartha l-dun'ya nu'tihi min'ha wama lahu fi l-akhirati min nasibin
am lahum shurakau sharaʿu lahum mina l-dini ma lam yadhan bihi l-lahu walawla kalimatu l-fasli laqudiya baynahum wa-inna l-zalimina lahum ʿadhabun alimun
tara l-zalimina mush'fiqina mimma kasabu wahuwa waqiʿun bihim wa-alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati fi rawdati l-janati lahum ma yashauna ʿinda rabbihim dhalika huwa l-fadlu l-kabiru
dhalika alladhi yubashiru l-lahu ʿibadahu alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati qul la asalukum ʿalayhi ajran illa l-mawadata fi l-qur'ba waman yaqtarif hasanatan nazid lahu fiha hus'nan inna l-laha ghafurun shakurun
am yaquluna if'tara ʿala l-lahi kadhiban fa-in yasha-i l-lahu yakhtim ʿala qalbika wayamhu l-lahu l-batila wayuhiqqu l-haqa bikalimatihi innahu ʿalimun bidhati l-suduri
wahuwa alladhi yaqbalu l-tawbata ʿan ʿibadihi wayaʿfu ʿani l-sayiati wayaʿlamu ma tafʿaluna
wayastajibu alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati wayaziduhum min fadlihi wal-kafiruna lahum ʿadhabun shadidun
walaw basata l-lahu l-riz'qa liʿibadihi labaghaw fi l-ardi walakin yunazzilu biqadarin ma yashau innahu biʿibadihi khabirun basirun
wahuwa alladhi yunazzilu l-ghaytha min baʿdi ma qanatu wayanshuru rahmatahu wahuwa l-waliyu l-hamidu
wamin ayatihi khalqu l-samawati wal-ardi wama batha fihima min dabbatin wahuwa ʿala jamʿihim idha yashau qadirun
wama asabakum min musibatin fabima kasabat aydikum wayaʿfu ʿan kathirin
wama antum bimuʿ'jizina fi l-ardi wama lakum min duni l-lahi min waliyyin wala nasirin
wamin ayatihi l-jawari fi l-bahri kal-aʿlami
in yasha yus'kini l-riha fayazlalna rawakida ʿala zahrihi inna fi dhalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakurin
aw yubiq'hunna bima kasabu wayaʿfu ʿan kathirin
wayaʿlama alladhina yujadiluna fi ayatina ma lahum min mahisin
fama utitum min shayin famataʿu l-hayati l-dun'ya wama ʿinda l-lahi khayrun wa-abqa lilladhina amanu waʿala rabbihim yatawakkaluna
wa-alladhina yajtanibuna kabaira l-ith'mi wal-fawahisha wa-idha ma ghadibu hum yaghfiruna
wa-alladhina is'tajabu lirabbihim wa-aqamu l-salata wa-amruhum shura baynahum wamimma razaqnahum yunfiquna
wa-alladhina idha asabahumu l-baghyu hum yantasiruna
wajazau sayyi-atin sayyi-atun mith'luha faman ʿafa wa-aslaha fa-ajruhu ʿala l-lahi innahu la yuhibbu l-zalimina
walamani intasara baʿda zul'mihi fa-ulaika ma ʿalayhim min sabilin
innama l-sabilu ʿala alladhina yazlimuna l-nasa wayabghuna fi l-ardi bighayri l-haqi ulaika lahum ʿadhabun alimun
walaman sabara waghafara inna dhalika lamin ʿazmi l-umuri
waman yud'lili l-lahu fama lahu min waliyyin min baʿdihi watara l-zalimina lamma ra-awu l-ʿadhaba yaquluna hal ila maraddin min sabilin
watarahum yuʿ'raduna ʿalayha khashiʿina mina l-dhuli yanzuruna min tarfin khafiyyin waqala alladhina amanu inna l-khasirina alladhina khasiru anfusahum wa-ahlihim yawma l-qiyamati ala inna l-zalimina fi ʿadhabin muqimin
wama kana lahum min awliyaa yansurunahum min duni l-lahi waman yud'lili l-lahu fama lahu min sabilin
is'tajibu lirabbikum min qabli an yatiya yawmun la maradda lahu mina l-lahi ma lakum min malja-in yawma-idhin wama lakum min nakirin
fa-in aʿradu fama arsalnaka ʿalayhim hafizan in ʿalayka illa l-balaghu wa-inna idha adhaqna l-insana minna rahmatan fariha biha wa-in tusib'hum sayyi-atun bima qaddamat aydihim fa-inna l-insana kafurun
lillahi mul'ku l-samawati wal-ardi yakhluqu ma yashau yahabu liman yashau inathan wayahabu liman yashau l-dhukura
aw yuzawwijuhum dhuk'ranan wa-inathan wayajʿalu man yashau ʿaqiman innahu ʿalimun qadirun
wama kana libasharin an yukallimahu l-lahu illa wahyan aw min warai hijabin aw yur'sila rasulan fayuhiya bi-idh'nihi ma yashau innahu ʿaliyyun hakimun
wakadhalika awhayna ilayka ruhan min amrina ma kunta tadri ma l-kitabu wala l-imanu walakin jaʿalnahu nuran nahdi bihi man nashau min ʿibadina wa-innaka latahdi ila siratin mus'taqimin
sirati l-lahi alladhi lahu ma fi l-samawati wama fi l-ardi ala ila l-lahi tasiru l-umuru
hha-meem
wal-kitabi l-mubini
inna jaʿalnahu qur'anan ʿarabiyyan laʿallakum taʿqiluna
wa-innahu fi ummi l-kitabi ladayna laʿaliyyun hakimun
afanadribu ʿankumu l-dhik'ra safhan an kuntum qawman mus'rifina
wakam arsalna min nabiyyin fi l-awalina
wama yatihim min nabiyyin illa kanu bihi yastahziuna
fa-ahlakna ashadda min'hum batshan wamada mathalu l-awalina
wala-in sa-altahum man khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda layaqulunna khalaqahunna l-ʿazizu l-ʿalimu
alladhi jaʿala lakumu l-arda mahdan wajaʿala lakum fiha subulan laʿallakum tahtaduna
wa-alladhi nazzala mina l-samai maan biqadarin fa-ansharna bihi baldatan maytan kadhalika tukh'rajuna
wa-alladhi khalaqa l-azwaja kullaha wajaʿala lakum mina l-ful'ki wal-anʿami ma tarkabuna
litastawu ʿala zuhurihi thumma tadhkuru niʿ'mata rabbikum idha is'tawaytum ʿalayhi wataqulu sub'hana alladhi sakhara lana hadha wama kunna lahu muq'rinina
wa-inna ila rabbina lamunqalibuna
wajaʿalu lahu min ʿibadihi juz'an inna l-insana lakafurun mubinun
ami ittakhadha mimma yakhluqu banatin wa-asfakum bil-banina
wa-idha bushira ahaduhum bima daraba lilrrahmani mathalan zalla wajhuhu mus'waddan wahuwa kazimun
awaman yunasha-u fi l-hil'yati wahuwa fi l-khisami ghayru mubinin
wajaʿalu l-malaikata alladhina hum ʿibadu l-rahmani inathan ashahidu khalqahum satuk'tabu shahadatuhum wayus'aluna
waqalu law shaa l-rahmanu ma ʿabadnahum ma lahum bidhalika min ʿil'min in hum illa yakhrusuna
am ataynahum kitaban min qablihi fahum bihi mus'tamsikuna
bal qalu inna wajadna abaana ʿala ummatin wa-inna ʿala atharihim muh'taduna
wakadhalika ma arsalna min qablika fi qaryatin min nadhirin illa qala mut'rafuha inna wajadna abaana ʿala ummatin wa-inna ʿala atharihim muq'taduna
qala awalaw ji'tukum bi-ahda mimma wajadttum ʿalayhi abaakum qalu inna bima ur'sil'tum bihi kafiruna
fa-intaqamna min'hum fa-unzur kayfa kana ʿaqibatu l-mukadhibina
wa-idh qala ib'rahimu li-abihi waqawmihi innani baraon mimma taʿbuduna
illa alladhi fatarani fa-innahu sayahdini
wajaʿalaha kalimatan baqiyatan fi ʿaqibihi laʿallahum yarjiʿuna
bal mattaʿtu haulai waabaahum hatta jaahumu l-haqu warasulun mubinun
walamma jaahumu l-haqu qalu hadha sih'run wa-inna bihi kafiruna
waqalu lawla nuzzila hadha l-qur'anu ʿala rajulin mina l-qaryatayni ʿazimin
ahum yaqsimuna rahmata rabbika nahnu qasamna baynahum maʿishatahum fi l-hayati l-dun'ya warafaʿna baʿdahum fawqa baʿdin darajatin liyattakhidha baʿduhum baʿdan sukh'riyyan warahmatu rabbika khayrun mimma yajmaʿuna
walawla an yakuna l-nasu ummatan wahidatan lajaʿalna liman yakfuru bil-rahmani libuyutihim suqufan min fiddatin wamaʿarija ʿalayha yazharuna
walibuyutihim abwaban wasururan ʿalayha yattakiuna
wazukh'rufan wa-in kullu dhalika lamma mataʿu l-hayati l-dun'ya wal-akhiratu ʿinda rabbika lil'muttaqina
waman yaʿshu ʿan dhik'ri l-rahmani nuqayyid lahu shaytanan fahuwa lahu qarinun
wa-innahum layasuddunahum ʿani l-sabili wayahsabuna annahum muh'taduna
hatta idha jaana qala yalayta bayni wabaynaka buʿ'da l-mashriqayni fabi'sa l-qarinu
walan yanfaʿakumu l-yawma idh zalamtum annakum fi l-ʿadhabi mush'tarikuna
afa-anta tus'miʿu l-suma aw tahdi l-ʿum'ya waman kana fi dalalin mubinin
fa-imma nadhhabanna bika fa-inna min'hum muntaqimuna
aw nuriyannaka alladhi waʿadnahum fa-inna ʿalayhim muq'tadiruna
fa-is'tamsik bi-alladhi uhiya ilayka innaka ʿala siratin mus'taqimin
wa-innahu ladhik'run laka waliqawmika wasawfa tus'aluna
wasal man arsalna min qablika min rusulina ajaʿalna min duni l-rahmani alihatan yuʿ'baduna
walaqad arsalna musa biayatina ila fir'ʿawna wamala-ihi faqala inni rasulu rabbi l-ʿalamina
falamma jaahum biayatina idha hum min'ha yadhakuna
wama nurihim min ayatin illa hiya akbaru min ukh'tiha wa-akhadhnahum bil-ʿadhabi laʿallahum yarjiʿuna
waqalu yaayyuha l-sahiru ud'ʿu lana rabbaka bima ʿahida ʿindaka innana lamuh'taduna
falamma kashafna ʿanhumu l-ʿadhaba idha hum yankuthuna
wanada fir'ʿawnu fi qawmihi qala yaqawmi alaysa li mul'ku mis'ra wahadhihi l-anharu tajri min tahti afala tub'siruna
am ana khayrun min hadha alladhi huwa mahinun wala yakadu yubinu
falawla ul'qiya ʿalayhi aswiratun min dhahabin aw jaa maʿahu l-malaikatu muq'tarinina
fa-is'takhaffa qawmahu fa-ataʿuhu innahum kanu qawman fasiqina
falamma asafuna intaqamna min'hum fa-aghraqnahum ajmaʿina
fajaʿalnahum salafan wamathalan lil'akhirina
walamma duriba ub'nu maryama mathalan idha qawmuka min'hu yasidduna
waqalu aalihatuna khayrun am huwa ma darabuhu laka illa jadalan bal hum qawmun khasimuna
in huwa illa ʿabdun anʿamna ʿalayhi wajaʿalnahu mathalan libani is'raila
walaw nashau lajaʿalna minkum malaikatan fi l-ardi yakhlufuna
wa-innahu laʿil'mun lilssaʿati fala tamtarunna biha wa-ittabiʿuni hadha siratun mus'taqimun
wala yasuddannakumu l-shaytanu innahu lakum ʿaduwwun mubinun
walamma jaa ʿisa bil-bayinati qala qad ji'tukum bil-hik'mati wali-ubayyina lakum baʿda alladhi takhtalifuna fihi fa-ittaqu l-laha wa-atiʿuni
inna l-laha huwa rabbi warabbukum fa-uʿ'buduhu hadha siratun mus'taqimun
fa-ikh'talafa l-ahzabu min baynihim fawaylun lilladhina zalamu min ʿadhabi yawmin alimin
hal yanzuruna illa l-saʿata an tatiyahum baghtatan wahum la yashʿuruna
al-akhilau yawma-idhin baʿduhum libaʿdin ʿaduwwun illa l-mutaqina
yaʿibadi la khawfun ʿalaykumu l-yawma wala antum tahzanuna
alladhina amanu biayatina wakanu mus'limina
ud'khulu l-janata antum wa-azwajukum tuh'baruna
yutafu ʿalayhim bisihafin min dhahabin wa-akwabin wafiha ma tashtahihi l-anfusu wataladhu l-aʿyunu wa-antum fiha khaliduna
watil'ka l-janatu allati urith'tumuha bima kuntum taʿmaluna
lakum fiha fakihatun kathiratun min'ha takuluna
inna l-muj'rimina fi ʿadhabi jahannama khaliduna
la yufattaru ʿanhum wahum fihi mub'lisuna
wama zalamnahum walakin kanu humu l-zalimina
wanadaw yamaliku liyaqdi ʿalayna rabbuka qala innakum makithuna
laqad ji'nakum bil-haqi walakinna aktharakum lil'haqqi karihuna
am abramu amran fa-inna mub'rimuna
am yahsabuna anna la nasmaʿu sirrahum wanajwahum bala warusuluna ladayhim yaktubuna
qul in kana lilrrahmani waladun fa-ana awwalu l-ʿabidina
sub'hana rabbi l-samawati wal-ardi rabbi l-ʿarshi ʿamma yasifuna
fadharhum yakhudu wayalʿabu hatta yulaqu yawmahumu alladhi yuʿaduna
wahuwa alladhi fi l-samai ilahun wafi l-ardi ilahun wahuwa l-hakimu l-ʿalimu
watabaraka alladhi lahu mul'ku l-samawati wal-ardi wama baynahuma waʿindahu ʿil'mu l-saʿati wa-ilayhi tur'jaʿuna
wala yamliku alladhina yadʿuna min dunihi l-shafaʿata illa man shahida bil-haqi wahum yaʿlamuna
wala-in sa-altahum man khalaqahum layaqulunna l-lahu fa-anna yu'fakuna
waqilihi yarabbi inna haulai qawmun la yu'minuna
fa-is'fah ʿanhum waqul salamun fasawfa yaʿlamuna
hha-meem
wal-kitabi l-mubini
inna anzalnahu fi laylatin mubarakatin inna kunna mundhirina
fiha yuf'raqu kullu amrin hakimin
amran min ʿindina inna kunna mur'silina
rahmatan min rabbika innahu huwa l-samiʿu l-ʿalimu
rabbi l-samawati wal-ardi wama baynahuma in kuntum muqinina
la ilaha illa huwa yuh'yi wayumitu rabbukum warabbu abaikumu l-awalina
bal hum fi shakkin yalʿabuna
fa-ir'taqib yawma tati l-samau bidukhanin mubinin
yaghsha l-nasa hadha ʿadhabun alimun
rabbana ik'shif ʿanna l-ʿadhaba inna mu'minuna
anna lahumu l-dhik'ra waqad jaahum rasulun mubinun
thumma tawallaw ʿanhu waqalu muʿallamun majnunun
inna kashifu l-ʿadhabi qalilan innakum ʿaiduna
yawma nabtishu l-batshata l-kub'ra inna muntaqimuna
walaqad fatanna qablahum qawma fir'ʿawna wajaahum rasulun karimun
an addu ilayya ʿibada l-lahi inni lakum rasulun aminun
wa-an la taʿlu ʿala l-lahi inni atikum bisul'tanin mubinin
wa-inni ʿudh'tu birabbi warabbikum an tarjumuni
wa-in lam tu'minu li fa-iʿ'taziluni
fadaʿa rabbahu anna haulai qawmun muj'rimuna
fa-asri biʿibadi laylan innakum muttabaʿuna
wa-ut'ruki l-bahra rahwan innahum jundun mugh'raquna
kam taraku min jannatin waʿuyunin
wazuruʿin wamaqamin karimin
wanaʿmatin kanu fiha fakihina
kadhalika wa-awrathnaha qawman akharina
fama bakat ʿalayhimu l-samau wal-ardu wama kanu munzarina
walaqad najjayna bani is'raila mina l-ʿadhabi l-muhini
min fir'ʿawna innahu kana ʿaliyan mina l-mus'rifina
walaqadi ikh'tarnahum ʿala ʿil'min ʿala l-ʿalamina
waataynahum mina l-ayati ma fihi balaon mubinun
inna haulai layaquluna
in hiya illa mawtatuna l-ula wama nahnu bimunsharina
fatu biabaina in kuntum sadiqina
ahum khayrun am qawmu tubbaʿin wa-alladhina min qablihim ahlaknahum innahum kanu muj'rimina
wama khalaqna l-samawati wal-arda wama baynahuma laʿibina
ma khalaqnahuma illa bil-haqi walakinna aktharahum la yaʿlamuna
inna yawma l-fasli miqatuhum ajmaʿina
yawma la yugh'ni mawlan ʿan mawlan shayan wala hum yunsaruna
illa man rahima l-lahu innahu huwa l-ʿazizu l-rahimu
inna shajarata l-zaqumi
taʿamu l-athimi
kal-muh'li yaghli fi l-butuni
kaghalyi l-hamimi
khudhuhu fa-iʿ'tiluhu ila sawai l-jahimi
thumma subbu fawqa rasihi min ʿadhabi l-hamimi
dhuq innaka anta l-ʿazizu l-karimu
inna hadha ma kuntum bihi tamtaruna
inna l-mutaqina fi maqamin aminin
fi jannatin waʿuyunin
yalbasuna min sundusin wa-is'tabraqin mutaqabilina
kadhalika wazawwajnahum bihurin ʿinin
yadʿuna fiha bikulli fakihatin aminina
la yadhuquna fiha l-mawta illa l-mawtata l-ula wawaqahum ʿadhaba l-jahimi
fadlan min rabbika dhalika huwa l-fawzu l-ʿazimu
fa-innama yassarnahu bilisanika laʿallahum yatadhakkaruna
fa-ir'taqib innahum mur'taqibuna
hha-meem
tanzilu l-kitabi mina l-lahi l-ʿazizi l-hakimi
inna fi l-samawati wal-ardi laayatin lil'mu'minina
wafi khalqikum wama yabuthu min dabbatin ayatun liqawmin yuqinuna
wa-ikh'tilafi al-layli wal-nahari wama anzala l-lahu mina l-samai min riz'qin fa-ahya bihi l-arda baʿda mawtiha watasrifi l-riyahi ayatun liqawmin yaʿqiluna
til'ka ayatu l-lahi natluha ʿalayka bil-haqi fabi-ayyi hadithin baʿda l-lahi waayatihi yu'minuna
waylun likulli affakin athimin
yasmaʿu ayati l-lahi tut'la ʿalayhi thumma yusirru mus'takbiran ka-an lam yasmaʿha fabashir'hu biʿadhabin alimin
wa-idha ʿalima min ayatina shayan ittakhadhaha huzuwan ulaika lahum ʿadhabun muhinun
min waraihim jahannamu wala yugh'ni ʿanhum ma kasabu shayan wala ma ittakhadhu min duni l-lahi awliyaa walahum ʿadhabun ʿazimun
hadha hudan wa-alladhina kafaru biayati rabbihim lahum ʿadhabun min rij'zin alimun
al-lahu alladhi sakhara lakumu l-bahra litajriya l-ful'ku fihi bi-amrihi walitabtaghu min fadlihi walaʿallakum tashkuruna
wasakhara lakum ma fi l-samawati wama fi l-ardi jamiʿan min'hu inna fi dhalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaruna
qul lilladhina amanu yaghfiru lilladhina la yarjuna ayyama l-lahi liyajziya qawman bima kanu yaksibuna
man ʿamila salihan falinafsihi waman asaa faʿalayha thumma ila rabbikum tur'jaʿuna
walaqad atayna bani is'raila l-kitaba wal-huk'ma wal-nubuwata warazaqnahum mina l-tayibati wafaddalnahum ʿala l-ʿalamina
waataynahum bayyinatin mina l-amri fama ikh'talafu illa min baʿdi ma jaahumu l-ʿil'mu baghyan baynahum inna rabbaka yaqdi baynahum yawma l-qiyamati fima kanu fihi yakhtalifuna
thumma jaʿalnaka ʿala shariʿatin mina l-amri fa-ittabiʿ'ha wala tattabiʿ ahwaa alladhina la yaʿlamuna
innahum lan yugh'nu ʿanka mina l-lahi shayan wa-inna l-zalimina baʿduhum awliyau baʿdin wal-lahu waliyyu l-mutaqina
hadha basairu lilnnasi wahudan warahmatun liqawmin yuqinuna
am hasiba alladhina ij'tarahu l-sayiati an najʿalahum ka-alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati sawaan mahyahum wamamatuhum saa ma yahkumuna
wakhalaqa l-lahu l-samawati wal-arda bil-haqi walituj'za kullu nafsin bima kasabat wahum la yuz'lamuna
afara-ayta mani ittakhadha ilahahu hawahu wa-adallahu l-lahu ʿala ʿil'min wakhatama ʿala samʿihi waqalbihi wajaʿala ʿala basarihi ghishawatan faman yahdihi min baʿdi l-lahi afala tadhakkaruna
waqalu ma hiya illa hayatuna l-dun'ya namutu wanahya wama yuh'likuna illa l-dahru wama lahum bidhalika min ʿil'min in hum illa yazunnuna
wa-idha tut'la ʿalayhim ayatuna bayyinatin ma kana hujjatahum illa an qalu i'tu biabaina in kuntum sadiqina
quli l-lahu yuh'yikum thumma yumitukum thumma yajmaʿukum ila yawmi l-qiyamati la rayba fihi walakinna akthara l-nasi la yaʿlamuna
walillahi mul'ku l-samawati wal-ardi wayawma taqumu l-saʿatu yawma-idhin yakhsaru l-mub'tiluna
watara kulla ummatin jathiyatan kullu ummatin tud'ʿa ila kitabiha l-yawma tuj'zawna ma kuntum taʿmaluna
hadha kitabuna yantiqu ʿalaykum bil-haqi inna kunna nastansikhu ma kuntum taʿmaluna
fa-amma alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati fayud'khiluhum rabbuhum fi rahmatihi dhalika huwa l-fawzu l-mubinu
wa-amma alladhina kafaru afalam takun ayati tut'la ʿalaykum fa-is'takbartum wakuntum qawman muj'rimina
wa-idha qila inna waʿda l-lahi haqqun wal-saʿatu la rayba fiha qul'tum ma nadri ma l-saʿatu in nazunnu illa zannan wama nahnu bimus'tayqinina
wabada lahum sayyiatu ma ʿamilu wahaqa bihim ma kanu bihi yastahziuna
waqila l-yawma nansakum kama nasitum liqaa yawmikum hadha wamawakumu l-naru wama lakum min nasirina
dhalikum bi-annakumu ittakhadhtum ayati l-lahi huzuwan wagharratkumu l-hayatu l-dun'ya fal-yawma la yukh'rajuna min'ha wala hum yus'taʿtabuna
falillahi l-hamdu rabbi l-samawati warabbi l-ardi rabbi l-ʿalamina
walahu l-kib'riyau fi l-samawati wal-ardi wahuwa l-ʿazizu l-hakimu
hha-meem
tanzilu l-kitabi mina l-lahi l-ʿazizi l-hakimi
ma khalaqna l-samawati wal-arda wama baynahuma illa bil-haqi wa-ajalin musamman wa-alladhina kafaru ʿamma undhiru muʿ'riduna
qul ara-aytum ma tadʿuna min duni l-lahi aruni madha khalaqu mina l-ardi am lahum shir'kun fi l-samawati i'tuni bikitabin min qabli hadha aw atharatin min ʿil'min in kuntum sadiqina
waman adallu mimman yadʿu min duni l-lahi man la yastajibu lahu ila yawmi l-qiyamati wahum ʿan duʿaihim ghafiluna
wa-idha hushira l-nasu kanu lahum aʿdaan wakanu biʿibadatihim kafirina
wa-idha tut'la ʿalayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qala alladhina kafaru lil'haqqi lamma jaahum hadha sih'run mubinun
am yaquluna if'tarahu qul ini if'taraytuhu fala tamlikuna li mina l-lahi shayan huwa aʿlamu bima tufiduna fihi kafa bihi shahidan bayni wabaynakum wahuwa l-ghafuru l-rahimu
qul ma kuntu bid'ʿan mina l-rusuli wama adri ma yuf'ʿalu bi wala bikum in attabiʿu illa ma yuha ilayya wama ana illa nadhirun mubinun
qul ara-aytum in kana min ʿindi l-lahi wakafartum bihi washahida shahidun min bani is'raila ʿala mith'lihi faamana wa-is'takbartum inna l-laha la yahdi l-qawma l-zalimina
waqala alladhina kafaru lilladhina amanu law kana khayran ma sabaquna ilayhi wa-idh lam yahtadu bihi fasayaquluna hadha if'kun qadimun
wamin qablihi kitabu musa imaman warahmatan wahadha kitabun musaddiqun lisanan ʿarabiyyan liyundhira alladhina zalamu wabush'ra lil'muh'sinina
inna alladhina qalu rabbuna l-lahu thumma is'taqamu fala khawfun ʿalayhim wala hum yahzanuna
ulaika ashabu l-janati khalidina fiha jazaan bima kanu yaʿmaluna
wawassayna l-insana biwalidayhi ih'sanan hamalathu ummuhu kur'han wawadaʿathu kur'han wahamluhu wafisaluhu thalathuna shahran hatta idha balagha ashuddahu wabalagha arbaʿina sanatan qala rabbi awziʿ'ni an ashkura niʿ'mataka allati anʿamta ʿalayya waʿala walidayya wa-an aʿmala salihan tardahu wa-aslih li fi dhurriyyati inni tub'tu ilayka wa-inni mina l-mus'limina
ulaika alladhina nataqabbalu ʿanhum ahsana ma ʿamilu wanatajawazu ʿan sayyiatihim fi ashabi l-janati waʿda l-sid'qi alladhi kanu yuʿaduna
wa-alladhi qala liwalidayhi uffin lakuma ataʿidanini an ukh'raja waqad khalati l-qurunu min qabli wahuma yastaghithani l-laha waylaka amin inna waʿda l-lahi haqqun fayaqulu ma hadha illa asatiru l-awalina
ulaika alladhina haqqa ʿalayhimu l-qawlu fi umamin qad khalat min qablihim mina l-jini wal-insi innahum kanu khasirina
walikullin darajatun mimma ʿamilu waliyuwaffiyahum aʿmalahum wahum la yuz'lamuna
wayawma yuʿ'radu alladhina kafaru ʿala l-nari adhhabtum tayyibatikum fi hayatikumu l-dun'ya wa-is'tamtaʿtum biha fal-yawma tuj'zawna ʿadhaba l-huni bima kuntum tastakbiruna fi l-ardi bighayri l-haqi wabima kuntum tafsuquna
wa-udh'kur akha ʿadin idh andhara qawmahu bil-ahqafi waqad khalati l-nudhuru min bayni yadayhi wamin khalfihi alla taʿbudu illa l-laha inni akhafu ʿalaykum ʿadhaba yawmin ʿazimin
qalu aji'tana litafikana ʿan alihatina fatina bima taʿiduna in kunta mina l-sadiqina
qala innama l-ʿil'mu ʿinda l-lahi wa-uballighukum ma ur'sil'tu bihi walakinni arakum qawman tajhaluna
falamma ra-awhu ʿaridan mus'taqbila awdiyatihim qalu hadha ʿaridun mum'tiruna bal huwa ma is'taʿjaltum bihi rihun fiha ʿadhabun alimun
tudammiru kulla shayin bi-amri rabbiha fa-asbahu la yura illa masakinuhum kadhalika najzi l-qawma l-muj'rimina
walaqad makkannahum fima in makkannakum fihi wajaʿalna lahum samʿan wa-absaran wa-afidatan fama aghna ʿanhum samʿuhum wala absaruhum wala afidatuhum min shayin idh kanu yajhaduna biayati l-lahi wahaqa bihim ma kanu bihi yastahziuna
walaqad ahlakna ma hawlakum mina l-qura wasarrafna l-ayati laʿallahum yarjiʿuna
falawla nasarahumu alladhina ittakhadhu min duni l-lahi qur'banan alihatan bal dallu ʿanhum wadhalika if'kuhum wama kanu yaftaruna
wa-idh sarafna ilayka nafaran mina l-jini yastamiʿuna l-qur'ana falamma hadaruhu qalu ansitu falamma qudiya wallaw ila qawmihim mundhirina
qalu yaqawmana inna samiʿ'na kitaban unzila min baʿdi musa musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi yahdi ila l-haqi wa-ila tariqin mus'taqimin
yaqawmana ajibu daʿiya l-lahi waaminu bihi yaghfir lakum min dhunubikum wayujir'kum min ʿadhabin alimin
waman la yujib daʿiya l-lahi falaysa bimuʿ'jizin fi l-ardi walaysa lahu min dunihi awliyau ulaika fi dalalin mubinin
awalam yaraw anna l-laha alladhi khalaqa l-samawati wal-arda walam yaʿya bikhalqihinna biqadirin ʿala an yuh'yiya l-mawta bala innahu ʿala kulli shayin qadirun
wayawma yuʿ'radu alladhina kafaru ʿala l-nari alaysa hadha bil-haqi qalu bala warabbina qala fadhuqu l-ʿadhaba bima kuntum takfuruna
fa-is'bir kama sabara ulu l-ʿazmi mina l-rusuli wala tastaʿjil lahum ka-annahum yawma yarawna ma yuʿaduna lam yalbathu illa saʿatan min naharin balaghun fahal yuh'laku illa l-qawmu l-fasiquna
alladhina kafaru wasaddu ʿan sabili l-lahi adalla aʿmalahum
wa-alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati waamanu bima nuzzila ʿala muhammadin wahuwa l-haqu min rabbihim kaffara ʿanhum sayyiatihim wa-aslaha balahum
dhalika bi-anna alladhina kafaru ittabaʿu l-batila wa-anna alladhina amanu ittabaʿu l-haqa min rabbihim kadhalika yadribu l-lahu lilnnasi amthalahum
fa-idha laqitumu alladhina kafaru fadarba l-riqabi hatta idha athkhantumuhum fashuddu l-wathaqa fa-imma mannan baʿdu wa-imma fidaan hatta tadaʿa l-harbu awzaraha dhalika walaw yashau l-lahu la-intasara min'hum walakin liyabluwa baʿdakum bibaʿdin wa-alladhina qutilu fi sabili l-lahi falan yudilla aʿmalahum
sayahdihim wayus'lihu balahum
wayud'khiluhumu l-janata ʿarrafaha lahum
yaayyuha alladhina amanu in tansuru l-laha yansur'kum wayuthabbit aqdamakum
wa-alladhina kafaru fataʿsan lahum wa-adalla aʿmalahum
dhalika bi-annahum karihu ma anzala l-lahu fa-ahbata aʿmalahum
afalam yasiru fi l-ardi fayanzuru kayfa kana ʿaqibatu alladhina min qablihim dammara l-lahu ʿalayhim walil'kafirina amthaluha
dhalika bi-anna l-laha mawla alladhina amanu wa-anna l-kafirina la mawla lahum
inna l-laha yud'khilu alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati jannatin tajri min tahtiha l-anharu wa-alladhina kafaru yatamattaʿuna wayakuluna kama takulu l-anʿamu wal-naru mathwan lahum
waka-ayyin min qaryatin hiya ashaddu quwwatan min qaryatika allati akhrajatka ahlaknahum fala nasira lahum
afaman kana ʿala bayyinatin min rabbihi kaman zuyyina lahu suu ʿamalihi wa-ittabaʿu ahwaahum
mathalu l-janati allati wuʿida l-mutaquna fiha anharun min main ghayri asinin wa-anharun min labanin lam yataghayyar taʿmuhu wa-anharun min khamrin ladhatin lilsharibina wa-anharun min ʿasalin musaffan walahum fiha min kulli l-thamarati wamaghfiratun min rabbihim kaman huwa khalidun fi l-nari wasuqu maan hamiman faqattaʿa amʿaahum
wamin'hum man yastamiʿu ilayka hatta idha kharaju min ʿindika qalu lilladhina utu l-ʿil'ma madha qala anifan ulaika alladhina tabaʿa l-lahu ʿala qulubihim wa-ittabaʿu ahwaahum
wa-alladhina ih'tadaw zadahum hudan waatahum taqwahum
fahal yanzuruna illa l-saʿata an tatiyahum baghtatan faqad jaa ashratuha fa-anna lahum idha jaathum dhik'rahum
fa-iʿ'lam annahu la ilaha illa l-lahu wa-is'taghfir lidhanbika walil'mu'minina wal-mu'minati wal-lahu yaʿlamu mutaqallabakum wamathwakum
wayaqulu alladhina amanu lawla nuzzilat suratun fa-idha unzilat suratun muh'kamatun wadhukira fiha l-qitalu ra-ayta alladhina fi qulubihim maradun yanzuruna ilayka nazara l-maghshiyi ʿalayhi mina l-mawti fa-awla lahum
taʿatun waqawlun maʿrufun fa-idha ʿazama l-amru falaw sadaqu l-laha lakana khayran lahum
fahal ʿasaytum in tawallaytum an tuf'sidu fi l-ardi watuqattiʿu arhamakum
ulaika alladhina laʿanahumu l-lahu fa-asammahum wa-aʿma absarahum
afala yatadabbaruna l-qur'ana am ʿala qulubin aqfaluha
inna alladhina ir'taddu ʿala adbarihim min baʿdi ma tabayyana lahumu l-huda l-shaytanu sawwala lahum wa-amla lahum
dhalika bi-annahum qalu lilladhina karihu ma nazzala l-lahu sanutiʿukum fi baʿdi l-amri wal-lahu yaʿlamu is'rarahum
fakayfa idha tawaffathumu l-malaikatu yadribuna wujuhahum wa-adbarahum
dhalika bi-annahumu ittabaʿu ma askhata l-laha wakarihu rid'wanahu fa-ahbata aʿmalahum
am hasiba alladhina fi qulubihim maradun an lan yukh'rija l-lahu adghanahum
walaw nashau la-araynakahum falaʿaraftahum bisimahum walataʿrifannahum fi lahni l-qawli wal-lahu yaʿlamu aʿmalakum
walanabluwannakum hatta naʿlama l-mujahidina minkum wal-sabirina wanabluwa akhbarakum
inna alladhina kafaru wasaddu ʿan sabili l-lahi washaqqu l-rasula min baʿdi ma tabayyana lahumu l-huda lan yadurru l-laha shayan wasayuh'bitu aʿmalahum
yaayyuha alladhina amanu atiʿu l-laha wa-atiʿu l-rasula wala tub'tilu aʿmalakum
inna alladhina kafaru wasaddu ʿan sabili l-lahi thumma matu wahum kuffarun falan yaghfira l-lahu lahum
fala tahinu watadʿu ila l-salmi wa-antumu l-aʿlawna wal-lahu maʿakum walan yatirakum aʿmalakum
innama l-hayatu l-dun'ya laʿibun walahwun wa-in tu'minu watattaqu yu'tikum ujurakum wala yasalkum amwalakum
in yasalkumuha fayuh'fikum tabkhalu wayukh'rij adghanakum
haantum haulai tud'ʿawna litunfiqu fi sabili l-lahi faminkum man yabkhalu waman yabkhal fa-innama yabkhalu ʿan nafsihi wal-lahu l-ghaniyu wa-antumu l-fuqarau wa-in tatawallaw yastabdil qawman ghayrakum thumma la yakunu amthalakum
inna fatahna laka fathan mubinan
liyaghfira laka l-lahu ma taqaddama min dhanbika wama ta-akhara wayutimma niʿ'matahu ʿalayka wayahdiyaka siratan mus'taqiman
wayansuraka l-lahu nasran ʿazizan
huwa alladhi anzala l-sakinata fi qulubi l-mu'minina liyazdadu imanan maʿa imanihim walillahi junudu l-samawati wal-ardi wakana l-lahu ʿaliman hakiman
liyud'khila l-mu'minina wal-mu'minati jannatin tajri min tahtiha l-anharu khalidina fiha wayukaffira ʿanhum sayyiatihim wakana dhalika ʿinda l-lahi fawzan ʿaziman
wayuʿadhiba l-munafiqina wal-munafiqati wal-mush'rikina wal-mush'rikati l-zanina bil-lahi zanna l-sawi ʿalayhim dairatu l-sawi waghadiba l-lahu ʿalayhim walaʿanahum wa-aʿadda lahum jahannama wasaat masiran
walillahi junudu l-samawati wal-ardi wakana l-lahu ʿazizan hakiman
inna arsalnaka shahidan wamubashiran wanadhiran
litu'minu bil-lahi warasulihi watuʿazziruhu watuwaqqiruhu watusabbihuhu buk'ratan wa-asilan
inna alladhina yubayiʿunaka innama yubayiʿuna l-laha yadu l-lahi fawqa aydihim faman nakatha fa-innama yankuthu ʿala nafsihi waman awfa bima ʿahada ʿalayhu l-laha fasayu'tihi ajran ʿaziman
sayaqulu laka l-mukhalafuna mina l-aʿrabi shaghalatna amwaluna wa-ahluna fa-is'taghfir lana yaquluna bi-alsinatihim ma laysa fi qulubihim qul faman yamliku lakum mina l-lahi shayan in arada bikum darran aw arada bikum nafʿan bal kana l-lahu bima taʿmaluna khabiran
bal zanantum an lan yanqaliba l-rasulu wal-mu'minuna ila ahlihim abadan wazuyyina dhalika fi qulubikum wazanantum zanna l-sawi wakuntum qawman buran
waman lam yu'min bil-lahi warasulihi fa-inna aʿtadna lil'kafirina saʿiran
walillahi mul'ku l-samawati wal-ardi yaghfiru liman yashau wayuʿadhibu man yashau wakana l-lahu ghafuran rahiman
sayaqulu l-mukhalafuna idha intalaqtum ila maghanima litakhudhuha dharuna nattabiʿ'kum yuriduna an yubaddilu kalama l-lahi qul lan tattabiʿuna kadhalikum qala l-lahu min qablu fasayaquluna bal tahsudunana bal kanu la yafqahuna illa qalilan
qul lil'mukhallafina mina l-aʿrabi satud'ʿawna ila qawmin uli basin shadidin tuqatilunahum aw yus'limuna fa-in tutiʿu yu'tikumu l-lahu ajran hasanan wa-in tatawallaw kama tawallaytum min qablu yuʿadhib'kum ʿadhaban aliman
laysa ʿala l-aʿma harajun wala ʿala l-aʿraji harajun wala ʿala l-maridi harajun waman yutiʿi l-laha warasulahu yud'khil'hu jannatin tajri min tahtiha l-anharu waman yatawalla yuʿadhib'hu ʿadhaban aliman
laqad radiya l-lahu ʿani l-mu'minina idh yubayiʿunaka tahta l-shajarati faʿalima ma fi qulubihim fa-anzala l-sakinata ʿalayhim wa-athabahum fathan qariban
wamaghanima kathiratan yakhudhunaha wakana l-lahu ʿazizan hakiman
waʿadakumu l-lahu maghanima kathiratan takhudhunaha faʿajjala lakum hadhihi wakaffa aydiya l-nasi ʿankum walitakuna ayatan lil'mu'minina wayahdiyakum siratan mus'taqiman
wa-ukh'ra lam taqdiru ʿalayha qad ahata l-lahu biha wakana l-lahu ʿala kulli shayin qadiran
walaw qatalakumu alladhina kafaru lawallawu l-adbara thumma la yajiduna waliyyan wala nasiran
sunnata l-lahi allati qad khalat min qablu walan tajida lisunnati l-lahi tabdilan
wahuwa alladhi kaffa aydiyahum ʿankum wa-aydiyakum ʿanhum bibatni makkata min baʿdi an azfarakum ʿalayhim wakana l-lahu bima taʿmaluna basiran
humu alladhina kafaru wasaddukum ʿani l-masjidi l-harami wal-hadya maʿkufan an yablugha mahillahu walawla rijalun mu'minuna wanisaon mu'minatun lam taʿlamuhum an tatauhum fatusibakum min'hum maʿarratun bighayri ʿil'min liyud'khila l-lahu fi rahmatihi man yashau law tazayyalu laʿadhabna alladhina kafaru min'hum ʿadhaban aliman
idh jaʿala alladhina kafaru fi qulubihimu l-hamiyata hamiyyata l-jahiliyati fa-anzala l-lahu sakinatahu ʿala rasulihi waʿala l-mu'minina wa-alzamahum kalimata l-taqwa wakanu ahaqqa biha wa-ahlaha wakana l-lahu bikulli shayin ʿaliman
laqad sadaqa l-lahu rasulahu l-ru'ya bil-haqi latadkhulunna l-masjida l-harama in shaa l-lahu aminina muhalliqina ruusakum wamuqassirina la takhafuna faʿalima ma lam taʿlamu fajaʿala min duni dhalika fathan qariban
huwa alladhi arsala rasulahu bil-huda wadini l-haqi liyuz'hirahu ʿala l-dini kullihi wakafa bil-lahi shahidan
muhammadun rasulu l-lahi wa-alladhina maʿahu ashiddau ʿala l-kufari ruhamau baynahum tarahum rukkaʿan sujjadan yabtaghuna fadlan mina l-lahi warid'wanan simahum fi wujuhihim min athari l-sujudi dhalika mathaluhum fi l-tawrati wamathaluhum fi l-injili kazarʿin akhraja shatahu faazarahu fa-is'taghlaza fa-is'tawa ʿala suqihi yuʿ'jibu l-zuraʿa liyaghiza bihimu l-kufara waʿada l-lahu alladhina amanu waʿamilu l-salihati min'hum maghfiratan wa-ajran ʿaziman
yaayyuha alladhina amanu la tuqaddimu bayna yadayi l-lahi warasulihi wa-ittaqu l-laha inna l-laha samiʿun ʿalimun
yaayyuha alladhina amanu la tarfaʿu aswatakum fawqa sawti l-nabiyi wala tajharu lahu bil-qawli kajahri baʿdikum libaʿdin an tahbata aʿmalukum wa-antum la tashʿuruna
inna alladhina yaghudduna aswatahum ʿinda rasuli l-lahi ulaika alladhina im'tahana l-lahu qulubahum lilttaqwa lahum maghfiratun wa-ajrun ʿazimun
inna alladhina yunadunaka min warai l-hujurati aktharuhum la yaʿqiluna
walaw annahum sabaru hatta takhruja ilayhim lakana khayran lahum wal-lahu ghafurun rahimun
yaayyuha alladhina amanu in jaakum fasiqun binaba-in fatabayyanu an tusibu qawman bijahalatin fatus'bihu ʿala ma faʿaltum nadimina
wa-iʿ'lamu anna fikum rasula l-lahi law yutiʿukum fi kathirin mina l-amri laʿanittum walakinna l-laha habbaba ilaykumu l-imana wazayyanahu fi qulubikum wakarraha ilaykumu l-kuf'ra wal-fusuqa wal-ʿis'yana ulaika humu l-rashiduna
fadlan mina l-lahi waniʿ'matan wal-lahu ʿalimun hakimun
wa-in taifatani mina l-mu'minina iq'tatalu fa-aslihu baynahuma fa-in baghat ih'dahuma ʿala l-ukh'ra faqatilu allati tabghi hatta tafia ila amri l-lahi fa-in faat fa-aslihu baynahuma bil-ʿadli wa-aqsitu inna l-laha yuhibbu l-muq'sitina
innama l-mu'minuna ikh'watun fa-aslihu bayna akhawaykum wa-ittaqu l-laha laʿallakum tur'hamuna
yaayyuha alladhina amanu la yaskhar qawmun min qawmin ʿasa an yakunu khayran min'hum wala nisaon min nisain ʿasa an yakunna khayran min'hunna wala talmizu anfusakum wala tanabazu bil-alqabi bi'sa l-s'mu l-fusuqu baʿda l-imani waman lam yatub fa-ulaika humu l-zalimuna
yaayyuha alladhina amanu ij'tanibu kathiran mina l-zani inna baʿda l-zani ith'mun wala tajassasu wala yaghtab baʿdukum baʿdan ayuhibbu ahadukum an yakula lahma akhihi maytan fakarih'tumuhu wa-ittaqu l-laha inna l-laha tawwabun rahimun
yaayyuha l-nasu inna khalaqnakum min dhakarin wa-untha wajaʿalnakum shuʿuban waqabaila litaʿarafu inna akramakum ʿinda l-lahi atqakum inna l-laha ʿalimun khabirun
qalati l-aʿrabu amanna qul lam tu'minu walakin qulu aslamna walamma yadkhuli l-imanu fi qulubikum wa-in tutiʿu l-laha warasulahu la yalit'kum min aʿmalikum shayan inna l-laha ghafurun rahimun
innama l-mu'minuna alladhina amanu bil-lahi warasulihi thumma lam yartabu wajahadu bi-amwalihim wa-anfusihim fi sabili l-lahi ulaika humu l-sadiquna
qul atuʿallimuna l-laha bidinikum wal-lahu yaʿlamu ma fi l-samawati wama fi l-ardi wal-lahu bikulli shayin ʿalimun
yamunnuna ʿalayka an aslamu qul la tamunnu ʿalayya is'lamakum bali l-lahu yamunnu ʿalaykum an hadakum lil'imani in kuntum sadiqina
inna l-laha yaʿlamu ghayba l-samawati wal-ardi wal-lahu basirun bima taʿmaluna
qaf wal-qur'ani l-majidi
bal ʿajibu an jaahum mundhirun min'hum faqala l-kafiruna hadha shayon ʿajibun
a-idha mit'na wakunna turaban dhalika rajʿun baʿidun
qad ʿalim'na ma tanqusu l-ardu min'hum waʿindana kitabun hafizun
bal kadhabu bil-haqi lamma jaahum fahum fi amrin marijin
afalam yanzuru ila l-samai fawqahum kayfa banaynaha wazayyannaha wama laha min furujin
wal-arda madadnaha wa-alqayna fiha rawasiya wa-anbatna fiha min kulli zawjin bahijin
tabsiratan wadhik'ra likulli ʿabdin munibin
wanazzalna mina l-samai maan mubarakan fa-anbatna bihi jannatin wahabba l-hasidi
wal-nakhla basiqatin laha talʿun nadidun
riz'qan lil'ʿibadi wa-ahyayna bihi baldatan maytan kadhalika l-khuruju

waʿadun wafir'ʿawnu wa-ikh'wanu lutin
wa-ashabu l-aykati waqawmu tubbaʿin kullun kadhaba l-rusula fahaqqa waʿidi
afaʿayina bil-khalqi l-awali bal hum fi labsin min khalqin jadidin
walaqad khalaqna l-insana wanaʿlamu ma tuwaswisu bihi nafsuhu wanahnu aqrabu ilayhi min habli l-waridi
idh yatalaqqa l-mutalaqiyani ʿani l-yamini waʿani l-shimali qaʿidun
ma yalfizu min qawlin illa ladayhi raqibun ʿatidun
wajaat sakratu l-mawti bil-haqi dhalika ma kunta min'hu tahidu
wanufikha fi l-suri dhalika yawmu l-waʿidi
wajaat kullu nafsin maʿaha saiqun washahidun
laqad kunta fi ghaflatin min hadha fakashafna ʿanka ghitaaka fabasaruka l-yawma hadidun
waqala qarinuhu hadha ma ladayya ʿatidun
alqiya fi jahannama kulla kaffarin ʿanidin
mannaʿin lil'khayri muʿ'tadin muribin

qala qarinuhu rabbana ma atghaytuhu walakin kana fi dalalin baʿidin
qala la takhtasimu ladayya waqad qaddamtu ilaykum bil-waʿidi
